'''泰勒·艾莉森·斯威夫特'''（{{lang-en|Taylor Alison Swift}}，{{bd|1989年|12月13日|catIdx=S}}），是一名美國天后級[[創作歌手|創作歌手]]、[[音樂製作人|唱片製作人]]、[[慈善家|慈善家]]及[[演員|演員]]。作为当今全世界最有影响力的歌手之一，她以创作叙述个人生活的歌曲及不使用修音而闻名，并以此受到了众多好评。

泰勒絲出生并成长于[[宾夕法尼亚州|宾夕法尼亚州]]，14岁时举家搬到了音乐之乡[[田纳西州|田纳西州]][[纳什维尔|纳許维爾]]，由此投身于[[乡村音乐|乡村音乐]]事业，她与[[大機器唱片|大机器唱片]]签约，并成为了[[索尼/聯合電視音樂出版|索尼/聯合電視音樂出版]]签约的最年轻的艺人。泰勒絲2006年发行的[[泰勒·斯威夫特_(專輯)|个人首张同名专辑]]在[[公告牌二百强专辑榜|《公告牌》二百强专辑榜]]上获得了最高第五名的成绩，并成为了2000年代在该榜单上停留时间最长的专辑，专辑第三支单曲《[[我們的歌_(泰勒絲歌曲)|我們的歌]]》在[[公告牌热门乡村歌曲榜|热门乡村歌曲榜]]上夺得了冠军，使泰勒絲成为了登上该榜单的最年轻个人。泰勒絲的第二张专辑《[[放手去爱_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|放手去爱]]》发行于2008年，乡村与流行混合风格的歌曲《[[爱情故事_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|爱情故事]]》和《[[与我同在_(歌曲)|与我同在]]》大获成功，使得《放手去爱》成为了2009年美国最畅销的专辑之一，该张专辑赢得了四项[[葛萊美獎|格莱美奖]]，并使泰勒絲成为“{{Le|格莱美奖年度专辑|Grammy Award for Album of the Year|年度专辑}}”奖项最年轻得主。

2010年，泰勒絲发行了由自己独自创作的第三张专辑《[[爱的告白|爱的告白]]》，专辑空降美国专辑榜第一位，其中的单曲《[[卑鄙_(歌曲)|卑鄙]]》获得了两项格莱美奖。2012年，泰勒絲发行了第四张专辑《[[红_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|红]]》，单曲《[[我们再也回不去了|我们再也回不去了]]》和《[[我知道你是大麻煩|我知道你是大麻烦]]》在全球大获成功。2014年，泰勒絲发行了专注于流行风格的第五张专辑《[[1989_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|1989]]》，专辑获得了三项格莱美奖，使她成为了获得两次“年度专辑”奖项的第一位女性，同时也是第五位取得该成就的艺人，专辑中的单曲《[[通通甩掉|通通甩掉]]》、《[[空格_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|空格]]》和《[[壞到底_(歌曲)|壞到底]]》在美国、澳大利亚和加拿大均夺得榜首。2017年，泰勒絲发行了第六张专辑《[[名誉_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|名誉]]》，專輯類型為流行樂、電子流行及合成器流行，专辑和首支单曲《[[瞧你们让我做了什么|瞧你们让我做了什么]]》均在美国和英国的专辑和单曲榜上夺冠；该专辑与之前发行的几张专辑使得泰勒絲成为了美国第一位拥有四张{{Le|最快售出专辑列表|Lists of fastest-selling albums|在发行首周内卖出超过一百万张专辑}}的艺人。

泰勒絲是史上[[畅销音乐艺人列表|最畅销的音乐艺人]]之一，她的专辑销量超过五千万张——其中在美国售出了2,780万张，她的单曲下载量达到了1.5亿次。作为一位词曲作家，泰勒絲获得了{{Le|泰勒·斯威夫特奖项与提名列表|List of awards and nominations received by Taylor Swift|众多奖项}}，其中包括{{Le|纳什维尔词曲作家协会|Nashville Songwriters Association}}和{{Le|词曲作家名人堂|Songwriters Hall of Fame}}的嘉奖以及入选2015年《[[滚石_(杂志)|滚石]]》评选的{{Le|滚石史上最伟大的百大词曲作家|Rolling Stone's 100 Greatest Songwriters of All Time|史上最伟大的百大词曲作家}}，此外，她共获得了10项[[葛萊美獎|格莱美奖]]、23项[[公告牌音乐奖|《公告牌》音乐奖]]、23项[[全美音樂獎|全美音樂獎]]、12项[[乡村音乐协会奖|乡村音乐协会奖]]、8項鄉村音樂學院獎、69項BMI大獎、6项[[吉尼斯世界纪录|吉尼斯世界纪录]]、1項[[艾美奖|艾美獎]]...等大獎。泰勒絲曾于2010年、2015年及2019年三次入选《[[时代杂志|时代]]》的[[时代百大人物|百大人物]]，她也在2014年、2017年及2019年登上《時代》雜誌的封面人物，是首位女性登上《時代》雜誌封面三次。泰勒絲也入选《[[福布斯|福布斯]]》音乐界收入最高的女性（2011年–2015年）、[[世界百名权威女性|百名权威女性]]（2015年）和[[世界百大名人权力榜|百大名人权力榜]]（2016年）榜单，她在百大名人权力榜上排名第一位，并成为了榜单上最年轻的女性，2018年在《[[告示牌_(雜誌)|吿示牌]]》獲得最佳女歌手...等獎項。

== 早年生活 ==
1989年12月13日，泰勒絲在[[宾夕法尼亚州|宾夕法尼亚州]][[雷丁_(宾夕法尼亚州)|雷丁]]出生<ref name="Rolling Stone bio">{{cite web | url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/artists/taylor-swift/biography | title=Taylor Swift | work=Rolling Stone | accessdate=2015-04-09 | first=Chuck | last=Eddy | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120709093054/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/artists/taylor-swift/biography | archivedate=2012-07-09 }}</ref><ref name=biographydotcom>{{cite web| url= http://www.biography.com/people/taylor-swift-369608| title= Taylor Swift Biography: Singer (1989–)| publisher= Biography.com (FYI) / A&E Networks| accessdate= 2015-04-09| deadurl= no| archiveurl= https://web.archive.org/web/20160830131709/http://www.biography.com/people/taylor-swift-369608| archivedate= 2016-08-30}}</ref><ref name=allmusic>{{cite web | url = http://www.allmusic.com/artist/taylor-swift-mn0000472102/biography | title = [Taylor Swift] Artist Biography | first = Andrew | last = Leahey | website = AllMusic | accessdate = 2015-04-09 | deadurl = no | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20150405204335/http://www.allmusic.com/artist/taylor-swift-mn0000472102/biography | archivedate = 2015-04-05 }}</ref>，其名源自鄉村歌手[[詹姆士·泰勒|詹姆士·泰勒]]<ref>{{cite news | title= Walter Scott Asks ... James Taylor | work= Parade | date= 2015-06-14}}</ref>。父亲斯科特·金斯利·斯威夫特（{{lang|en|Scott Kingsley Swift}}）是[[美林证券|美林证券]]的财务顾问<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.udel.edu/udaily/2010/sep/swift092309.html |title=Taylor Swift's father is a Blue Hen |publisher=Udel.edu |date=2009-09-23 |accessdate=2012-04-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120818132347/http://www.udel.edu/udaily/2010/sep/swift092309.html |archivedate=2012-08-18 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.newyorksocialdiary.com/node/1909249 |title=4.1.13: LIZ SMITH: I'm a Taylor Swift "Groupie." |publisher=New York Social Diary |date=2013-04-01 |accessdate=2013-12-14 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131213143014/http://www.newyorksocialdiary.com/node/1909249 |archivedate=2013-12-13 }}</ref>；他在宾夕法尼亚州长大，祖先三代当银行行长<ref name="widdicombe1">{{cite news |last=Widdicombe |first=Lizzie |title=You Belong With Me |url=http://www.newyorker.com/reporting/2011/10/10/111010fa_fact_widdicombe?currentPage=all |accessdate=2011-10-10 |newspaper=The New Yorker }}</ref><ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08">Rolling Stone Interview: The Unabridged Taylor Swift, 2008-12-02</ref>。母亲安德里·加德纳·斯威夫特（婚前的姓氏為「芬利」)（{{lang|en|Andrea Gardner Swift , née "Finlay"}}）<ref name=cnn2015>{{cite web| url=http://www.cnn.com/2015/04/09/entertainment/taylor-swift-mother-cancer-feat/| title=Taylor Swift: My mom has cancer| first=Brandon| last=Griggs| publisher=CNN| date=2015-04-09| accessdate=2015-04-09| deadurl=no| archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150412024926/http://www.cnn.com/2015/04/09/entertainment/taylor-swift-mother-cancer-feat| name="marieclaire1">{{cite web |last=Cutter |first=Kimberly |url=http://www.marieclaire.com/celebrity-lifestyle/celebrities/taylor-swift-quotes-2 |title=Taylor Swift's Rise to America's Sweetheart |page=2 |work=Marie Claire |date=2010-06-02 |accessdate=2012-04-19 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120315024847/http://www.marieclaire.com/celebrity-lifestyle/celebrities/taylor-swift-quotes-2 |archivedate=2012-03-15 }}</ref>。泰勒絲的母亲虽是美国人，但在[[新加坡|新加坡]]生活了10年，后回国定居于[[得克萨斯州|得克萨斯州]]；其父是工程师，主管全[[东南亚|东南亚]]工作<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" />。泰勒絲還有一個弟弟[[奧斯汀·斯威夫特|奧斯汀‧斯威夫特]]，目前是一名演員。

泰勒絲的童年是在宾夕法尼亚州{{le|库鲁姆镇区 (宾夕法尼亚州)|Cumru Township, Pennsylvania|库鲁姆镇区}}的圣诞树农场度过的<ref>{{cite web |url=http://news.google.com/newspapers?id=uWUlAAAAIBAJ&sjid=8qYFAAAAIBAJ&pg=2689%2C4515063 |title=New golf course is no picnic |last=Reinbrecht |first=Steve |publisher=''Reading Eagle'' (via Google Books) |date=1996-10-07 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140908123448/http://news.google.com/newspapers?id=uWUlAAAAIBAJ&sjid=8qYFAAAAIBAJ&pg=2689,4515063 |archivedate=2014-09-08 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |last=Raab |first=Scott |url=http://www.esquire.com/entertainment/music/a30491/taylor-swift-1114/ |title=Taylor Swift Interview |website=Esquire |date=2014-10-20 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150216031004/http://www.esquire.com/entertainment/music/a30491/taylor-swift-1114/ |archivedate=2015-02-16 }}</ref>。她在[[方济各会|方济各会]]修女经营的安微尼亚·[[蒙台梭利教育法|蒙台梭利]]学校（{{lang|en|Alvernia Montessori School}}）读学前班和幼儿园<ref>{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift was a Montessori student|url=http://www.examiner.com/article/taylor-swift-was-a-montessori-student|website=Examiner.com|accessdate=2015-09-03|date=2010-02-14|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150924072314/http://www.examiner.com/article/taylor-swift-was-a-montessori-student|archivedate=2015-09-24}}</ref>，后转学到男女混合的私立学校{{le|韦恩德克罗夫学校|Wyndcroft School}}<ref name="readingeagle1">{{cite web |last=Hatza |first=George |url=http://readingeagle.com/article.aspx?id=116460 |title=Taylor Swift: Growing into superstardom |website=Readingeagle |date=2008-12-08 |accessdate=2012-04-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120401101613/http://readingeagle.com/article.aspx?id=116460 |archivedate=2012-04-01 }}</ref>。泰勒絲和他的弟弟在[[长老会|长老会]]的信仰影响下长大，每年夏季她都会去[[假期聖經學校|假期聖經學校]]<ref>{{cite web |url=http://raretaylorswift.webs.com/apps/photos/photo?photoid=175759985 |title=Article about Taylor's dad – Rare Taylor Swift |website=Raretaylorswift |date=2013-03-07 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131102032324/http://raretaylorswift.webs.com/apps/photos/photo?photoid=175759985 |archivedate=2013-11-02 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://words-of-whimsy.blogspot.co.uk/2011/04/taylor-swift-was-my-bff.html |title=words of whimsy: Taylor Swift Was My BFF |website=Words of whimsy |date=2011-04-19 |accessdate=2013-12-06 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131203010348/http://words-of-whimsy.blogspot.co.uk/2011/04/taylor-swift-was-my-bff.html |archivedate=2013-12-03 }}</ref>。九岁那年，举家迁往宾夕法尼亚州怀俄米辛郊区的出租屋<ref>{{cite web |author=Lauren Mennen, Philly.com |url=http://www.philly.com/philly/classifieds/real_estate/Taylor_Swifts_Wyomissing_childhood_home_on_the_market_for_799500.html |title=Taylor Swift's Wyomissing childhood home on the market for $799,500 |work=Philadelphia Daily News |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=no |archivedate=2013-11-04 }}</ref>。泰勒絲就读于{{le|西雷德中心小学|West Reading Elementary Center}}和{{le|怀俄米辛中学|Wyomissing Area Junior/Senior High School}}<ref>{{cite web |url=http://blogs.mcall.com/lehighvalleymusic/2010/01/wyomissing-schools-get-swift-gift-taylor-made-for-them.html |title=Wyomissing Schools get Swift gift Taylor made for them – Lehigh Valley Music }}</ref>。每到夏天，泰勒絲就去父母在新泽西州{{le|石港 (新泽西州)|Stone Harbor, New Jersey|石港}}的海滨度假屋避暑，她表示那儿是「我的大多数童年记忆形成」的地方<ref name="vogue4">{{cite web |last=Van Meter |first=Jonathan |url=http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/?mbid=syn+d_omg#4 |title=Taylor Swift: The Single Life – Magazine |page=4 |work=Vogue |date=2012-01-17 |accessdate=2012-04-17 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120404032213/http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/?mbid=syn+d_omg#4 |archivedate=2012-04-04 }}</ref>。

也是在九岁那年，泰勒絲对伯克斯青年戏剧学院（{{lang|en|Berks Youth Theatre Academy}}）制作的众多音乐剧和表演非常感兴趣<ref>{{cite web|author1=Andrea Simpson|title=Taylor Swift and Her Chubby Cheeks Once Starred in 'Bye Bye Birdie'|url=http://www.celebuzz.com/2013-11-06/taylor-swift-and-her-chubby-cheeks-once-starred-in-bye-bye-birdie/|website=Celebuzz|publisher=Spinmedia|accessdate=2015-01-03|date=2013-11-06|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150103073009/http://www.celebuzz.com/2013-11-06/taylor-swift-and-her-chubby-cheeks-once-starred-in-bye-bye-birdie/|archivedate=2015-01-03}}</ref>，并定期前往百老汇旁听声乐课和表演课<ref>{{cite web |author=Brittany Joy Cooper |url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-acting-emma-stone/ |title=Taylor Swift Opens Up About a Future in Acting and Admiration for Emma Stone |work=Taste of Country |date=2012-04-15 |accessdate=2012-04-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120417225849/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-acting-emma-stone/ |archivedate=2012-04-17 }}</ref>。泰勒絲后来把注意力转向乡村音乐，因为[[仙妮亚·唐恩|仙妮亚·唐恩]]的歌曲让她“围着街区跑了四次，做着什么都有的白日梦”<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.guardian.co.uk/music/2012/oct/18/taylor-swift-want-believe-pretty-lies |location=London |work=The Guardian |first=Alex |last=MacPherson |title=Taylor Swift: 'I want to believe in pretty lies' |date=2012-10-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121023104047/http://www.guardian.co.uk/music/2012/oct/18/taylor-swift-want-believe-pretty-lies |archivedate=2012-10-23 }}</ref>。她依靠在当地节日、咖啡馆、博览会、歌唱比赛、花园俱乐部、童子军会议和体育赛事上表演度过周末<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" /><ref name="marieclaire1" /><ref>{{cite web |last=DeLuca |first=Dan |url=http://articles.philly.com/2011-08-08/news/29864618_1_taylor-swift-local-angle-show-woman |title=Taylor Swift works crowd, local angle smoothly |work=Philadelphia Daily News |date=2010-08-08 |accessdate=2012-04-19 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121119003408/http://articles.philly.com/2011-08-08/news/29864618_1_taylor-swift-local-angle-show-woman |archivedate=2012-11-19 }}</ref>。11岁时，屡次碰壁后<ref name="albuminfo">{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1546980/when-she-thinks-tim-mcgraw-taylor-swift-savors-payoff.jhtml |title=When She Thinks "Tim McGraw," Taylor Swift Savors Payoff: Hardworking Teen to Open for George Strait Next Year |date=2006-12-01 |first=Edward |last=Morris |publisher=CMT |accessdate=2010-03-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sLt6qhM?url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1546980/when-she-thinks-tim-mcgraw-taylor-swift-savors-payoff.jhtml |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref>，泰勒絲最终赢得当地的才艺比赛，有机会为[[查理·丹尼尔斯|查理·丹尼尔斯]]在{{le|斯特劳斯镇|Strausstown}}露天剧场的演出的开场表演中登台献艺<ref>{{cite web|author1=Lisa Popeil|title=How Did Taylor Swift Make It?|url=http://voicecouncil.com/how-did-taylor-swift-make-it/|publisher=Voice Council Magazine|accessdate=2015-01-03|date=2014-11-30|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150103073326/http://voicecouncil.com/how-did-taylor-swift-make-it/|archivedate=2015-01-03}}</ref>。

观看了《{{le|音乐背后|Behind the Music}}》介绍[[菲丝·希尔|菲丝·希尔]]的一集节目后，泰勒絲清楚地意识到，要追求音乐事业，必须去[[田纳西州|田纳西州]][[纳什维尔|纳什维尔]]<ref name="telegraph1">{{cite news |author=Nisha Lilia Diu |url=http://www.telegraph.co.uk/culture/music/8421110/Taylor-Swift-I-wont-do-sexy-shoots.html |title=Taylor Swift: 'I won't do sexy shoots' |newspaper=The Daily Telegraph |date=2011-04-03 |accessdate=2012-04-17 |location=London |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121030041323/http://www.telegraph.co.uk/culture/music/8421110/Taylor-Swift-I-wont-do-sexy-shoots.html |archivedate=2012-10-30 }}</ref>。11岁那年，她和母亲去纳什维尔向唱片公司{{le|音乐街|Music Row}}递交卡拉OK翻唱[[桃莉·巴顿|桃莉·巴顿]]和[[南方小鸡|南方小鸡]]歌曲的试样唱片<ref name="CMT 2008-11-26">{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1600309/cmt-insider-interview-taylor-swift-part-1-of-2.jhtml |title=News : CMT Insider Interview: Taylor Swift (Part 1 of 2) |publisher=CMT |date=2008-11-26 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113174613/http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1600309/cmt-insider-interview-taylor-swift-part-1-of-2.jhtml |archivedate=2012-11-13 }}</ref>。被唱片公司摈弃后，泰勒絲意识到“我跟镇子里的每个人想要做同一件事。所以，我一直想，我需要走出一条与众不同的道路<ref name="americansongwriter2">{{cite web |url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/ |title=Taylor Swift: The Garden In The Machine |publisher=American Songwriter |date=2011-05-02 |accessdate=2012-05-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120510173906/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/ |archivedate=2012-05-10 }}</ref>。”

12岁那年，泰勒絲学会弹奏吉他三和弦，这激励着她创作个人第一首歌《幸运的你》（{{lang|en|''Lucky You''}}）<ref>{{cite web |last=Rollo |first=Sarah |url=http://www.digitalspy.com/showbiz/news/a185076/computer-repairman-taught-swift-guitar.html |title=Showbiz – News – Computer repairman taught Swift guitar |work=Digital Spy |date=2009-11-03 |accessdate=2009-12-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20091225165049/http://www.digitalspy.com/showbiz/news/a185076/computer-repairman-taught-swift-guitar.html |archivedate=2009-12-25 }}</ref>。此前，她曾凭借个人诗作《我衣橱里的怪物》（{{lang|en|''Monster in My Closet''}}）赢得全国诗歌大赛，但现在她专注于写歌<ref>{{cite news |url=http://voices.washingtonpost.com/postrock/2008/02/her_song_talking_taylor_swift_1.html |title=Her Song: Talking Taylor Swift – Post Rock |work=The Washington Post |date=2008-02-28 |accessdate=2012-04-19}}</ref>。2003年，泰勒絲和父母开始与纽约音乐经纪人丹·迪米特洛（{{lang|en|Dan Dymtrow}}）合作。在迪米特洛的帮助下，泰勒絲为[[Abercrombie_&_Fitch|Abercrombie & Fitch]]当模特儿，这是他们的“明日之星”计划的一部分，而她的原创歌曲收入[[美宝莲|美宝莲]]精选CD，还受邀与各大唱片公司的面谈<ref name="americanbar">{{cite web |title=americanbar.org |format=PDF |url=http://www.americanbar.org/content/dam/aba/migrated/Forums/entsports/PublicDocuments/oppositionbrief.authcheckdam.PDF |accessdate=2012-04-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121011190303/http://www.americanbar.org/content/dam/aba/migrated/Forums/entsports/PublicDocuments/oppositionbrief.authcheckdam.PDF |archivedate=2012-10-11 }}</ref>。在[[RCA唱片|RCA唱片]]的舞台上演绎原创歌曲后，这位八年级的学生获得艺人发展合同，开始与母亲频繁前往纳什维尔<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/31032270/ns/dateline_nbc-newsmakers/t/tour-taylor-swift/ |title=On tour with Taylor Swift – Dateline NBC – Newsmakers |publisher=MSNBC |date=2009-05-31 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121107044904/http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/31032270/ns/dateline_nbc-newsmakers/t/tour-taylor-swift/ |archivedate=2012-11-07 }}</ref>。为帮助泰勒絲打入乡村音乐界，父亲在她14岁那年被调到美林证券纳什维尔分部，全家人搬进田纳西州{{le|亨德森维尔|Hendersonville, Tennessee}}的湖景大宅<ref name="widdicombe1" />。

{{quote|为了释放所有压力，我们父母安慰自己：“我们搬家是因为我们爱这个地方，所以不要担心。”其实他们一点也不了解这个行业，没有涉足过娱乐界，但我迷恋着它，所以他们做了研究，广泛阅读相关书籍，用尽他们能做到的一切办法帮助我。他们的确很了不起<ref>{{cite news |author=Lina Das |url=http://www.dailymail.co.uk/home/you/article-2218012/Taylor-Swift-Men-hand-inspiration-plate.html |title=Taylor Swift: 'Men hand me inspiration on a plate' |work=Daily Mail |date=2012-10-29 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |location=London |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160709072701/http://www.dailymail.co.uk/home/you/article-2218012/Taylor-Swift-Men-hand-inspiration-plate.html |archivedate=2016-07-09 }}</ref>。}}

在田纳西州，泰勒絲在{{tsl|en|Hendersonville_High_School_(Tennessee)|田纳西州亨德森维尔高中|亨德森维尔高中}}读高一和高二<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1648575/taylor-swifts-high-school-names-auditorium-in-her-honor.jhtml |title=News : Taylor Swift's High School Names Auditorium in Her Honor |publisher=CMT |date=2010-09-23 |accessdate=2012-04-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120427205811/http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1648575/taylor-swifts-high-school-names-auditorium-in-her-honor.jhtml |archivedate=2012-04-27 }}</ref>。后来，为了给巡演日程腾出空间，泰勒絲转学到提供家教服务的私立基督教学校亚伦学院（{{lang|en|Aaron Academy}}）。泰勒絲保持了4.0级的平均成绩，并于2008年获得高中文凭，花一年时间提前学完最后两年的课程<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2008/02/27/AR2008022703749.html |title=Taylor Swift Puts The Kid in Country |work=The Washington Post |date=2008-02-27 |accessdate=2012-07-06 |first=J. Freedom |last=du Lac |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110820135852/http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2008/02/27/AR2008022703749.html |archivedate=2011-08-20 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |author=Vanessa Grigoriadis |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/the-very-pink-very-perfect-life-of-taylor-swift-20090305 |title=The Very Pink, Very Perfect Life of Taylor Swift | Music News |work=Rolling Stone |date=2009-03-05 |accessdate=2012-10-31 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121015183138/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/the-very-pink-very-perfect-life-of-taylor-swift-20090305 |archivedate=2012-10-15 }}</ref>。

14岁时，泰勒絲搬到田纳西州納許維爾<ref name="Ray">{{cite web |url=http://www.britannica.com/EBchecked/topic/1580265/Taylor-Swift |title=Taylor Swift |last=Ray |first=Michael |work=Encyclopædia Britannica |accessdate=2014-11-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141112110409/http://www.britannica.com/EBchecked/topic/1580265/Taylor-Swift |archivedate=2014-11-12 }}</ref>，与[[RCA唱片|RCA唱片]]签订艺人发展合約<ref>{{cite web|author1=Vicky Castro|title=How to Succeed as an Entrepreneur, Taylor Swift Style|url=http://www.inc.com/vicky-castro/how-to-succeed-as-an-entrepreneur-taylor-swift-style.html|website=Inc.com|publisher=Monsueto Ventures|accessdate=2015-02-09|date=2015-02-06|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/6klgx4ZPE?url=http://www.inc.com/vicky-castro/how-to-succeed-as-an-entrepreneur-taylor-swift-style.html|archivedate=2016-09-24}}</ref>。泰勒絲继续与经验丰富的音乐街词曲作者合作，其中包括{{le|特洛伊·福吉斯|Troy Verges}}、{{le|布雷特·比威尔斯|Brett Beavers}}、{{le|布雷特·詹姆斯|Brett James}}、{{le|麦克·麦克安内|Mac McAnally}}和{{le|沃伦兄弟|The Warren Brothers}}<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/3/ |title=Taylor Swift: The Garden In The Machine |publisher=American Songwriter |date=2011-05-02 |accessdate=2012-05-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130807054922/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/3/ |archivedate=2013-08-07 }}</ref><ref name="sonydeal">{{cite web |url=http://www.bmi.com/news/entry/234444 |title=Songwriter Taylor Swift Signs Publishing Deal With Sony/ATV |publisher=BMI.com |date=2005-05-12 |accessdate=2012-04-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121204104706/http://www.bmi.com/news/entry/234444 |archivedate=2012-12-04 }}</ref>。她最终与{{le|利兹·罗斯|Liz Rose}}建立了长期的合作关系。泰勒絲观看了罗斯在RCA作曲家活动上的表演，建议他们应该共同写歌<ref name="americansongwriter1">{{cite web |last=Kosser |first=Michael |url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2010/06/liz-rose-co-writer-to-the-stars/ |title=Liz Rose: Co-Writer to the Stars |work=American Songwriter |date=2010-06-03 |accessdate=2012-04-19 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111224215950/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2010/06/liz-rose-co-writer-to-the-stars/ |archivedate=2011-12-24 }}</ref>。两人在泰勒絲每周二下午放学后上两小时的作曲课程<ref name="majorlyindie1">{{cite web |url=http://www.majorlyindie.com/enewsletter/oleSpecialEditionNov08P2.cfm?storyid=350 |title=How Liz Rose and Taylor Swift Wrote the Hits |publisher=Majorlyindie.com |date=2008-11-20 |accessdate=2012-04-19}}</ref>。罗斯曾表示该课程是他“曾做过的最简单的事。基本上，我只做她的编辑。她会写那一天在学校发生的事。她对自己想要说的事有清晰的想象。她一定会成为最不可思议的苗子<ref>Blender, April 2008, page 54</ref>。”泰勒絲也开始与制作人{{le|内森·查普曼|Nathan Chapman (record producer)}}录制唱片样碟<ref name="americansongwriter1" />。

2004年在[[广播音乐公司|广播音乐公司]]词曲作者圈（{{lang|en|BMI Songwriter's Circle}}）于纽约{{le|痛苦终点酒吧|The Bitter End}}表演后<ref name="sonydeal" /><ref name="Eisenberg">{{cite web |url=http://www.businessinsider.com/taylor-swifts-journey-to-success-2012-10?op=1 |title=How Taylor Swift Conquered The Music World By Age 22 |last=Eisenbery |first=Dana |date=2012-10-25 |publisher=Business Insider |accessdate=2014-11-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141112074750/http://www.businessinsider.com/taylor-swifts-journey-to-success-2012-10?op=1 |archivedate=2014-11-12 }}</ref>，泰勒絲成为有史以来受雇于[[索尼/联合电视音乐出版|索尼/联合电视音乐出版]]最年轻的词曲作者<ref>{{cite web |last=DeLuca |first=Dan |title=Focused on 'great songs' Taylor Swift isn't thinking about "the next level" or Joe Jon as gossip |url=http://articles.philly.com/2008-11-11/news/25256467_1_big-machine-records-joe-jonas-country-music-association-awards |page=1 |work=Philadelphia Daily News |accessdate=2012-04-17 |date=2008-11-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121118235847/http://articles.philly.com/2008-11-11/news/25256467_1_big-machine-records-joe-jonas-country-music-association-awards |archivedate=2012-11-18 }}</ref>。15岁时，泰勒絲离开[[RCA唱片|RCA唱片]]，公司希望她录制其他詞曲作家的作品，直至等到18岁发行专辑，但她已准备好带上她自己的素材踏上职业生涯<ref name="albuminfo" /><ref>{{cite news |last=Willman |first=Chris |title=Taylor Swift's Road to Fame – The chipmunk years |url=http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0,,20176102_2,00.html |work=Entertainment Weekly |accessdate=2012-04-22 |page=2 |date=2008-02-05 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130502223051/http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0,,20176102_2,00.html |archivedate=2013-05-02 }}</ref>。泰勒絲后来回忆：“我真的觉得留给我的时间不多了。我想在专辑里捕捉我这些年来的生活轨迹，它们依然代表着我的经历<ref>{{cite news |author=Rock and Pop Music |url=http://www.telegraph.co.uk/culture/music/rockandpopmusic/5202294/Taylor-Swift-the-19-year-old-country-music-star-conquering-America-and-now-Britain.html |title=Taylor Swift: the 19-year-old country music star conquering America – and now Britain – ''The Daily Telegraph'' |newspaper=The Daily Telegraph |accessdate=2012-08-30 |location=London |date=2009-04-26 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120105153224/http://www.telegraph.co.uk/culture/music/rockandpopmusic/5202294/Taylor-Swift-the-19-year-old-country-music-star-conquering-America-and-now-Britain.html |archivedate=2012-01-05 }}</ref>。”她还跟经纪人丹·迪米特洛分道扬镳，这让丹后来将泰勒絲及她的父母诉诸法律。2010年，法官驳回迪米特洛的六项法律索偿，剩下的[[不当得利|不当得利]]索偿达成庭外和解<ref name="americanbar" /><ref name="Bell"/><ref name="Bell">{{cite web|author1=Matthew Belloni|title=Taylor Swift's Ex-Manager Suing Over Contract Dispute|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/954687/taylor-swifts-ex-manager-suing-over-contract-dispute|work=Billboard|accessdate=2015-01-03|date=2010-10-08|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141226130844/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/954687/taylor-swifts-ex-manager-suing-over-contract-dispute|archivedate=2014-12-26}}</ref>。

2005年在纳什维尔{{le|青鸟咖啡店|Bluebird Cafe}}的行业展示会上，泰勒絲受到{{le|梦工厂唱片|DreamWorks Records}}高管{{le|斯科特·波切塔|Scott Borchetta}}的关注，其时波切塔正筹建他的独立唱片公司[[大機器唱片|大机器唱片]]。泰勒絲成为了首位签约该公司的艺人，她的父亲还购买了这间新兴公司的百分之三的股份，估值12万美元<ref>Rolling Stone, October 25, 2012, Taylor in Wonderland by Brian Hiatt, page 39</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.forbes.com/sites/zackomalleygreenburg/2013/06/26/toby-keith-cowboy-capitalist-countrys-500-million-man/2/ |work=Forbes |title=Toby Keith, Cowboy Capitalist: Country's $500 Million Man – Forbes |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160827173032/http://www.forbes.com/sites/zackomalleygreenburg/2013/06/26/toby-keith-cowboy-capitalist-countrys-500-million-man/2/ |archivedate=2016-08-27 }}</ref>。当作认识乡村音乐行业，波切塔安排泰勒絲去{{le|乡村音乐学院音乐节|CMA Music Festival|CMA音乐节}}担任艺人保镖的实习工作<ref name="marieclaire2">{{cite web |last=Reuter |first=Annie |url=http://www.marieclaire.com/celebrity-lifestyle/celebrities/taylor-swift-interview |title=Taylor Swift Interview |publisher=Marie Claire |date=2009-07-22 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120428051631/http://www.marieclaire.com/celebrity-lifestyle/celebrities/taylor-swift-interview |archivedate=2012-04-28 }}</ref>。

== 演唱生涯 ==

=== 2006年－2008年：《[[泰勒·斯威夫特_(專輯)|泰勒絲]]》===
[[File:taylor_Swift.jpg|thumb]][[圣玛丽亚_(加利福尼亚州)|圣玛丽亚]]Maverick Saloon & Grill表演]]
與[[大機器唱片|大機器唱片]]签约后不久，泰勒絲开始创作[[泰勒·斯威夫特_(专辑)|首张同名专辑]]。与老牌纳什维尔制作人一番摸索后，泰勒说服大机器雇佣内森·查普曼当她的样碟制作人。虽说是首次录制录音室专辑，但泰勒絲感觉两人产生了很好的“化学反应”<ref name="albuminfo" />。泰勒絲独自创作了专辑里的三首歌曲，包括两首单曲，其余八首与罗斯、{{le|罗伯特·埃利斯·奥拉尔|Robert Ellis Orrall}}、布莱恩·马赫（{{lang|en|Brian Maher}}）和{{le|安杰洛·佩特拉杰吉亚|Angelo Petraglia}}共同创作<ref name="liner">{{cite AV media notes |title=Taylor Swift |others=Taylor Swift |year=2006 |type=CD |publisher=Big Machine Records |id=BMR120702}}</ref>。从音乐上讲，这张专辑“混杂了传统乡村音乐和轻快的摇滚吉他<ref name=albumguide>{{cite web|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140322081241/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/artists/taylor-swift/albumguide |archivedate=2014-03-22 |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/artists/taylor-swift/albumguide |title=Taylor Swift: Album Guide |publisher=Rolling Stone Music |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。”

专辑于2006年10月24日发布，《[[纽约时报|纽约时报]]》的乔恩·卡拉马尼卡（{{lang|en|Jon Caramanica}}）把专辑形容为“流行乐理念的乡村音乐小杰作，泰勒絲女士坚实、恳求般的声线蕴含着天真和愤世嫉俗<ref name="nytimes2">{{cite web|url=http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/07/arts/music/07cara.html|title=A Young Outsider's Life Turned Inside Out] By Jon Caramanica|work=The New York Times|date=2008-09-05|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130522012819/http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/07/arts/music/07cara.html|archivedate=2013-05-22}}</ref>。”《[[纽约客|纽约客]]》杂志的{{le|萨沙·弗里尔-琼斯|Sasha Frere-Jones}}将16岁的泰勒絲称为“神童”。他指出，《[[我们的歌_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|我们的歌]]》“让我想再听几遍”。他还赞赏歌词“他一手握着方向盘，另一只手抚摸我的心房”（He's got a one-hand feel on the steering wheel, the other on my heart.）<ref>{{cite web|author1=Sasha Frere-Jones |title=Prodigy |url=http://www.newyorker.com/magazine/2008/11/10/prodigy-6 |website=The New Yorker |accessdate=2015-07-14 |date=2008-11-10 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141101063854/http://www.newyorker.com/magazine/2008/11/10/prodigy-6 |archivedate=2014-11-01 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。《[[滚石_(杂志)|滚石]]》杂志的乐评人称泰勒絲“天真但非常地经验老到”，并钦佩《我们的歌》“疯狂跷课跑去唱歌的曲调跟[[布兰妮·斯皮尔斯|布兰妮]]一样，有点{{le|佩西·克莱恩|Patsy Cline|佩西}}的风格<ref name=albumguide />。”

[[File:Taylor_Swift_at_Yahoo_crop.jpg|left]][[森尼韦尔_(加利福尼亚州)|森尼韦尔]][[雅虎|雅虎]]总部表演]]
2006年6月主打单曲《[[蒂姆·麦格劳_(歌曲)|蒂姆·麦格劳]]》发布时，大机器唱片仍处在起步阶段，泰勒絲在母亲的帮助下把“单曲CD装进信封寄给电台<ref name="EW1">{{cite news |last=Willman |first=Chris |title=Taylor Swift's Road to Fame |url=http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0,,20176102_3,00.html |work=Entertainment Weekly |accessdate=2012-04-22 |page=3 |date=2008-02-05 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130502210917/http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0,,20176102_3,00.html |archivedate=2013-05-02 }}</ref>。”她花了2006年的大部分时间在电台巡演中宣传专辑。后来她表示，“电台巡演对于大多数歌手而言只需六个星期，而我的搞了半年<ref name="albuminfo" />。”泰勒絲还烤饼干、画画送给在电台中播放她歌曲的主持人<ref name="Rolling Stone 2009-03">Rolling Stone, March 2009</ref>。她还在多档电视节目中亮相，包括《{{le|奥普里大剧院|Grand Ole Opry}}》<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-cFIJKat0Z0&lr=1 |title=Taylor Swift performs 'Teardrops on My Guitar' at the Grand Ole Opry |publisher=YouTube |accessdate=2012-08-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130218023418/http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-cFIJKat0Z0&lr=1 |archivedate=2013-02-18 }}</ref>、《[[早安美国|早安美国]]》<ref name="taylorjoinstour">{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1543489/taylor-swift-joins-rascal-flatts-tour.jhtml |title=Taylor Swift Joins Rascal Flatts Tour |date=2006-10-18 |work=CMT News |accessdate=2010-03-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sM43Mo9?url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1543489/taylor-swift-joins-rascal-flatts-tour.jhtml |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref>和《{{le|互动全方位|Total Request Live}}》<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.mtv.com/videos/news/318549/trl-embraced-me-for-who-i-am.jhtml#id=1599439 |title=TRL Embraced Me for who I Am |publisher=MTV |accessdate=2010-03-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sM5Z9hF?url=http://www.mtv.com/videos/news/318549/trl-embraced-me-for-who-i-am.jhtml#id=1599439 |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref>。泰勒絲自称为“网络儿童”，利用[[Myspace|Myspace]]建立粉丝群<ref>{{cite web |last=Gonzalez |first=John |title=Taylor Swift comes to VanAndel Arena this week on Fearless Tour |url=http://www.mlive.com/entertainment/grand-rapids/index.ssf/2009/09/taylor_swift_comes_to_vanandel.html |publisher=mlive.com |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2009-09-27 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121024232440/http://www.mlive.com/entertainment/grand-rapids/index.ssf/2009/09/taylor_swift_comes_to_vanandel.html |archivedate=2012-10-24 }}</ref>。这在当时是“乡村音乐的革命”<ref name="Caramanica 2008-11-07">{{cite news |last=Caramanica |first=Jon |title=My Music, MySpace, My Life |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2008/11/09/arts/music/09cara.html?_r=1&pagewanted=all |work=The New York Times |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2008-11-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130522023759/http://www.nytimes.com/2008/11/09/arts/music/09cara.html?_r=1&pagewanted=all |archivedate=2013-05-22 }}</ref>。波切塔表示他决定签下这名16岁的创作型歌手，起初让他在唱片业同行中扬眉吐气，但泰勒的已被挖掘进这个她此前还不了解的行业：十几岁的女孩听乡村音乐<ref name="Caramanica 2008-11-07" />。

除了《蒂姆·麦格劳》，2007年和2008年全年还有四首单曲被发布：《[[泪洒吉他|泪洒吉他]]》、《我们的歌》、《[[烧掉的回忆|烧掉的回忆]]》和《[[早该拒绝|早该拒绝]]》。四首歌均在公告牌热门乡村歌曲榜单中取得优异的成绩，其中《我们的歌》和《早该拒绝》位列榜首。《我们的歌》让泰勒絲成为凭借一己之力创作并演唱榜首乡村歌曲的最年轻个人<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.gactv.com/gac/cda/article_print/0,3008,GAC_26063_5769818_DS-ARTICLE-RIGHT-RAIL,00.html |title=Taylor Swift No. 1 on iTunes |date=2007-12-19 |work=Great American Country |publisher=Scripps Networks Interactive |accessdate=2010-07-05 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120303122404/http://www.gactv.com/gac/cda/article_print/0%2C3008%2CGAC_26063_5769818_DS-ARTICLE-RIGHT-RAIL%2C00.html |archivedate=2012-03-03 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。《泪洒吉他》成为次等的流行热门单曲，位列[[公告牌百强单曲榜|公告牌百强单曲榜]]第13位<ref name="billboard">{{cite web |url={{BillboardURLbyName |artist=taylor swift |chart=all}}|title=Teardrops on My Guitar – Taylor Swift|work=Billboard|accessdate=2010-12-15}}</ref>。专辑发行首周售出39000万张<ref>{{cite web |author=Chris Harris |url=http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1599721/20081119/swift__taylor.jhtml |title=Taylor Swift Scores First Chart-Topping Debut With Fearless |date=2008-11-19 |publisher=MTV |accessdate=2008-12-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20081220070517/http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1599721/20081119/swift__taylor.jhtml |archivedate=2008-12-20 }}</ref>，截至2011年3月，在全球已卖出超过550万张<ref>{{cite press release |url=http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/taylor-swift-tops-20-million-in-record-sales-118987324.html |title=Taylor Swift Tops 20 Million in Record Sales |date=2011-03-31 |publisher=Big Machine Records |accessdate=2011-04-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/6DiM06qum?url=http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/taylor-swift-tops-20-million-in-record-sales-118987324.html |archivedate=2013-01-16 }}</ref>。2007年10月，泰勒絲发行了假日专辑《{{le|四季之声：泰勒·斯威夫特假日精选集|Sounds of the Season: The Taylor Swift Holiday Collection}}》，后于2008年7月发行[[迷你专辑|迷你专辑]]《[[美丽的双眼|美丽的双眼]]》<ref name="cst">{{cite web |url=http://www.countrystandardtime.com/news/newsitem.asp?xid=1947 |title=Taylor Swift owns top of country chart |accessdate=2008-12-26 |work=Country Standard Time |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20080731160355/http://www.countrystandardtime.com/news/newsitem.asp?xid=1947 |archivedate=2008-07-31 }}</ref><ref name="gac">{{cite web|url=http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0,3034,GAC_26063_5903580_,00.html |title=Wal-Mart "Eyes" New Taylor Swift Project |accessdate=2008-07-24 |work=Great American Country |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20080719100609/http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0%2C3034%2CGAC_26063_5903580_%2C00.html |archivedate=2008-07-19 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。

泰勒絲开展广泛的巡演，宣传《[[泰勒·斯威夫特_(專輯)|泰勒絲]]》。除了自己的歌曲，泰勒絲还翻唱了[[碧昂丝|碧昂丝]]、[[蕾哈娜|蕾哈娜]]、{{link-en|約翰·懷特 (歌手)|John White (singer)|约翰·怀特}}、[[林纳·史金纳|林纳·史金纳]]和[[埃米纳姆|埃米纳姆]]的歌曲<ref name="CMT 2007-11-12">{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/20-questions/1574118/20-questions-with-taylor-swift.jhtml |title=News : 20 Questions With Taylor Swift |publisher=Country Music Television |date=2007-11-12 |accessdate=2012-04-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sLx8yBw?url=http://www.cmt.com/news/20-questions/1574118/20-questions-with-taylor-swift.jhtml |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,1893502,00.html |title=Interview with Taylor Swift |work=Time |date=2009-04-23 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120531092027/http://www.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,1893502,00.html |archivedate=2012-05-31 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://articles.mcall.com/2007-02-10/features/3716545_1_orpheus-chamber-orchestra-swift-string-orchestra |title=The Week in Review – Morning Call |publisher=Articles.mcall.com |date=2007-02-10 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131221004014/http://articles.mcall.com/2007-02-10/features/3716545_1_orpheus-chamber-orchestra-swift-string-orchestra |archivedate=2013-12-21 }}</ref>。她还在演唱会前后与歌迷进行长达四小时的零距离接触的見面會<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0,,GAC_26063_5735572,00.html |title=Taylor Swift Embraces the Meet & Greet |publisher=Gactv.com |date=2010-10-31 |accessdate=2012-05-21 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130807155454/http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0%2C%2CGAC_26063_5735572%2C00.html |archivedate=2013-08-07 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。除了音乐节和戏剧日，泰勒絲还为多位乡村音乐家的巡演作开场表演。2006年年底，她为[[雷可福磊斯|雷可福磊斯]]的“我和我的帮派巡演”（{{lang|en|Me & My Gang Tour}}）最后九场表演作开场演出，替换被解雇的客串艺人{{le|艾瑞克·乔治|Eric Church}}<ref name="taylorjoinstour" />。泰勒絲随后向乔治寄去她的首张金唱片，附带字条：“感谢您在福磊斯巡演上‘过于冗长’和‘过于吵杂’的演出，我由衷地感激。——泰勒絲<ref>{{cite web |last=Burch |first=Cathalena E. |url=http://azstarnet.com/entertainment/blogs/caliente-tuned-in/article_61cb6c52-5bd1-11e0-88bd-001cc4c002e0.html |title=Eric Church's Taylor Swift story : Welcome to StarNet – Tucson, Arizona |publisher=Azstarnet.com |date=2011-03-31 |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120821153154/http://azstarnet.com/entertainment/blogs/caliente-tuned-in/article_61cb6c52-5bd1-11e0-88bd-001cc4c002e0.html |archivedate=2012-08-21 }}</ref>。”2007年，她为[[乔治·斯特雷特|乔治·斯特雷特]]巡演的头二十场表演作开场表演<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1546137/taylor-swift-joins-george-straits-2007-tour.jhtml |title=Taylor Swift Joins George Straits 2007 Tour |date=2006-11-17 |work=CMT News |accessdate=2010-03-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sQjGLvQ?url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1546137/taylor-swift-joins-george-straits-2007-tour.jhtml |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref>，并在{{le|肯尼·薛士尼|Kenny Chesney}}的“拖鞋夏日巡演”（{{lang|en|Flip-Flop Summer Tour}}）<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/20-questions/1574118/20-questions-with-taylor-swift.jhtml |title=20 Questions With Taylor Swift |publisher=CMT |date=2007-11-12 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sLx8yBw?url=http://www.cmt.com/news/20-questions/1574118/20-questions-with-taylor-swift.jhtml |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref>、[[布拉德·帕斯利|布拉德·帕斯利]]的“篝火与扩音器巡演”（{{lang|en|Bonfires & Amplifiers Tour}}）特定场次<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1549598/brad-paisley-plans-tour-with-three-opening-acts.jhtml |title=Brad Paisley Plans Tour With Three Opening Acts |date=2007-01-09 |work=CMT News |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref>和[[蒂姆·麦格罗|蒂姆·麦格罗]]与菲斯的“{{le|灵魂碰撞II联合巡演|Soul2Soul II Tour}}”中登场<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1561014/taylor-swift-joins-tim-mcgraw-faith-hill-on-tour.jhtml |title=Taylor Swift Joins Tim McGraw, Faith Hill on Tour |date=2007-07-01 |work=CMT News |accessdate=2010-03-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sQkpoIr?url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1561014/taylor-swift-joins-tim-mcgraw-faith-hill-on-tour.jhtml |archivedate=2012-08-13 }}</ref>。泰勒于2008年于“感觉依然良好”巡演（{{lang|en|Still Feels Good Tour}}）中再次为福磊斯开场<ref>{{cite web |url=http://countrymusic.about.com/od/concertreviewsm1/a/RFlattsConc08.htm |title=Rascal Flatts & Taylor Swift in Concert – Sacramento, CA – April 10, 2008 |first=Shelly |last=Fabian |publisher=About.com |accessdate=2010-06-22 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/69sQingeY?url=http://countrymusic.about.com/od/concertreviewsm1/a/RFlattsConc08.htm |archivedate=2012年8月13日 }}</ref>。

泰勒絲和{{le|阿兰·杰克逊|Alan Jackson}}共同被评为2007年{{le|纳什维尔歌曲作者协会|Nashville Songwriters Association}}年度词曲作者/艺人，泰勒絲成为获得该项殊荣的最年轻个人<ref>{{cite web|title=Success comes quickly for Taylor Swift|url=http://articles.mcall.com/2008-02-10/news/3984893_1_swift-platinum-taylor/2|website=MCall|accessdate=2015-07-13|date=2008-02-10|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150713130734/http://articles.mcall.com/2008-02-10/news/3984893_1_swift-platinum-taylor/2|archivedate=2015-07-13}}</ref>。她还赢得了{{le|乡村音乐协会|Country Music Association}}天际奖（{{lang|en|Horizon Award}}）最佳新人奖<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/pictures/taylor-swift/photo-gallery/2389485/2657043/artist_photo.jhtml |title=Photos : All Taylor Swift Pictures : Horizon Award Winner Poses in the Pressroom |publisher=CMT |date=2007-09-07 |accessdate=2012-05-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113174555/http://www.cmt.com/pictures/taylor-swift/photo-gallery/2389485/2657043/artist_photo.jhtml |archivedate=2012-11-13 }}</ref>、{{le|乡村音乐学院奖|Academy of Country Music Awards}}最佳女性歌手新人奖<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/pictures/43rd-annual-acm-awards-onstage-winners/1587677/2970629/photo.jhtml |title=Photos : 43rd Annual ACM Awards – Onstage: Winners : Acceptance Speech |publisher=CMT |date=2008-05-18 |accessdate=2012-05-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113174530/http://www.cmt.com/pictures/43rd-annual-acm-awards-onstage-winners/1587677/2970629/photo.jhtml |archivedate=2012-11-13 }}</ref>和[[全美音乐奖|全美音乐奖]]最受欢迎乡村女歌手奖<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.roughstock.com/blog/taylor-swift-rascal-flatts-carrie-underwood-score-@-2008-ama-awards |title=Taylor Swift, Rascal Flatts, Carrie Underwood Score at 2008 AMA Awards |publisher=Roughstock.com |date=2008-11-24 |accessdate=2012-05-21 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20091025180053/http://www.roughstock.com/blog/taylor-swift-rascal-flatts-carrie-underwood-score-%40-2008-ama-awards |archivedate=2009-10-25 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。她还被提名为2008年[[格莱美奖|格莱美奖]]最佳新人奖，但惜败给[[艾米·怀恩豪斯|艾米·怀恩豪斯]]<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.people.com/people/package/article/0,,20173658_20177270,00.html |title=Amy Winehouse Wins Best New Artist, Kanye West Pays Tribute to Mom – Grammy Awards 2008, Grammy Awards |work=People |date=2008-10-02 |accessdate=2012-05-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113083832/http://www.people.com/people/package/article/0%2C%2C20173658_20177270%2C00.html |archivedate=2012-11-13 }}</ref>。

=== 2008年－2010年：《[[放手去爱_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|無懼的愛]]》 ===
泰勒絲的第二张录音室专辑《[[放手去爱_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|放手去爱]]》于2008年10月11日发布。泰勒絲独自创作了专辑的七首歌曲，包括两首单曲，其余六首与罗斯、[[约翰·里奇|约翰·里奇]]、[[科尔比·凯雷|科尔比·凯雷]]和{{le|希拉里·林德茜|Hillary Lindsey}}共同创作<ref name="BMRATS0250">{{cite AV media notes |title=Fearless Platinum Edition |others=Taylor Swift |year=2008 |type=CD |publisher=Big Machine Records |id=BMRATS0250}}</ref>。专辑由她和内森·查普曼共同制作<ref name="BMRATS0250" />。从音乐上讲，专辑的特点被认为是“吉他声响亮却低沉，副歌激动人心”，偶尔有“小提琴和班卓琴交织”<ref name="rosen1">{{cite web |last=Rosen |first=Jody |title=Albums Reviews – Fearless |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/fearless-20081113 |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2008-11-13 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120815082027/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/fearless-20081113 |archivedate=2012-08-15 }}</ref>。

《[[纽约时报|纽约时报]]》的卡拉马尼卡称泰勒絲是“最优秀的流行乐词曲作者之一，是乡村音乐界最重要的实用主义者，她对内心世界的接触比大多数成年人还要多<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2008/12/21/arts/music/21cara.html?_r=1 |title=Sounds of Swagger and Sob Stories |date=2008-12-19 |work=The New York Times |accessdate=2008-12-20 |first=Jon |last=Caramanica |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090417044027/http://www.nytimes.com/2008/12/21/arts/music/21cara.html?_r=1 |archivedate=2009-04-17 }}</ref>。”《{{le|乡村之音|The Village Voice}}》的{{le|乔什·勒夫|Josh Love}}认为她展现出“超自然的智慧和包容性”，“巧妙地避开了陈腐平庸和假装深刻的废话典型日记作家陷阱<ref>{{cite web |last=Love |first=Josh |title=Taylor Swift's Teenage Country-Star Tales, Spiked With Actual Wisdom |url=http://www.villagevoice.com/2008-11-19/music/taylor-swift-s-teenage-country-star-tales-spiked-with-actual-wisdom/ |work=The Village Voice |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2008-11-19 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120708170250/http://www.villagevoice.com/2008-11-19/music/taylor-swift-s-teenage-country-star-tales-spiked-with-actual-wisdom/ |archivedate=2012-07-08 }}</ref>”。《[[滚石|滚石]]》的{{le|乔迪·罗森|Jody Rosen}}指出泰勒絲“是一位在主歌－副歌－连结架构方面有直观天赋的作曲学者，”其歌曲“亲切和真实得让人局促不安”，仿佛“从字面上撕开了乡下女孩的日记<ref name="rosen1" />”。乐评人[[罗伯特·克里斯盖乌|罗伯特·克里斯盖乌]]指出泰勒絲是一位“她还是个少女，但天赋和强大不能说是非比寻常，简直不可思议<ref name="RobertChristgau">{{cite web |title=Robert Christgau: CG: taylor swift |url=http://robertchristgau.com/get_artist.php?name=taylor+swift |publisher=robertchristgau.com |accessdate=2012-05-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120328103544/http://robertchristgau.com/get_artist.php?name=Taylor+Swift |archivedate=2012-03-28 }}</ref>。”

泰勒絲如今由罗伯特·艾伦打理的经纪公司掌管<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/biz/articles/news/1099235/billboard-power-100-taylor-swift |title=Power 100: Taylor Swift |work=Billboard |date=2012-01-26 |accessdate=2014-04-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140706084325/http://www.billboard.com/biz/articles/news/1099235/billboard-power-100-taylor-swift |archivedate=2014-07-06 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.allaccess.com/net-news/archive/story/118620/cma-announces-industry-sro-awards-nominees?ref=search |title=CMA Announces Industry SRO Awards Nominees |publisher=AllAccess.com |date=2013-05-21 |accessdate=2014-04-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140421095709/http://www.allaccess.com/net-news/archive/story/118620/cma-announces-industry-sro-awards-nominees?ref=search |archivedate=2014-04-21 }}</ref>，自发行之日起，他们对《无惧的爱》的宣传非常的重视。有一集《[[艾伦秀|艾伦秀]]》专门为专辑的发行而设，泰勒絲也频繁亮相各大谈话节目<ref name="Caramanica 2008-11-07" /><ref>{{cite web |last=Keel |first=Beverly |url=http://www.tennessean.com/article/20081109/TUNEIN/105260003/Taylor-Swift-Regular-teenager-country-star |title=Taylor Swift: Regular teenager, country star |work=The Tennessean |date=2008-11-09 |accessdate=2012-05-29}}</ref>。她透过[[Twitter|Twitter]]、个人视频播客等社交媒体平台与粉丝交流，还共同主持了[[2008年MTV音乐录影带大奖|2008年MTV音乐录影带大奖]]的暖场秀<ref name="Caramanica 2008-11-07" />。

专辑的主打单曲《[[爱情故事|爱情故事]]》于2008年9月发行，成为史上销量第二的乡村单曲，在[[公告牌百强单曲榜|公告牌百强单曲榜]]的排位最高时达到第四位<ref>{{cite web |url={{BillboardURLbyName |artist=taylor swift |chart=all}}|title=Love Story – Taylor Swift|work=Billboard|accessdate=2011-03-05}}</ref>。另外四首于2008年和2009年全年发布的单曲为《{{le|白马 (斯威夫特歌曲)|White Horse (Taylor Swift song)|白马}}》、《[[与我同在_(歌曲)|与我同在]]》、《[[十五岁|十五岁]]》和《[[放手去爱_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|放手去爱]]》。《与我同在》是专辑在榜单上排位最高的单曲，在百强单曲榜的最高排位达到第二位<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/267724/black-eyed-peas-jason-mraz-tie-records-on-billboard-hot-100 |title=Black Eyed Peas, Jason Mraz Tie Records on Billboard Hot 100 |last=Ben-Yehuda |first=Ayala |date=2009-08-13 |work=Billboard |accessdate=2010-03-13 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130508183109/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/267724/black-eyed-peas-jason-mraz-tie-records-on-billboard-hot-100 |archivedate=2013-05-08 }}</ref>。专辑以榜首成绩首次亮相[[公告牌二百强专辑榜|公告牌二百强专辑榜]]，销量达到592304张，全球销量已达到860万张<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0,,GAC_26063_5939337,00.html |title=Taylor Swift's Fearless Makes History With No 1 Debut on Billboard's Top 200 All-Genre Album Sales Chart |date=2008-11-20 |publisher=TOP 40 Charts |accessdate=2008-12-24 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090606122348/http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0%2C%2CGAC_26063_5939337%2C00.html |archivedate=2009-06-06 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>，成为2009年销量最高的专辑，给泰勒絲带来了众多{{le|Crossover_(music)#Crossover_country|跨界 (音乐)|跨界成功}}<ref>{{cite web |url=http://new.music.yahoo.com/blogs/chart_watch/74364/chart-watch-extra-20-years-of-top-albums/ |title=Chart Watch Extra: 20 Years Of Top Albums |first=Paul |last=Grein |date=2011-05-12 |publisher=Yahoo! Music |accessdate=2011-06-10 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110623063535/http://new.music.yahoo.com/blogs/chart_watch/74364/chart-watch-extra-20-years-of-top-albums |archivedate=2011-06-23 }}</ref>。

[[File:FearlessPrudentialCentMay2010.jpg|thumb]][[新泽西州|新泽西州]]站上演出，摄于2010年]]
泰勒絲开展了首次由她领衔的巡演，以宣传《无惧的爱》。105场[[無懼的愛巡迴演唱會|无惧的爱巡回演唱会]]在北美、欧洲、澳大利亚和亚洲举办<ref>{{cite web |last=Herrera |first=Monica |title=Taylor Swift Announces Second Leg Of 'Fearless' Tour |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/267140/taylor-swift-announces-second-leg-of-fearless-tour |work=Billboard |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2009-10-08}}</ref>。泰勒絲力邀[[约翰·梅尔|约翰·梅尔]]、[[凱蒂·佩芮|凯蒂·佩芮]]在北美演出的不同场次跟她作一次过的二重唱，而客串歌星还包括[[贾斯汀·比伯|小贾斯汀]]<ref>{{cite news |title=Taylor Swift FEARLESS TOUR 2010 |publisher=Ticketek |url=http://premier.ticketek.com.au/shows/show.aspx?sh=TAYLORSW10&searchId=464a7869-8d63-4190-a249-e63b830df60d |accessdate=2010-01-08 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140908122756/http://premier.ticketek.com.au/shows/show.aspx?sh=TAYLORSW10&searchId=464a7869-8d63-4190-a249-e63b830df60d |archivedate=2014-09-08 }}</ref>。有110万歌迷观看了巡演，票房收入超过6300万美元<ref>{{cite web |last=Mapes |first=Jillian |title=Taylor Swift Announces 'Speak Now' World Tour |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/photos/live/950374/taylor-swift-announces-speak-now-world-tour |work=Billboard |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2010-11-23 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130508182314/http://www.billboard.com/articles/photos/live/950374/taylor-swift-announces-speak-now-world-tour |archivedate=2013-05-08 }}</ref>。演唱会电影《{{le|泰勒·斯威夫特：无惧的爱之旅|Taylor Swift: Journey to Fearless}}》于电视播出，随后还发行了[[DVD|DVD]]和[[蓝光|蓝光]]<ref>{{cite web |url=http://press.discovery.com/us/hub/programs/taylor-swifts-journey-fearless |title=Taylor Swift's Journey to Fearless : Programs : The Hub : Discovery Press Web |publisher=Press.discovery.com |accessdate=2011-10-10 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111003000917/http://press.discovery.com/us/hub/programs/taylor-swifts-journey-fearless/ |archivedate=2011-10-03 }}</ref>。泰勒也在[[凯斯·艾尔本|凯斯·厄本]]的“一起逃跑世界巡演”（{{lang|en|Escape Together World Tour}}）中担任嘉宾<ref>{{cite web |title=Keith Urban Tours With Taylor Swift, Sugarland + More |url=http://www.theboot.com/2008/12/02/keith-urban-tours-with-taylor-swift-sugarland-more/ |work=The Boot |accessdate=2012-05-15 |author=Stephen L. Betts |date=2008-12-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20100901035639/http://www.theboot.com/2008/12/02/keith-urban-tours-with-taylor-swift-sugarland-more |archivedate=2010-09-01 }}</ref>。

除了巡演，这位歌手还在电视表演中表达对各位同行歌手的敬意。她在《CMT巨人：阿兰·杰克逊》（{{lang|en|''CMT Giants: Alan Jackson''}}）节目中翻唱了阿兰·杰克逊的《Drive》，参与了摇滚乐队[[威豹乐队|威豹乐队]]在纳什维尔的联合电视演唱会，在授予斯特拉特年代艺术家称号的ACM电视节目中翻唱了斯特拉特的《Run》<ref>{{cite news |last=Gerome |first=John |url=http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2009-04-07-strait-decade_N.htm |title=Stars salute Strait as ACM's Artist of the Decade |work=USA Today |date=2009-04-07 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090416034619/http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2009-04-07-strait-decade_N.htm |archivedate=2009-04-16 }}</ref>。泰勒絲和[[麦莉·赛勒斯|麦莉·希拉]]在[[第51届格莱美奖|第51届格莱美奖]]上共同演唱她的歌曲《十五岁》，并与[[T-Pain|T-Pain]]在CMT大奖上即兴饶舌<ref>{{cite web |author=Daniel Kreps |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-raps-with-t-pain-rocks-with-def-leppard-at-cmts-20090617 |title=Taylor Swift Raps With T-Pain, Rocks With Def Leppard at CMTs |work=Rolling Stone |date=2009-06-17 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120805041840/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-raps-with-t-pain-rocks-with-def-leppard-at-cmts-20090617 |archivedate=2012-08-05 }}</ref>。

泰勒絲还录制了一些周边歌曲。2009年，她透过[[Rhapsody|Rhapsody]]发布了[[汤姆·佩蒂|汤姆·佩蒂]]歌曲《{{le|美国女孩|American Girl (Tom Petty song)}}》的翻唱版<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0,3034,gac_26063_5944409_,00.html |title=News : Headlines : Tim McGraw, Taylor Swift: New Songs Coming |publisher=Gactv.com |date=2009-06-29 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090702041753/http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0%2C3034%2CGAC_26063_5944409_%2C00.html |archivedate=2009-07-02 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>，并有幸与佩蒂共同录制歌曲直至2013年<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2011-06-09-taylor-swift-lyrics-on-arm_n.htm |title=Taylor Swift arms herself with lyrics onstage |work=USA Today |accessdate=2012-09-14 |date=2011-06-09 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110808024625/http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2011-06-09-taylor-swift-lyrics-on-arm_n.htm |archivedate=2011-08-08 }}</ref>。她还担任梅尔第四张专辑《{{le|战争研究|Battle Studies (album)}}》歌曲《[[半颗心|半颗心]]》的伴唱<ref>{{cite web |last=Vena |first=Jocelyn |title=John Mayer Talks Taylor Swift Collaboration 'Half of My Heart' |url=http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1625724/john-mayer-talks-taylor-swift-collaboration-half-my-heart.jhtml |publisher=MTV |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2009-11-06 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120414193121/http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1625724/john-mayer-talks-taylor-swift-collaboration-half-my-heart.jhtml |archivedate=2012-04-14 }}</ref>。她还与{{le|凯莉·皮克雷|Kellie Pickler}}共同创作并录制了歌曲《{{le|在你一生中美好日子|Best Days of Your Life}}》<ref>{{cite news |last=Mansfield |first=Brian |title=Carrie Underwood tops Idol downloads; Adam Lambert on the rise |url=http://content.usatoday.com/communities/idolchatter/post/2010/06/carrie-underwood-tops-idol-downloads-adam-lambert-on-the-rise/1 |work=USA Today |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2010-06-23}}</ref>，并分别与{{le|马丁·约翰逊|Martin Johnson}}和{{le|罗伯特·埃利斯·奥拉尔|Robert Ellis Orrall}}共同创作了电影《{{Le|汉娜·蒙塔娜 (电影版)|Hannah Montana: The Movie|汉娜·蒙塔娜}}》中的两首插曲《{{le|找到回家的路|You'll Always Find Your Way Back Home}}》和《{{le|再疯一点|Crazier (Taylor Swift song)}}》<ref name="prod">{{cite web |url=http://www.visualhollywood.com/movies_2009/hanna_montana/notes.pdf |title=Hannah Montana The Movie Production Notes |work=Walt Disney Pictures |publisher=VisualHollywood.com |accessdate=2009-11-03 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/5lNC4Dlzi?url=http://www.visualhollywood.com/movies_2009/hanna_montana/notes.pdf |archivedate=2009-11-18 }}</ref>。泰勒絲还为[[Boys_Like_Girls|男生爱女生]]的歌曲《[[Two_Is_Better_Than_One|两人世界总比单身要强]]》作伴唱，该曲由马丁·约翰逊创作<ref>{{cite web |title=Boys Like Girls Dish on Taylor Swift |url=http://www.seventeen.com/cosmogirl/boys-like-girls-jingle-ball |work=Seventeen |publisher=seventeen.com |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2009-12-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110709210945/http://www.seventeen.com/cosmogirl/boys-like-girls-jingle-ball |archivedate=2011-07-09 }}</ref>。她还为电影《[[情人节快乐|情人节快乐]]》原声带贡献了包括《{{le|今天是个童话|Today Was a Fairytale}}》在内的两首插曲<ref name="slate">{{cite web |url=http://www.slate.com/blogs/blogs/browbeat/archive/2010/01/28/track-of-the-week-taylor-swift-today-was-a-fairytale.aspx |title=Track of the Week: Taylor Swift, "Today Was a Fairytale" |first=Jonah |last=Weiner |author2=Jody Rosen |date=2010-01-28 |work=Slate |accessdate=2010-06-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/6ACC3gZSI?url=http://www.slate.com/content/slate/blogs/browbeat/2010/01/28/track_of_the_week_taylor_swift_today_was_a_fairytale.html |archivedate=2012-08-26 }}</ref>，并为《{{le|把希望送到海地|Hope for Haiti Now}}》翻唱了{{le|泄露天机合唱团|Better Than Ezra}}的歌曲《无力呼吸》（{{lang|en|Breathless}}）<ref>{{cite web |last=Vena |first=Jocelyn |url=http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1630485/better-than-ezra-honored-by-taylor-swifts-breathless-performance.jhtml |title=Better Than Ezra 'Honored' By Taylor Swift's Performance Of 'Breathless' At Haiti Telethon |publisher=MTV |date=2010-01-26 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120209071227/http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1630485/better-than-ezra-honored-by-taylor-swifts-breathless-performance.jhtml |archivedate=2012-02-09 }}</ref>。

[[File:StaplesCenterFearless.jpg|thumb]]
2009年，泰勒絲凭借《与我同行》赢得最受欢迎女歌手音乐录影带奖，成为首个赢得[[MTV音乐录影带大奖|MTV音乐录影带大奖]]的乡村音乐歌手<ref name="msnbc.msn.com">{{cite web |title=Kanye calls Taylor Swift after 'View' appearance |work=Associated Press/MSNBC |date=2009-09-15 |accessdate=2009-09-16 |url=http://www.today.com/id/32861800 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131006213404/http://www.today.com/id/32861800 |archivedate=2013-10-06 }}</ref>。但当她发表获奖感言时，被说唱歌手[[坎耶·韦斯特|坎耶·韦斯特]][[2009年MTV音乐录影带大奖#争议|打断]]。威斯特此前曾涉及多起颁奖典礼事故<ref>{{cite news |title=Sorry, MTV VMA queen Taylor Swift: Kanye West is king of award-show tantrums |url=http://goldderby.latimes.com/awards_goldderby/2009/09/mtv-vma-video-music-awards-kanye-west-taylor-swift-music-news.html |work=Los Angeles Times |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2009-09-13 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120606160004/http://goldderby.latimes.com/awards_goldderby/2009/09/mtv-vma-video-music-awards-kanye-west-taylor-swift-music-news.html |archivedate=2012-06-06 }}</ref>。在活动的新闻发布厅里，泰勒絲表示她是坎耶的歌迷<ref>{{cite web |last=Vena |first=Jocelyn |title=Taylor Swift Talks Acting, College and a Dream Collaboration With 'Amazing' T.I. |url=http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1599659/taylor-swift-talks-acting-college-dream-collaborations.jhtml |publisher=MTV |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2008-11-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120415123516/http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1599659/taylor-swift-talks-acting-college-dream-collaborations.jhtml |archivedate=2012-04-15 }}</ref>，自己跟他没有“任何过节”<ref name="Beyonce1">{{cite web |title=Taylor Swift Thanks "Gracious" Beyonce for Inviting Her Onstage After Kanye Stunt at VMAs |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-thanks-gracious-beyonce-for-inviting-her-onstage-after-kanye-stunt-at-vmas-20090914 |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2009-09-14 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120615184835/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-thanks-gracious-beyonce-for-inviting-her-onstage-after-kanye-stunt-at-vmas-20090914 |archivedate=2012-06-15 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |title=Taylor Swift Speaks Out on Kanye Incident |url=http://www.usmagazine.com/entertainment/news/taylor-swift-2009149 |work=Us Weekly |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2009-09-14 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130429152259/http://www.usmagazine.com/entertainment/news/taylor-swift-2009149 |archivedate=2013-04-29 }}</ref>。事件受到媒体的关注，在[[网络迷因|网上爆红]]<ref>{{cite web |accessdate=2009-10-03 |url=http://newsroom.mtv.com/2009/09/16/kanye-wests-vma-interruption-photos/ |title=Kanye West's VMA Interruption Gives Birth To Internet Photo Meme |publisher=MTV |date=2009-09-16 |author=Anderson, Kyle |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20091001234936/http://newsroom.mtv.com/2009/09/16/kanye-wests-vma-interruption-photos |archivedate=2009-10-01 }}</ref>。几天后，泰勒絲告诉一名记者，威斯特私底下给她道了歉，她接受了：“他很真诚<ref name=msnbc.msn.com />。”在随后的采访中，她拒绝谈论这一事件，以免招致“大麻烦”：“这件事发生在电视上，所以大家都看清楚了事件的原委……我并不认为我们需要谈这些<ref>{{cite web |author=Marianne Horner |url=http://www.theboot.com/2009/09/19/taylor-swift-seeks-clarity-amidst-story-that-just-wont-die/ |title=Taylor Swift Seeks Clarity Amidst Story That Just Won't Die |publisher=The Boot |date=2009-09-19 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20100906130650/http://www.theboot.com/2009/09/19/taylor-swift-seeks-clarity-amidst-story-that-just-wont-die |archivedate=2010-09-06 }}</ref>。”有人表示，这起事件和后续的媒体关注度，让泰勒絲变成“一位真正的友善的主流名人<ref name="montgomery1">{{cite web |last=Montgomery |first=James |title=Why You Shouldn't Hate on Taylor Swift |url=http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1631093/why-shouldnt-hate-on-taylor-swift.jhtml |publisher=MTV |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2010-02-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120103100702/http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1631093/why-shouldnt-hate-on-taylor-swift.jhtml |archivedate=2012-01-03 }}</ref>。”

2010年，泰勒絲在[[第52届格莱美奖|第52屆葛萊美獎]]上收获八项提名，其中有四项夺得大奖<ref>{{cite web |last=Gilbert |first=Calvin |title=Taylor Swift Nets Eight Grammy Nominations |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1627496/taylor-swift-nets-eight-grammy-nominations.jhtml |work=CMT |accessdate=2012-02-13 |date=2009-12-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120125102125/http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1627496/taylor-swift-nets-eight-grammy-nominations.jhtml |archivedate=2012-01-25 }}</ref>。《无惧的爱》被提名为年度专辑和最佳乡村专辑，而《白马》则被提名为最佳乡村歌曲和最佳乡村女歌手<ref>{{cite web |last=Kreps |first=Daniel |title=Beyonce, Taylor Swift Dominate 2010 Grammy Awards |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/beyonce-taylor-swift-dominate-2010-grammy-awards-20100201 |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2012-02-13 |date=2010-02-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120215201914/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/beyonce-taylor-swift-dominate-2010-grammy-awards-20100201 |archivedate=2012-02-15 }}</ref>。她也因此成为赢得年度专辑奖的最年轻女艺人<ref name="NYTgrammy">{{cite news |last=Caramanica |first=Jon |title=For Young Superstar Taylor Swift, Big Wins Mean Innocence Lost |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2010/02/02/arts/music/02taylor.html |work=The New York Times |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2010-02-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120828162727/http://www.nytimes.com/2010/02/02/arts/music/02taylor.html |archivedate=2012-08-28 }}</ref>，《天生一對》也入圍了年度製作及年度歌曲，也替泰勒絲入圍了最佳流行女歌手，《呼吸》替泰勒絲及[[蔻比·凱蕾|寇比·凱雷]]入圍了最佳流行對唱）英語：Best Pop Collaboration with Vocals）。

2010年格莱美奖颁奖典礼期间，泰勒絲与[[史蒂薇·尼克斯|史蒂薇·尼克斯]]共同演唱《与我同在》和《{{le|雷亚农|Rhiannon}}》。但泰勒絲的声乐表现遭到恶评，并引发众多媒体的强烈反响<ref name="montgomery1" /><ref>{{cite web |last=Kreps |first=Daniel |title=Taylor Swift's Label Lashes Out at Critics of Grammy Performance |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swifts-label-lashes-out-at-critics-of-grammy-performance-20100204 |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2010-02-04 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130119163829/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swifts-label-lashes-out-at-critics-of-grammy-performance-20100204 |archivedate=2013-01-19 }}</ref>。她的唱功被不同程度地描述为“严重走音”、“惊人的糟糕”和“难以置信的猥琐”<ref name="EWduet">{{cite web |last=Collis |first=Clark |title=Taylor Swift and Stevie Nicks' Grammys duet: Out of sight, or out of tune? |url=http://music-mix.ew.com/2010/01/31/tayor-swift-and-stevie-nicks-grammys-duet-out-of-sight-or-out-of-tune/ |work=Entertainment Weekly |accessdate=2012-04-22 |date=2010-01-31 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120427143543/http://music-mix.ew.com/2010/01/31/tayor-swift-and-stevie-nicks-grammys-duet-out-of-sight-or-out-of-tune/ |archivedate=2012-04-27 }}</ref><ref name="thebootgrammy">{{cite web |last=Thompson |first=Gayle |title=Taylor Swift & Stevie Nicks' Grammy Performance Invites Critics, Defenders |url=http://www.theboot.com/2010/02/02/taylor-swifts-grammy-performance/ |work=The Boot |accessdate=2012-04-22 |date=2010-02-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120923015124/http://www.theboot.com/2010/02/02/taylor-swifts-grammy-performance |archivedate=2012-09-23 }}</ref>。虽然《纽约时报》的卡拉马尼卡认为“看到这么有天赋的一个人突然让人大跌眼镜很新鲜”，表示泰勒絲“是过去几年中最重要的新晋流行歌手<ref name="NYTgrammy" />。”乐评人{{le|鲍勃·雷夫塞特玆|Bob Lefsetz}}预言她的职业生涯将在“一夜之间”玩完。他认为“泰勒絲还很年轻，愚蠢得还没有意识到她犯下错误”，并公开呼吁泰勒的父亲聘请“危机宣传代理人”来处理这事。《时代》杂志专栏作者[[史蒂薇·尼克斯|史蒂薇·尼克斯]]则为这位歌手辩护<ref>{{cite web |url=http://lefsetz.com/wordpress/index.php/archives/2010/02/01/grammys/ |title=Lefsetz Letter " Blog Archive " Grammys |publisher=Lefsetz.com |date=2010-02-01 |accessdate=2012-05-21}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://lefsetz.com/wordpress/index.php/archives/2010/02/04/saving-taylor-swift/ |title=Lefsetz Letter " Blog Archive " Saving Taylor Swift |publisher=Lefsetz.com |date=2011-03-22 |accessdate=2012-07-30}}</ref>：

{{quote|泰勒絲的决心和孩子般的天性让我想起我自己。这是一种非常特别、非常罕见的纯真。这位女孩写的歌让全世界为之唱和，就像尼尔·戴蒙德（{{lang|en|Neil Diamond}}）和[[艾爾頓·強|-{zh-tw:艾爾頓·強;zh-cn:艾尔顿·约翰;zh-hk:艾爾頓·約翰;}-]]那样……这位女性摇滚-乡村-流行乐创作型歌手回来了，她的名字叫泰勒絲。真正拯救音乐界的便是这样的女人<ref name="nicks1">{{cite news |last=Nicks |first=Stevie |title=The 2010 TIME 100 – Taylor Swift |url=http://www.time.com/time/specials/packages/article/0,28804,1984685_1984940_1985536,00.html |work=Time |accessdate=2012-04-22 |date=2010-04-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120421164010/http://www.time.com/time/specials/packages/article/0,28804,1984685_1984940_1985536,00.html |archivedate=2012-04-21 }}</ref>。}}

《无惧的爱》获得众多奖项，成为乡村音乐史上获奖最多的专辑<ref>{{cite web |last=Schneider |first=Marc |title=Taylor Swift Named Billboard Woman of the Year |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/466285/taylor-swift-named-billboard-woman-of-the-year |work=Billboard |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2011-10-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130209044825/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/466285/taylor-swift-named-billboard-woman-of-the-year |archivedate=2013-02-09 }}</ref>。泰勒絲成为了被乡村音乐协会提名为年度最佳艺人的最年轻艺人，是被提名该奖的六名女艺人之一<ref name="CMA2009">{{cite news |url=http://www.foxnews.com/entertainment/2009/11/11/taylor-swift-wins-cma-entertainer-year/ |title=Taylor Swift Wins CMA Entertainer of the Year |publisher=Fox News Channel |accessdate=2010-04-17 |date=2009-11-11 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20100323025859/http://www.foxnews.com/entertainment/2009/11/11/taylor-swift-wins-cma-entertainer-year/ |archivedate=2010-03-23 }}</ref>。《无惧的爱》也赢得了协会的年度专辑奖及最佳鄉村專輯<ref name="CMA2009" />。泰勒絲也是赢得乡村音乐学院年度专辑奖的最年轻艺人<ref>{{cite web|url=http://sev.prnewswire.com/music/20090406/CL9518106042009-1.html |title=Taylor Swift Wins Album of the Year at Academy of Country Music Awards |date=2009-04-06 |publisher=Big Machine Press Release |accessdate=2009-04-07 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090416165833/http://sev.prnewswire.com/music/20090406/CL9518106042009-1.html |archivedate=2009-04-16 }}</ref>。[[全美音樂獎|全美音乐奖]]授予泰勒絲年度艺人奖和最受欢迎乡村专辑奖<ref>{{cite web|last=Ditzian|first=Eric|title=Taylor Swift, Michael Jackson Big Winners at American Music Awards|url=http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1626845/taylor-swift-michael-jackson-big-winners-at-american-music-awards.jhtml|publisher=MTV|accessdate=2012-05-15|year=2009|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120630181520/http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1626845/taylor-swift-michael-jackson-big-winners-at-american-music-awards.jhtml|archivedate=2012-06-30}}</ref>。她还被{{le|詞曲作家名人堂|Songwriters Hall of Fame}}授予{{le|哈尔·大卫|Hal David}}星光奖<ref>{{vcite web|title=Taylor Swift Will Receive Hal David Starlight Award for Songwriting|url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1638866/taylor-swift-will-receive-hal-david-starlight-award-for-songwriting.jhtml|publisher=CMT|accessdate=2012-05-15|date=2010-05-11|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113174721/http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1638866/taylor-swift-will-receive-hal-david-starlight-award-for-songwriting.jhtml|archivedate=2012-11-13}}</ref>，被纳什维尔词曲作家协会提名为年度词曲作家/艺人<ref>{{vcite web|last=Richards|first=Kevin|title=Taylor Swift, Toby Keith, and Wynn Varble Win Big at NSAI Awards|url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2009/10/taylor-swift-toby-keith-and-wynn-varble-win-big-at-nsai-awards/|accessdate=2012-05-15|date=2009-10-19|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120320091151/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2009/10/taylor-swift-toby-keith-and-wynn-varble-win-big-at-nsai-awards/|archivedate=2012-03-20}}</ref>。《[[公告牌|公告牌]]》杂志提名她为2009年的年度艺人<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/266432/2009-artists-of-the-year|title=2009 Artists of the Year|work=Billboard|date=2009-12-20|accessdate=2012-05-21|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/5mW9hgHyq?url=http://www.billboard.com/|archivedate=2010-01-04}}</ref>。泰勒絲在2010年入选《时代》杂志100大最具影响力人士榜单<ref name=autogenerated4>{{cite news|last=Nicks|first=Stevie|title=The 2010 TIME 100 – Taylor Swift|url=http://www.time.com/time/specials/packages/article/0,28804,1984685_1984940_1985536,00.html|work=Time|accessdate=2012-04-22|date=2010-04-29|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120421164010/http://www.time.com/time/specials/packages/article/0,28804,1984685_1984940_1985536,00.html|archivedate=2012-04-21}}</ref>。

=== 2010年－2012年：《[[爱的告白|爱的告白]]》 ===
泰勒絲于2010年10月25日发行了她的第三张录音室专辑《[[爱的告白|爱的告白]]》。她创作了全部14首歌曲，与长期合作者查普曼共同制作专辑<ref name="NYT">{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2010/10/24/arts/music/24swift.html?_r=1 |title=Taylor Swift, Angry on 'Speak Now' – ''The New York Times'' |last=Caramanica |first=Jon |work=The New York Times |date=2010-10-20 |accessdate=2010-10-23 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130522005907/http://www.nytimes.com/2010/10/24/arts/music/24swift.html?_r=1 |archivedate=2013-05-22 }}</ref>。在音乐上，据称专辑让“乡村流行乐领域向另类摇滚和肮脏泡泡糖流行乐扩张<ref name="LAT">{{cite news |url=http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/music_blog/2010/10/album-review-taylor-swifts-speak-now.html |title=Album review: Taylor Swift's 'Speak Now' |last=Powers |first=Ann |work=Los Angeles Times |date=2010-10-25 |accessdate=2010-10-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20101028003032/http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/music_blog/2010/10/album-review-taylor-swifts-speak-now.html |archivedate=2010-10-28 }}</ref>。

《纽约时报》的卡拉马尼卡称专辑有野心，音乐上多元化，“非常的优秀，可能是她最好的一次<ref name="NYT" />。”《乡村之声》的希恩·韦伯（{{lang|en|Theon Weber}}）表示，这张专辑需要“泰勒絲的才能不带忏悔的真正升级，但戏剧性的是：跟她的乡村乐词曲作者的前辈同行一样，她所塑造的人物和环境有些源于生活，她能找到有效的方法来描述他们<ref name="Voice">{{cite web |url=http://www.villagevoice.com/2010-11-03/music/the-iceberg-songs-of-taylor-swift/ |title=The Iceberg Songs of Taylor Swift |last=Weber |first=Theon |work=The Village Voice |date=2010-11-03 |accessdate=2010-11-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120707060458/http://www.villagevoice.com/2010-11-03/music/the-iceberg-songs-of-taylor-swift/ |archivedate=2012-07-07 }}</ref>。“克里斯瓜乌（{{lang|en|Christgau}}）认为专辑的歌曲“过长且冗杂”，但表示“它们所显露的一种努力承载着应受关注的显著的相似之处——也就是说，要关注最好的、最广泛的和最富情感的涵义<ref name="RobertChristgau" />。”《滚石》杂志的{{le|罗伯·谢菲尔德|Rob Sheffield}}称泰勒絲是“流行、摇滚或乡村音乐界”最优秀的词曲作家之一：“泰勒絲或许是一位聪颖的纳什维尔人，她洞悉所有的热单炮制招式，但她也是一个高度紧张、超级浪漫的女孩，有着艾卡法拉亚盆地那样大的夸张连胜纪录<ref name="RS">{{cite web |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/reviews/album/45342/225745 |title=Speak Now by Taylor Swift |last=Sheffield |first=Rob |work=Rolling Stone |date=2010-10-26 |accessdate=2010-10-26 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20101202061419/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/reviews/album/45342/225745 |archivedate=2010-12-02 }}</ref>。”

专辑发行前夕，泰勒絲开展了广泛的宣传活动<ref>{{cite news |last=Sisario |first=Ben |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2010/11/04/arts/music/04country.html?_r=1 |title=Taylor Swift Album Is a Sales Triumph |work=The New York Times |date=2010-11-03 |accessdate=2012-05-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130522010243/http://www.nytimes.com/2010/11/04/arts/music/04country.html?_r=1 |archivedate=2013-05-22 }}</ref>。她出席了各档谈话节目和日渐节目，并在不同寻常的地点举办免费的迷你演唱会，包括[[好莱坞大道|好莱坞大道]]上行驶着的开放式双层巴士和[[约翰·肯尼迪国际机场|约翰·肯尼迪国际机场]]的候机室<ref>{{cite web|url=http://voices.yahoo.com/taylor-swifts-speak-now-moves-back-7466108.html?cat=33 |title=Taylor Swift's '˜Speak Now' Moves Back to Number One on Billboard's Hot 200, Finishes Third for Year |publisher=Yahoo! Voices |date=2010-10-25 |accessdate=2012-05-10 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121011113137/http://voices.yahoo.com/taylor-swifts-speak-now-moves-back-7466108.html?cat=33 |archivedate=2012-10-11 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。她与[[克里斯·克里斯托佛森|克里斯·克里斯托佛森]]、[[愛美蘿·哈里斯|愛美蘿·哈里斯]]、{{le|文斯·吉尔|Vince Gill}}和[[莱昂纳尔·里奇|莱昂纳尔·里奇]]参加了洛杉矶{{le|诺基亚俱乐部|Club Nokia}}的即兴吉他弹唱活动。音乐家们同台轮流介绍并不插电演唱他们的歌曲，为[[乡村音乐名人堂博物馆|乡村音乐名人堂博物馆]]筹集资金<ref>{{cite news |last=Lewis |first=Randy |title=Taylor Swift joins Kris Kristofferson, Vince Gill, Lionel Richie and Emmylou Harris at Country Hall of Fame benefit |url=http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/music_blog/2010/09/taylor-swift-kristofferson-country-hall-fame.html |work=Los Angeles Times |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2010-09-14 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130807034807/http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/music_blog/2010/09/taylor-swift-kristofferson-country-hall-fame.html |archivedate=2013-08-07 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |last=Willman |first=Chris |title=Taylor Swift, Kris Kristofferson Bond at Country Music Hall of Fame Fundraiser |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/1644142/emmylou-harris-kris-kristofferson-taylor-swift-slated-for-hall-of-fame-fundraiser |publisher=CMT |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2010-07-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150713233604/http://www.cmt.com/news/1644142/emmylou-harris-kris-kristofferson-taylor-swift-slated-for-hall-of-fame-fundraiser/ |archivedate=2015-07-13 }}</ref>。

专辑的首支单曲《[[我的最爱_(歌曲)|我的最爱]]》于2010年8月发行，另外五首于2010年和2011年全年发布的单曲为《[[重回十二月|重回十二月]]》、《[[太刻薄|太刻薄]]》、《[[我们的故事_(歌曲)|我们的故事]]》、《[[火花飞舞|火花飞舞]]》和《{{le|有你有我|Ours (song)}}》<ref name="leak">{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1645091/taylor-swifts-new-single-mine-shipped-to-country-radio-after-leak.jhtml |title=Taylor Swift's New Single, "Mine," Shipped to Country Radio After Leak |date=2010-08-04 |publisher=Country Music Television |accessdate=2010-08-04 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20100817005252/http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1645091/taylor-swifts-new-single-mine-shipped-to-country-radio-after-leak.jhtml |archivedate=2010-08-17 }}</ref>。专辑在商业上获得重大成功，以榜首位置首次杀入[[公告牌二百强专辑榜|公告牌二百强专辑榜]]。发行首日销量为104.7万张，使得专辑成为美国历史上第16张单周卖出100万张的专辑<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.yahoo.com/music/bp/week-ending-dec-4-2011-songs-katy-goes-020228383.html |publisher=Yahoo! Music |title=Week Ending May 29, 2011. Albums: Gaga Goes On Sale |first1=Paul |last1=Grein |date=2011-12-04 |accessdate=2011-12-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141209082053/https://www.yahoo.com/music/bp/week-ending-dec-4-2011-songs-katy-goes-020228383.html |archivedate=2014年12月9日 }}</ref>。截至2012年2月，专辑已在全球售出超过570万份<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.pressparty.com/pg/newsdesk/taylorswift/view/32602/ |title=Taylor Swift to Release SPEAK NOW WORLD TOUR – LIVE, Concert CD/DVD & CD/Blu-Ray Set, on November 21st |publisher=Pressparty |date=2011-09-21 |accessdate=2012-03-19 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120824225023/http://www.pressparty.com/pg/newsdesk/taylorswift/view/32602/ |archivedate=2012-08-24 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://blog.gactv.com/blog/2011/09/20/taylor-swift-celebrates-nashville-homecoming/ |title=Taylor Swift Celebrates Nashville Homecoming |first=Sarah |last=Wyland |date=2011-09-20 |work=Great American Country |publisher=Scripps Networks Interactive |accessdate=2011-09-23 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20151104105419/http://blog.gactv.com/blog/2011/09/20/taylor-swift-celebrates-nashville-homecoming/ |archivedate=2015-11-04 }}</ref>。

[[File:Taylor_Swift_2011crop.jpg|thumb]][[新泽西州|新泽西州]][[紐華克_(紐澤西州)|纽瓦克]]站上表演，摄于2011年]]
泰勒絲在2011年全年和2012年初举办巡演宣传专辑。111场[[爱的告白世界巡回演唱会|世界巡演]]于北美、亚洲、欧洲、澳大利亚和新西兰举办<ref name="billboard1">{{cite web |last=Allen |first=Bob |url=http://www.billboard.biz/bbbiz/industry/touring/hot-tours-taylor-swift-george-strait-cirque-1006619952.story |title=Hot Tours: Taylor Swift, George Strait, Cirque Du Soleil |work=Billboard |date=2012-03-29 |accessdate=2012-05-10 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120510170736/http://www.billboard.biz/bbbiz/industry/touring/hot-tours-taylor-swift-george-strait-cirque-1006619952.story |archivedate=2012-05-10 }}</ref>。泰勒在北美巡演期间，力邀众多艺术家与她作一次过的二重唱。登台明星包括[[贾斯汀·比伯|小賈斯汀]]、[[提姆·麥克羅|提姆·麥格劳]]、[[詹姆斯·泰勒|詹姆斯·泰勒]]、[[杰森·玛耶兹|杰森·玛耶兹]]、{{le|肖恩·科尔文|Shawn Colvin}}、{{le|约翰·热兹尼克|John Rzeznik}}、{{le|安迪·格拉默|Andy Grammer}}、[[赛琳娜·戈麦斯|赛琳娜·戈麦斯]]、{{le|塔尔·巴赫曼|Tal Bachman}}、[[妮琪·米娜|妮琪·米娜]]、[[耐利|耐利]]、[[B.o.B|B.o.B]]、[[亚瑟小子|亚瑟小子]]、[[佛罗·里达|佛罗·里达]]、[[T.I.|T.I.]]、{{le|乔恩·福尔曼|Jon Foreman}}、{{le|吉米·阿德金斯|Jim Adkins}}、[[海莉·威廉斯|海莉·威廉斯]]、{{le|热情型男|Hot Chelle Rae}}、{{le|罗尼·邓恩|Ronnie Dunn}}、{{le|达柳斯·洛克|Darius Rucker}}和肯尼·薛士尼<ref>{{cite web |last=Glazer |first=Eliot |title=Watch Taylor Swift Duet With Shawn Colvin |url=http://www.vulture.com/2011/10/taylor_swift_shawn_colvin.html |work=New York |publisher=vulture.com |accessdate=2012-04-22 |date=2011-10-31 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120302051048/http://www.vulture.com/2011/10/taylor_swift_shawn_colvin.html |archivedate=2012-03-02 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |last=Roland |first=Tom |title=Taylor Swift: Billboard's Woman of the Year |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |work=Billboard |accessdate=2012-04-22 |date=2011-12-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130203232452/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |archivedate=2013-02-03 }}</ref>。在北美巡演站期间，每一场表演泰勒絲都会在左臂上写下不同的歌词，表示应该被当成夜间的“情绪戒指”<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2011-06-09-taylor-swift-lyrics-on-arm_n.htm |title=Taylor Swift arms herself with lyrics onstage |author=Brian Mansfield |work=USA Today |date=2011-06-09 |accessdate=2012-06-06 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110808024625/http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2011-06-09-taylor-swift-lyrics-on-arm_n.htm |archivedate=2011-08-08 }}</ref><ref name="Rolling Stone 2011-08-18">Rolling Stone, August 18, 2011, page 28, Q&A: Taylor Swift by Austin Scaggs</ref>。泰勒絲在北美巡演期间还表演了无数首不插电翻唱歌词。每到一个城市，她都会赞扬当地出生长大的艺术家<ref>{{cite web |last=Perpetua |first=Matthew |title=Videos: Taylor Swift's Coast-to-Coast Cover Songs |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/photos/videos-taylor-swifts-coast-to-coast-cover-songs-20111116 |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2012-05-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120428165347/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/photos/videos-taylor-swifts-coast-to-coast-cover-songs-20111116 |archivedate=2012-04-28 }}</ref>。她表示翻唱歌曲能让她在一场原本精心编排的节目“不那么被动”<ref>{{cite web |last=Roland |first=Tom |title=Taylor Swift: Billboard's Woman of the Year |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |work=Billboard |page=2 |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2011-12-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130203232452/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |archivedate=2013-02-03 }}</ref>。超过160万歌迷观看巡演，票房收入超过1.23亿美元<ref name="billboard1" />。泰勒絲首张现场专辑《{{le|爱的告白世界巡回演唱会：现场版|Speak Now World Tour: Live}}》收录了北美巡演的17场表演，于2011年11月发布<ref>{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift ‘Speak Now World Tour – Live’ CD/DVD Offers Best Seat In The House!|url=http://wycd.cbslocal.com/2011/11/17/taylor-swift-speak-now-world-tour-live-cd-dvd-street-date/|publisher=CBS Local|accessdate=2015-07-13|date=2011-11-17|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150713144515/http://wycd.cbslocal.com/2011/11/17/taylor-swift-speak-now-world-tour-live-cd-dvd-street-date/|archivedate=2015-07-13}}</ref>。

[[File:Taylor_Swift_Sydney.jpg|thumb]][[悉尼|悉尼]]站上表演，摄于2012年]]
在[[第54届格莱美奖|第54届格莱美奖]]颁奖典礼上，泰勒絲的歌曲《[[太刻薄|太刻薄]]》赢得最佳乡村歌曲，這首歌也替泰勒絲獲得最佳乡村歌手<ref name="54th Grammys">{{cite web |last=Wyland |first=Sarah |title=Taylor Swift Takes Home Two GRAMMYs at Tribute-Filled Show |url=http://blog.gactv.com/blog/2012/02/12/taylor-swift-takes-home-two-grammys-at-tribute-filled-show/ |publisher=Great American Country |accessdate=2012-02-13 |date=2012-02-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150906065943/http://blog.gactv.com/blog/2012/02/12/taylor-swift-takes-home-two-grammys-at-tribute-filled-show/ |archivedate=2015-09-06 }}</ref>。她也在典礼上演唱了这首歌曲。对她在2010年格莱美奖上的表演抨击得最为猛烈的雷夫塞特玆认为这首歌是写给他的<ref name="wired1">{{cite news |last=Raftery |first=Brian |url=http://www.wired.com/magazine/2012/02/mf_lefsetz/all/1 |title=Who the Hell Is Bob Lefsetz? |work=Wired |date=2012-02-17 |accessdate=2012-04-22 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120501111154/http://www.wired.com/magazine/2012/02/mf_lefsetz/all/1 |archivedate=2012-05-01 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://lefsetz.com/wordpress/index.php/archives/2012/06/08/sales-3/ |title=Lefsetz Letter " Blog Archive " Sales |publisher=Lefsetz.com |accessdate=2012-07-01}}</ref>，雷夫塞特玆此前很看好这位歌手的职业生涯<ref>{{cite web |url=http://lefsetz.com/wordpress/index.php/archives/2007/08/25/taylor-swifttim-mcgraw/ |title=Lefsetz Letter " Blog Archive " Taylor Swift/Tim McGraw |publisher=Lefsetz.com |date=2007-08-25 |accessdate=2012-04-22 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121114011041/http://lefsetz.com/wordpress/index.php/archives/2007/08/25/taylor-swifttim-mcgraw/ |archivedate=2012-11-14 }}</ref>，而泰勒絲不定期透过电子邮件和电话与雷夫塞特玆交流。《时代》杂志的克莱尔·苏达夫（{{lang|en|Claire Suddath}}）感觉泰勒絲“以复仇之心发表她要开启复出<ref>{{cite news |last=Suddath |first=Claire |title=Taylor Swift, "Mean" | The Best and Worst of the 2012 Grammys |url=http://entertainment.time.com/2012/02/12/the-best-and-worst-of-the-2012-grammys/slide/taylor-swift-mean/#taylor-swift-mean |work=Time |accessdate=2012-04-22 |date=2012-02-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120424081932/http://entertainment.time.com/2012/02/12/the-best-and-worst-of-the-2012-grammys/slide/taylor-swift-mean/#taylor-swift-mean |archivedate=2012-04-24 }}</ref>。而《[[今日美国|今日美国]]》的杰米·蒂尔维斯特（{{lang|en|Jayme Deerwester}}）则指出，2010年的批评似乎“让她成为了「更优秀的词曲作家和现场表演者」<ref>{{cite news |last=Deerwester |first=Jayme |title=Adoration for Adele: 6 Grammys |url=http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/awards/grammys/story/2012-02-12/live-grammys-story-2012/53063460/1 |work=USA Today |accessdate=2012-04-22 |date=2012-02-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120422173737/http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/awards/grammys/story/2012-02-12/live-grammys-story-2012/53063460/1 |archivedate=2012-04-22 }}</ref>。
