专辑也给泰勒絲带来了其他大奖。她于2010年和2011年被纳什维尔词曲作家协会提名为年度词曲作家/艺人<ref>{{cite web |last=Thompson |first=Gayle |url=http://www.theboot.com/2012/04/17/alan-jackson-country-radio/ |title=Alan Jackson Keeps It Country |work=The Boot |date=2012-04-17 |accessdate=2012-04-22 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120419195329/http://www.theboot.com/2012/04/17/alan-jackson-country-radio |archivedate=2012-04-19 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |author=Hazel Smith |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/hot-dish/1672997/hot-dish-taylor-swift-sings-alan-jacksons-masterpiece-at-nashville-songwriters-celebration.jhtml |title=News : HOT DISH: Taylor Swift Sings Alan Jackson's Masterpiece at Nashville Songwriters Celebration |publisher=CMT |date=2011-10-24 |accessdate=2012-04-22 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120315151858/http://www.cmt.com/news/hot-dish/1672997/hot-dish-taylor-swift-sings-alan-jacksons-masterpiece-at-nashville-songwriters-celebration.jhtml |archivedate=2012-03-15 }}</ref>，于2011年和2012年被乡村音乐学院提名为年度艺人<ref>{{cite news |title=Taylor Swift wins ACM entertainer of the year |url=http://news.yahoo.com/taylor-swift-wins-acm-entertainer-025913684.html |agency=Associated Press |publisher=Yahoo! News |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2012-04-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120405095712/http://news.yahoo.com/taylor-swift-wins-acm-entertainer-025913684.html |archivedate=2012-04-05 }}</ref>，被乡村音乐协会提名为2011年年度艺人<ref>{{cite news |title=CMA Awards 2011: Taylor Swift wins entertainer of the year |url=http://www.cbsnews.com/8301-31749_162-57321901-10391698/cma-awards-2011-taylor-swift-wins-entertainer-of-the-year/ |publisher=CBS News |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2011-11-09 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120424083658/http://www.cbsnews.com/8301-31749_162-57321901-10391698/cma-awards-2011-taylor-swift-wins-entertainer-of-the-year |archivedate=2012-04-24 }}</ref>。泰勒絲是2011年[[全美音乐奖|全美音乐奖]]年度艺人，而专辑则被提名为最受欢迎乡村专辑<ref>{{cite news |title=American Music Awards 2011: Taylor Swift wins artist of the year |url=http://www.cbsnews.com/8301-31749_162-57328407-10391698/american-music-awards-2011-taylor-swift-wins-artist-of-the-year/ |publisher=CBS News |accessdate=2012-05-15 |date=2011-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111224122709/http://www.cbsnews.com/8301-31749_162-57328407-10391698/american-music-awards-2011-taylor-swift-wins-artist-of-the-year |archivedate=2011-12-24 }}</ref>。《[[告示牌_(雜誌)|公告牌]]》将泰勒絲提名为2011年年度女性<ref>{{cite web |last=Roland |first=Tom |title=Taylor Swift: Billboard's Woman of the Year |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |work=Billboard |accessdate=2012-05-15 |page=1 |date=2011-12-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130203232452/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |archivedate=2013-02-03 }}</ref>。

尽管泰勒絲在2012年完成了她的第四张专辑，[[坦格活德|坦格活德]]邀请泰勒絲担任特别演出嘉宾，双方共同表演了《{{le|火雨|Fire and Rain}}》、《爱情故事》和《有你有我》<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.berkshireeagle.com/ci_20994725/taylored-please-jt-swift-bring-generations-fans-together |title=Taylored to please: James Taylor and Taylor Swift bring generations of fans together – Berkshire Eagle Online |publisher=Berkshireeagle.com |accessdate=2012-07-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120710100937/http://www.berkshireeagle.com/ci_20994725/taylored-please-jt-swift-bring-generations-fans-together |archivedate=2012-07-10 }}</ref>。在泰勒絲18岁首次与她见面的泰勒絲表示，“我们一拍即合。我喜欢她的歌，她在舞台上的亮相太棒了<ref name="autogenerated3">{{cite news |last=Lane |first=Mary M. |url=http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304050304577375872042368612.html |title=James Taylor Talks About Songwriting, Addiction and His New Friend Taylor Swift |work=The Wall Street Journal |date=2012-05-02 |accessdate=2012-07-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120630090037/http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304050304577375872042368612.html |archivedate=2012-06-30 }}</ref><ref name="post-gazette1">{{cite news |url=http://www.post-gazette.com/stories/ae/music/preview-james-taylor-talks-new-tour-taylor-swift-early-touring-days-641185/ |title=Preview: James Taylor talks new tour, Taylor Swift, early touring days – Pittsburgh Post-Gazette |publisher=Post-gazette.com |date=2012-06-20 |accessdate=2012-07-03 |first=Scott |last=Mervis |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120623203306/http://www.post-gazette.com/stories/ae/music/preview-james-taylor-talks-new-tour-taylor-swift-early-touring-days-641185/ |archivedate=2012-06-23 }}</ref>。”

在此期间，泰勒絲还为电影《[[饥饿游戏_(电影)|饥饿游戏]]》原声带贡献了两首原创歌曲。歌曲《[[安然無恙|安然无恙]]》由{{le|圣战乐团|The Civil Wars}}与{{le|T-本恩·本内特|T Bone Burnett}}共同创作和录制<ref>{{cite web |author=Monica Herrera |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-arcade-fire-talk-hunger-games-20120315 |title=Taylor Swift, Arcade Fire Talk 'Hunger Games' |work=Rolling Stone |date=2012-03-15 |accessdate=2012-05-10 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150627015052/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-arcade-fire-talk-hunger-games-20120315 |archivedate=2015-06-27 }}</ref>。{{le|约翰·保罗·怀特|John Paul White}}与泰勒絲共事是一种“启示……这确实是一次合作<ref>{{cite web |author=Ed Power |url=http://www.hotpress.com/8900799.html?new_layout=1&page_no=2&show_comments=1 |title=Keep It Civil |work=Hot Press |accessdate=2012-05-10 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130522032414/http://www.hotpress.com/8900799.html?new_layout=1&page_no=2&show_comments=1 |archivedate=2013-05-22 }}</ref>。”歌词作为专辑的主打单曲发布，截至2013年1月已在美国售出超过140万张<ref name="deadline.com">{{cite web |url=http://www.deadline.com/2013/01/taylor-swift-safe-and-sound-golden-globe-nominated-hunger-games/ |title=Swift's Poetry Turns into Globe-Nominated Tune |publisher=Deadline.com |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130115193205/http://www.deadline.com/2013/01/taylor-swift-safe-and-sound-golden-globe-nominated-hunger-games/ |archivedate=2013-01-15 }}</ref>。歌曲赢得了[[第55屆葛萊美獎|2013年格莱美奖]]最佳影視媒体歌曲创作奖，在[[第70届金球奖|第70届金球奖]]上被提名为最佳原创歌曲<ref name="Golden Globes">{{cite news |last=Labrecque |first=Jeff |title=Golden Globe nominations: 'Lincoln' leads with 7 nods |url=http://insidemovies.ew.com/2012/12/13/golden-globe-nominations-announced-nbc/ |accessdate=2012-12-13 |date=2012-12-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121214165107/http://insidemovies.ew.com/2012/12/13/golden-globe-nominations-announced-nbc/ |archivedate=2012-12-14 }}</ref>。泰勒絲给专辑贡献的第二首歌曲《{{le|睁开双眼 (歌曲)|Eyes Open (song)|睁开双眼}}》由她独自创作，製作人為她與查普曼<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.roughstock.com/blog/country-chart-news-top-30-digital-singles-the-week-of-april-11-2012 |title=Country Chart News: Top 30 Digital Singles: The Week of April 11, 2012 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120414003829/http://www.roughstock.com/blog/country-chart-news-top-30-digital-singles-the-week-of-april-11-2012 |archivedate=2012年4月14日 }}</ref>。此外，泰勒絲客串及共同創作美國饒舌歌手[[巴比瑞|巴比瑞]]《[[Both_of_Us|我們兩個]]》，该曲由[[卢克博士|卢克博士]]制作，出自巴比瑞的第二张专辑《{{tsl|en|Strange Clouds (album)|奇異雲彩|奇異雲彩}}》<ref>{{cite web |title=B.o.B Explains Origins of Taylor Swift Collaboration "Both of Us" |url=http://www.hiphopdx.com/index/news/id.19471/title.bob-explains-origins-of-taylor-swift-collaboration-both-of-us |publisher=HipHop DX |accessdate=2012-05-15 |author=Steven J. Horowitz |date=2012-04-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120426111603/http://www.hiphopdx.com/index/news/id.19471/title.bob-explains-origins-of-taylor-swift-collaboration-both-of-us |archivedate=2012-04-26 }}</ref>。

=== 2012年－2014年：《[[红_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|紅色]]》 ===
[[File:Swift_performs_in_St._Louis,_Missouri_in_2013.jpg|thumb]][[密苏里州|密苏里州]][[聖路易_(密蘇里州)|圣路易斯]]站上表演，摄于2013年]]
泰勒絲的第四张录音室专辑《[[红_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|紅色]]》于2012年10月22日发布<ref name="yahoo1">{{cite web|last=Willman |first=Chris |url=http://music.yahoo.com/blogs/our-country/scott-borchetta-taylor-tim-martina-band-perry-personalized-005314825.html |title=Scott Borchetta on Taylor, Tim, Martina, the Band Perry ... and the Personalized Machinery of Big Machine |publisher=Yahoo! Music |date=2012-06-13 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121009010116/http://music.aol.com/sessions/taylor-swift-change-sessions/ |archivedate=2012-10-09 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。专辑的16首歌中，有9首由她独自创作，剩下的7首与罗斯、[[马克斯·马丁|马克斯·马丁]]、{{le|丹·威尔逊|Dan Wilson}}、[[艾德·希兰|艾德·希兰]]和{{le|盖瑞·莱特博迪|Gary Lightbody}}共同创作。查普曼担任专辑的领衔制作人，但{{le|杰夫·巴哈斯克|Jeff Bhasker}}、{{le|布奇·沃克|Butch Walker}}、{{le|杰克耐夫·李|Jacknife Lee}}、{{le|丹·霍夫|Dann Huff}}和[[歇尔贝克|歇尔贝克]]亦分别制作曲目。查普曼表示他鼓励泰勒絲“拓展领域，在其他情况下考验她自己”<ref name="usatoday2">{{cite news |url=http://www.usatoday.com/story/life/music/2012/10/17/taylor-swift-red-interview/1637307/ |title=Taylor Swift sees 'Red' all over |work=USA Today |date=2012-10-17 |accessdate=2012-10-23 |first=Brian |last=Mansfield |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121023063529/http://www.usatoday.com/story/life/music/2012/10/17/taylor-swift-red-interview/1637307/ |archivedate=2012-10-23 }}</ref>。音乐上，专辑采用{{le|中心地带摇滚|Heartland rock}}、[[回响贝斯|迴響贝斯]]和[[流行舞曲|流行舞曲]]，“更符合泰勒絲的粉絲们的口味”<ref>{{cite news |author=Alex Macpherson |url=http://www.guardian.co.uk/music/2012/oct/18/taylor-swift-want-believe-pretty-lies |title=Taylor Swift: 'I want to believe in pretty lies' |work=The Guardian |accessdate=2012-10-23 |location=London |date=2012-10-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121023104047/http://www.guardian.co.uk/music/2012/oct/18/taylor-swift-want-believe-pretty-lies |archivedate=2012-10-23 }}</ref><ref name="slantmagazine.com">{{cite web |url=http://www.slantmagazine.com/music/review/taylor-swift-red/2900 |title=Taylor Swift: Red | Music Review |work=Slant Magazine |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130121055529/http://www.slantmagazine.com/music/review/taylor-swift-red/2900 |archivedate=2013-01-21 }}</ref>。
<!-- 檔案不存在 [[File:B25cfea7-f386-42f5-ac59-34c21dd97294|缩略图]] -->
《纽约时报》的卡拉马尼卡认为《紅色》“比她通常的作品要更急就章，缺少细节”<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2012/10/28/arts/music/no-more-kid-stuff-for-taylor-swift.html?_r=0 |title=No More Kid Stuff for Taylor Swift |last=Caramanica |first=Jon |work=The New York Times |date=2012-10-28 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140908124743/http://www.nytimes.com/2012/10/28/arts/music/no-more-kid-stuff-for-taylor-swift.html?_r=0 |archivedate=2014-09-08 }}</ref>，但把它放在个人年终榜单上的第二位，表示泰勒絲的专辑“停下来假装她除了是一名流行巨星外一无是处，这种逐渐扩大的关注度，就像双方彼此交谈，体会专辑怎样才能代表道德沦丧<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2012/12/16/arts/music/jon-caramanicas-top-10-albums-of-2012.html |title=Bright Colors, Grown-Up Concerns and Bruises: Jon Caramanica's Top 10 Albums of 2012 |author=Caramanica, Joe |newspaper=The New York Times |accessdate=2013-02-26 |date=2012-12-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130226022737/http://www.nytimes.com/2012/12/16/arts/music/jon-caramanicas-top-10-albums-of-2012.html |archivedate=2013-02-26 }}</ref>。”《时代》杂志的丽莎·威利科（{{lang|en|Lisa Verrico}}）称赞她的歌词“壮美”，尤其是《[[回忆太清晰|回忆太清晰]]》“引人深思”<ref>{{cite web |title=Pop, Rock & Jazz, Oct 21 |url=http://www.thesundaytimes.co.uk/sto/culture/music/pop_and_rock/article1150472.ece |work=The Sunday Times |accessdate=2013-06-10 |date=2012-10-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131012052203/http://www.thesundaytimes.co.uk/sto/culture/music/pop_and_rock/article1150472.ece |archivedate=2013-10-12 }}</ref>。《滚石》杂志乔恩·多兰欣赏的“看着泰勒絲在大词曲作家山上蹒跚学步。她经常成功地加入[[琼尼·米歇尔|琼妮]]/[[卡罗尔·金|卡罗尔·金]]鲜明的情感对比反映……她的自我发现计划是流行乐坛最优秀的故事之一<ref>{{cite web |last=Dolan |first=Jon |title=Red – Album Reviews |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/red-20121018 |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2013-06-10 |date=2012-10-23 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130605052613/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/red-20121018 |archivedate=2013-06-05 }}</ref>。”

[[File:Taylor_Swift_Red_Tour_2,_2013.jpg|thumb]][[密苏里州|密苏里州]][[圣路易斯|圣路易斯]]站上献唱，摄于2013年3月]]
为了宣传《紅色》，全球72家电台的代表在专辑发行首周飞赴纳什维尔，单独采访泰勒絲<ref name="haruch1">{{cite web |last=Haruch |first=Steve |url=http://www.nashvillescene.com/nashvillecream/archives/2012/10/12/dear-papa-john-taylor-swift-is-psyched-you-can-buy-her-new-album-with-your-pizza |title=Dear (Papa) John: Taylor Swift Is Psyched You Can Buy Her New Album With Your Pizza |publisher=Nashvillescene.com |date=2012-10-21 |accessdate=2012-10-23 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121020070944/http://www.nashvillescene.com/nashvillecream/archives/2012/10/12/dear-papa-john-taylor-swift-is-psyched-you-can-buy-her-new-album-with-your-pizza |archivedate=2012-10-20 }}</ref>。泰勒絲还在众多电视谈话节目中亮相，并在美国、英国、德国、法国、西班牙和澳大利亚的颁奖典礼上表演<ref>{{cite web |last=Bernstein |first=Alyssa |url=http://abcnews.go.com/blogs/headlines/2012/10/all-access-nashville-with-katie-couric-a-special-edition-of-2020-airs-friday-october-26-at-9-pm-et-on-abc/ |title="All Access Nashville with Katie Couric" A Special Edition of "20/20" Airs Friday, October 26 at 9 PM ET on ABC |publisher=ABC News |date=2012-10-16 |accessdate=2012-10-23 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121021230217/http://abcnews.go.com/blogs/headlines/2012/10/all-access-nashville-with-katie-couric-a-special-edition-of-2020-airs-friday-october-26-at-9-pm-et-on-abc/ |archivedate=2012-10-21 }}</ref>。

专辑的主打单曲《[[絕對絕對分定了|絕對絕對分定了]]》使泰勒絲在公告牌百强单曲榜上首次名列第一<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/480315/taylor-swift-scores-first-hot-100-no-1 |title=Taylor Swift Scores First Hot 100 No. 1 |author=Trust, Gary |work=Billboard |date=2012-08-22 |accessdate=2012-08-22 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130213010041/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/480315/taylor-swift-scores-first-hot-100-no-1 |archivedate=2013-02-13 }}</ref><ref name="officialcharts1">{{cite web |url=http://www.officialcharts.com/artist/5387/TAYLOR-SWIFT/ |title=Taylor Swift |publisher=Official Charts Company |date= |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150403022104/http://www.officialcharts.com/artist/5387/TAYLOR-SWIFT/ |archivedate=2015-04-03 }}</ref>。另外六首单曲为《[[重新開始_(泰勒絲歌曲)|重新开始]]》（专供乡村电台）、《[[我知道你是大麻烦|我知道你是大麻烦]]》、《[[二十二岁|二十二岁]]》、《[[都变了|都变了]]》、《[[最後一次_(泰勒絲歌曲)|最后一次]]》（专供流行和国际电台）和《[[红色_(歌曲)|红]]》（专供乡村电台）。《我们再也回不去了》和《我知道你是大麻烦》均为国际热门单曲<ref name="officialcharts1"/>。《紅色》凭借首周121万份的销量以榜首位置首秀公告牌二百强专辑榜，这是近十年来发行首日的最高销量，使得泰勒絲成为首位两张专辑在首发当天卖出一百万张的女性<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/474400/taylor-swifts-red-sells-121-million-biggest-sales-week-for-an-album-since-2002 |title=Taylor Swift's 'Red' Sells 1.21 Million; Biggest Sales Week for an Album Since 2002 |work=Billboard |date=2009-09-14 |accessdate=2012-11-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130201140727/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/474400/taylor-swifts-red-sells-121-million-biggest-sales-week-for-an-album-since-2002 |archivedate=2013-02-01 }}</ref>。截至2013年5月，专辑已在全球卖出超过600万张<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.adelaidenow.com.au/entertainment/music/taylor-swift-to-play-stadiums-on-australian-tour/story-e6freeuu-1226637858626 |title=Taylor Swift to play stadiums on Australian Red tour |last=Adams |first=Cameron |publisher=''The Advertiser'' (Adelaide) |date=2013-05-09 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150710023150/http://www.adelaidenow.com.au/entertainment/music/taylor-swift-to-play-stadiums-on-australian-tour/story-e6freeuu-1226637858626 |archivedate=2015-07-10 }}</ref>。

泰勒絲在北美、新西兰、澳大利亚、欧洲和亚洲举办86场[[红巡回演唱会|红巡回演唱会]]<ref>{{cite web |url=http://theboot.com/taylor-swift-2014-red-tour-dates-asia/ |title=Taylor Swift Announces 2014 Red Tour Dates in Asia |publisher=Theboot.com |date=2014-02-13 |accessdate=2014-04-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140404014306/http://theboot.com/taylor-swift-2014-red-tour-dates-asia/ |archivedate=2014-04-04 }}</ref>。[[紅髮艾德|紅髮艾德]]在北美站上担任表演嘉宾，每晚与泰勒絲演唱《都变了》。泰勒絲力邀的特殊嘉宾有{{le|卡莉·西蒙|Carly Simon}}、[[泰根与莎拉|泰根与莎拉]]、[[詹妮弗·洛佩兹|詹妮弗·洛佩兹]]、[[卢克·布莱恩|卢克·布莱恩]]、[[打倒男孩|打倒男孩]]的[[派崔克·史坦普|派崔克·史坦普]]、[[艾丽·高登|艾丽·高登]]、[[耐利|耐利]]、[[莎拉·芭瑞黎丝|莎拉·芭瑞黎丝]]、[[雪儿·洛薇|雪儿·洛薇]]、B.o.B、莱特博迪、[[追隨者合唱團|追隨者合唱團]]、[[霓虹树乐团|霓虹树乐团]]、弗拉茨、[[亨特·海耶斯|亨特·海耶斯]]、{{le|艾美莉·桑德|Emeli Sandé}}和[[山姆·史密斯_(歌手)|山姆·史密斯]]在巡演的不同场次与她对唱<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.complex.com/music/2013/03/watch-nelly-and-taylor-swift-perform-in-st-louis |title=Watch Nelly and Taylor Swift Perform in St. Louis |publisher=Complex |date=2013-03-21 |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130325092022/http://www.complex.com/music/2013/03/watch-nelly-and-taylor-swift-perform-in-st-louis |archivedate=2013-03-25 }}</ref>。超过170万歌迷出席演唱会，票房收入超过1.5亿美元<ref>{{cite web |first=Bob |last=Allen |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6150193/taylor-swift-red-all-time-country-tour |title=Taylor Swift's Red Wraps as All-Time Country Tour |publisher=Billboard |date=2014-07-03 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150601003002/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6150193/taylor-swift-red-all-time-country-tour |archivedate=2015-06-01 }}</ref>。

[[File:StaplesLA.jpg|thumb]]站上表演，摄于2013年]]
泰勒絲在《紅色》时期还与其他艺术家合作。她与[[杰克·安东诺夫|杰克·安东诺夫]]为电影《{{le|成名机会|One Chance}}》电影原声带共同创作及共同製作歌曲《{{le|比小说更甜美|Sweeter Than Fiction}}》，并获得[[第71届金球奖|第71届金球奖]]最佳原创歌曲提名<ref>{{cite news |author=Baz Bamigboye |url=http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-2406205/Taylor-Swift-pens-song-Paul-Potts-film-charting-Britains-Got-Talent-stars-rise-unlikely-maestro.html |title=Taylor Swift pens song for Paul Potts film charting Britain's Got Talent star's rise to unlikely maestro |work=Daily Mail |accessdate=2013-11-17 |location=London |date=2013-08-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131114083108/http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-2406205/Taylor-Swift-pens-song-Paul-Potts-film-charting-Britains-Got-Talent-stars-rise-unlikely-maestro.html |archivedate=2013-11-14 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |author=Jeff Labrecque |url=http://insidemovies.ew.com/2013/12/12/golden-globe-nominations-2013/ |title='12 Years a Slave' and 'American Hustle' lead Golden Globe nominees |work=Entertainment Weekly |date=2013-12-12 |accessdate=2013-12-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131212144444/http://insidemovies.ew.com/2013/12/12/golden-globe-nominations-2013/ |archivedate=2013-12-12 }}</ref>。她还與[[提姆·麥克羅|提姆·麦克羅]]和吉他[[凯斯·艾尔本|凱斯·艾爾本]]合作歌曲《{{le|公路不关心|Highway Don't Care}}》，此首歌曲入圍了[[第56届格莱美奖|第56屆葛萊美獎]]的最佳鄉村團體/組合，这三个人曾三次现场表演该曲<ref>{{cite web |author=Bonaguro, Alison |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/cmt-offstage/1700782/offstage-tim-mcgraw-wanted-to-make-taylor-swift-duet-an-event.jhtml |title=News : OFFSTAGE: Tim McGraw Wanted to Make Taylor Swift Duet an Event |publisher=CMT |date=2013-01-25 |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130305055555/http://www.cmt.com/news/cmt-offstage/1700782/offstage-tim-mcgraw-wanted-to-make-taylor-swift-duet-an-event.jhtml |archivedate=2013-03-05 }}</ref>。她还与{{le|文斯·吉尔|Vince Gill}}和[[艾莉森·克劳丝|艾莉森·克劳丝]]在2013年乡村音乐协会奖典礼上演唱不插电版的《紅色》<ref>{{cite web |url=http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2013/10/21/taylor-swift-invites-special-guests-to-cma-awards/ |title=Dave Grohl, Jason Mraz join CMA Awards lineup, Taylor Swift to perform with Alison Krauss, Vince Gill & more | Tune in Music City |work=The Tennessean |date=2013-10-21 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131023194809/http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2013/10/21/taylor-swift-invites-special-guests-to-cma-awards/ |archivedate=2013-10-23 }}</ref>。泰勒絲在[[滚石乐队|滚石乐队]]的{{le|50 & Counting|50 & Counting}}巡演芝加哥站上演唱歌曲《{{le|泪流满面|As Tears Go By}}》<ref>{{cite web |author=Doyle, Patrick |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-to-join-the-rolling-stones-onstage-tonight-20130603 |title=Taylor Swift Rolling Stones Chicago | Music News |work=Rolling Stone |date=2013-06-03 |accessdate=2013-06-10 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130608010925/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-to-join-the-rolling-stones-onstage-tonight-20130603 |archivedate=2013-06-08 }}</ref>。她还跟[[佛乔航线|佛乔航线]]在2013年国家广播研讨会上演唱《{{le|导弹 (歌曲)|Cruise (song)|导弹}}》<ref>{{cite web |url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-florida-georgia-line-perform-cruise/ |title=Taylor Swift Joins Florida Georgia Line Onstage for 'Cruise' |work=Taste of Country |date=2013-03-02 |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130316035144/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-florida-georgia-line-perform-cruise/ |archivedate=2013-03-16 }}</ref>。

尽管《紅色》被总共获得三项格莱美奖提名，但未赢得大奖。《絕對絕對分定了》在[[第55届格莱美奖|2013年格莱美奖]]上被提名为年度製作，而《紅色》则在[[第56届格莱美奖|2014年格莱美奖]]上被提名为年度专辑及最佳鄉村專輯，《重新開始》被提名最佳鄉村歌曲。同样，泰勒絲的第四张专辑并未赢得乡村音乐协会年度颁奖典礼的大奖。然而，泰勒絲被协会授予品尼高（{{lang|en|Pinnacle}}）奖，以表彰她所获得的“独一无二”等级的成功，此前加斯·布鲁克是该奖的唯一获奖者。麦格劳、希尔、厄本、弗莱茨、斯特拉特、布拉德·斯派利为泰勒絲颁发该奖，而[[米克·贾格尔|米克·贾格尔]]、西蒙、[[朱莉亚·罗伯茨|朱莉亚·罗伯茨]]、[[瑞茜·威瑟斯彭|瑞茜·威瑟斯彭]]、埃塞尔·肯尼迪和贾斯汀·汀布莱克录制视频祝贺其获奖。《纽约时报》认为该奖旨在讨好“乡村音乐的摇钱树、创作引擎和面向更广阔世界的大使”，以期她能坚守乡村风格<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2013/11/08/arts/music/at-country-music-awards-swift-is-celebrated.html?_r=1& |title=Country Awards Hold Swift Close |last=Caramanica |first=Jon |work=The New York Times |date=2013-11-07 |accessdate=2014-04-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140908122432/http://www.nytimes.com/2013/11/08/arts/music/at-country-music-awards-swift-is-celebrated.html?_r=1& |archivedate=2014-09-08 }}</ref>，然而《纽约人》想知道“这是否意味着泰勒絲和流派引导她告别过去，步向流行乐坛的统治地位<ref>{{cite web |last=Crouch |first=Ian |url=http://www.newyorker.com/online/blogs/culture/2013/11/taylor-swift-country-music-awards.html |title=Lifetime Achievements: Taylor Swift Says Goodbye to Country Music? |work=The New Yorker |accessdate=2014-04-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140225102040/http://www.newyorker.com/online/blogs/culture/2013/11/taylor-swift-country-music-awards.html |archivedate=2014-02-25 }}</ref>。”

泰勒絲在2012年[[MTV欧洲音乐大奖|MTV欧洲音乐大奖]]上赢得三项大奖，包括最佳女歌手和最佳现场表演<ref>{{cite web |last=McGovern |first=Kyle |title=MTV EMAs 2012: Taylor Swift Is Popular in Europe, Too |url=http://www.spin.com/articles/mtv-emas-2012-taylor-swift-justin-bieber-video |work=Spin |accessdate=2013-06-10 |date=2012-11-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130505124642/http://www.spin.com/articles/mtv-emas-2012-taylor-swift-justin-bieber-video/ |archivedate=2013-05-05 }}</ref>。《我知道你是大麻烦》赢得[[2013年MTV音乐录影带大奖|2013年MTV音乐录影带大奖]]年度音樂錄影帶及最佳女歌手音樂录影带奖<ref>{{cite web |url=http://music-mix.ew.com/2013/08/25/vmas-winners-list/ |title=VMAs: The 2013 Winner's List |work=Entertainment Weekly |date=2013-08-25 |accessdate=2013-08-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130826013236/http://music-mix.ew.com/2013/08/25/vmas-winners-list/ |archivedate=2013-08-26 }}</ref>。泰勒絲在2012年全美音乐奖上被提名为最佳女性乡村歌手，在2013年的典礼上被提名为年度艺人<ref>{{cite news |title=Taylor Swift AMA Awards 2012: Pop Star Performs 'I Knew You Were Trouble' (VIDEO) |url=http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2012/11/19/taylor-swift-ama-performa_n_2158758.html |work=The Huffington Post |accessdate=2013-06-10 |date=2012-11-19 |first=Carolyn |last=Gregoire |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130526094239/http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2012/11/19/taylor-swift-ama-performa_n_2158758.html |archivedate=2013-05-26 }}</ref>。纳什维尔词曲作家协会在2012年2013年分别连续第五年和第六年授予泰勒絲词曲作家/艺人奖<ref>{{cite web |last=Hackett |first=Vernell |title=Nashville Songwriters Hall of Fame Adds Mary Chapin Carpenter and More |url=http://www.theboot.com/2012/10/08/nashville-songwriters-hall-of-fame-mary-chapin-carpenter/ |work=The Boot |accessdate=2013-06-10 |date=2012-10-08 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130201073847/http://www.theboot.com/2012/10/08/nashville-songwriters-hall-of-fame-mary-chapin-carpenter/ |archivedate=2013-02-01 }}</ref>。

在《紅色》时期，泰勒絲的情感生活成为媒体的重点关注对象。{{le|高客网|Gawker}}表示泰勒絲已跟“宇宙中的所有男人约过会”<ref>{{cite web|author=12/05/12 6:09pm 12/05/12 6:09pm |url=http://gawker.com/5965470/who-has-taylor-swift-dated-a-brief-history-of-all-the-men-in-the-universe |title=Who Has Taylor Swift Dated: A Brief History of All The Men in the Universe |publisher=Gawker.com |date=2012-11-19 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131117022847/http://gawker.com/5965470/who-has-taylor-swift-dated-a-brief-history-of-all-the-men-in-the-universe |archivedate=2013-11-17 }}</ref>。[[威斯特布路浸信会|威斯特布路浸信会]]抗议泰勒絲开演唱会，称她的“妓女面容注定灭亡的美国”，而Abercrombie & Fitch则顺势销售印有指泰勒絲是“荡妇”标语的T恤<ref>{{cite web |url=http://nymag.com/thecut/2013/06/taylor-swift-slut-shaming-continues.html |title=The Taylor Swift Slut-Shaming Continues – The Cut |work=New York |date=2013-06-28 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131012065948/http://nymag.com/thecut/2013/06/taylor-swift-slut-shaming-continues.html |archivedate=2013-10-12 }}</ref>。《纽约时报》表示，她的“约会史开始轰动世界，感觉像是媒体广泛关注的开端”，并质疑泰勒絲是否处在“23岁人生危机”的夹缝中<ref>{{cite news |last=Chang |first=Bee-Shyuan |title=Taylor Swift Gets Some Mud on Her Boots |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2013/03/17/fashion/for-taylor-swifts-image-erosion-is-a-danger.html?_r=0 |work=The New York Times |accessdate=2013-06-10 |date=2013-03-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130319145352/http://www.nytimes.com/2013/03/17/fashion/for-taylor-swifts-image-erosion-is-a-danger.html?_r=0 |archivedate=2013-03-19 }}</ref>。在2013年的金球奖颁奖典礼上，喜剧女演员[[蒂娜·菲|蒂娜·菲]]和[[艾米·波勒|艾米·波勒]]拿泰勒絲不断约会的名声开玩笑，菲则警告泰勒絲离观众群中的年轻男性“远点”：“她需要一些‘我的’时间来了解自己<ref>{{cite web|first=Natalie |last=Finn |url=http://uk.eonline.com/news/379789/michael-j-fox-taylor-swift-never-ever-needs-to-date-my-son |title=Michael J. Fox: Taylor Swift Never, Ever Needs to Date My Son |publisher=E! Online |date=2013-01-17 |accessdate=2015-04-11}}</ref>。”泰勒絲随后在《[[名利场_(杂志)|名利场]]》的封面故事中质疑这一事件：“我可以笑我自己，但这一事件让每个人跳入了嘲笑‘搞太多约会’的行列中。”在其他文章中记者讨论“金球奖上的女孩一般很刻薄”的问题时，泰勒絲赞许地引述美国前国务卿[[玛德琳·奥尔布赖特|玛德琳·奥尔布赖特]]的一句话：“地狱自然有特殊办法处置那些不帮其他同胞的女人<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.vanityfair.com/hollywood/2013/04/taylor-swift-cover-story |title=Taylor Swift's Telltale Heart |work=Vanity Fair |accessdate=2013-08-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170130205206/http://www.vanityfair.com/hollywood/2013/04/taylor-swift-cover-story |archivedate=2017-01-30 }}</ref>。”而之后收录于第五張專輯《[[1989_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|1989]]》中的《[[空格_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|空格]]》也正是在讽刺媒体和[[蒂娜·菲|蒂娜·菲]]和[[艾米·波勒|艾米·波勒]]对泰勒絲的不断约会的关注。

=== 2014年－2017年：《[[1989_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|1989]]》 ===
[[File:Taylor_Swift_002_(18116992640).jpg|thumb]][[底特律|底特律]]站上表演]]
泰勒絲的第五张录音室专辑《[[1989_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|1989]]》于2014年10月27日发行<ref name="ReferenceA">{{cite web |url=http://www.usatoday.com/story/life/music/2014/08/18/taylor-swift-yahoo-live-stream/14242387/ |title=Taylor Swift debuts 'Shake It Off,' reveals '1989' album |author=Brian Mansfield, USA TODAY |date=2014-08-18 |work=USA Today |accessdate=2014-10-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140819121538/http://www.usatoday.com/story/life/music/2014/08/18/taylor-swift-yahoo-live-stream/14242387/ |archivedate=2014-08-19 }}</ref>。泰勒絲独自创作了其中的一首歌，其余12首与安东诺夫、马丁、歇尔贝克、[[伊莫珍·希普|伊莫珍·希普]]、[[莱恩·泰德|莱恩·泰德]]和阿里·帕亚米（{{lang|en|Ali Payami}}）共同创作<ref>{{cite AV media notes|title=1989|others=Taylor Swift|year=2014|type=Compact disc liner notes|publisher=Big Machine Records|id=BMRBD0500A}}</ref>。泰勒絲和马丁担任执行制作人，而查普曼、安东诺夫、希普、泰德、帕亚米和{{le|格瑞·格克斯汀|Greg Kurstin}}分别创作歌曲<ref>{{cite web |first=Alan |last=Light |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/events/women-in-music-2014/6363514/billboard-woman-of-the-year-taylor-swift-on-writing-her |title=Taylor Swift Cover Story on 1989, Writing Her Own Rules, Going Pop |publisher=Billboard |date=2014-12-05 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150417031350/http://www.billboard.com/articles/events/women-in-music-2014/6363514/billboard-woman-of-the-year-taylor-swift-on-writing-her |archivedate=2015-04-17 }}</ref>。音乐上，专辑被描述为“由代替吉他的合成器和鼓推动<ref name="Sam">{{cite news|author1=Sam Lansky|title=Review: 1989 Marks a Paradigm Swift|url=http://time.com/3533569/taylor-swift-1989-review/|website=TIME|accessdate=2015-01-14|date=2014-10-23|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150113142830/http://time.com/3533569/taylor-swift-1989-review/|archivedate=2015-01-13}}</ref>。”泰勒絲称《1989》是她的首个“正式”流行乐专辑，抛弃了长期樂團中的部分成员<ref name="Re">{{cite web|title=The Reinvention of Taylor Swift|url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/features/taylor-swift-1989-cover-story-20140908?page=2|work=Rolling Stone|accessdate=2015-02-02|date=2014-09-08|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150207074954/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/features/taylor-swift-1989-cover-story-20140908?page=2|archivedate=2015-02-07}}</ref><ref name="Slam" /><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.nashvillegab.com/2014/08/taylor-swifts-new-direction.html |title=Taylor Swift's NEW direction – NashvilleGab – Country music news and Nashville celebrity gossip |accessdate=2014-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141029225733/http://www.nashvillegab.com/2014/08/taylor-swifts-new-direction.html |archivedate=2014-10-29 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-reveals-five-things-to-expect-on-1989-20140916 |title=Taylor Swift Reveals Five Things to Expect on '1989' |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2014-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141128220143/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-reveals-five-things-to-expect-on-1989-20140916 |archivedate=2014-11-28 }}</ref>。

专辑的专业评价普遍积极。《[[滚石_(杂志)|滚石]]》的谢菲尔德表示：“非常怪异，异常兴奋的情绪，疯狂的热情，《1989》听起来的确像泰勒絲，尽管听起来跟她之前所尝试的一点也不像<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/taylor-swift-1989-20141024 |title=Taylor Swift's New Album: 1989 |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2014-10-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141025040444/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/taylor-swift-1989-20141024 |archivedate=2014-10-25 }}</ref>。”《{{le|格兰特地|Grantland}}》的莫莉·兰伯特（{{lang|en|Molly Lambert}}）评论道，“80后专辑《1989》真的就像布鲁斯·斯普林斯廷的《{{le|爱的隧道|Tunnel of Love}}》，指出这位两位艺术家都改变了音乐方向，在公众形象和与长期乐队成员的分道扬镳中作出转变<ref>{{cite web |url=http://grantland.com/hollywood-prospectus/taylor-swift-1989/ |title=It's Hip to Be Swift |work=Grantland |accessdate=2014-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141118033801/http://grantland.com/hollywood-prospectus/taylor-swift-1989/ |archivedate=2014-11-18 }}</ref>。”《卫报》的亚历克西斯·佩特里蒂斯（{{lang|en|Alexis Petridis}}）赞扬专辑的“斯普林斯汀式的逃脱式叙事和60年代女子组合所讨论的浪漫宿命的毁灭……《1989》的原因在于她被授予拒绝给她的同行尊重，这是非常地显而易见的。<ref name="guardianreview">{{cite web|last1=Petridis|first1=Alexis|title=Taylor Swift: 1989 review – leagues ahead of the teen-pop competition|url=http://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/oct/24/taylor-swift-1989-review|website=The Guardian|accessdate=2014-10-24|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141024103411/http://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/oct/24/taylor-swift-1989-review|archivedate=2014-10-24}}</ref>。”在《1989》的宣传活动中，泰勒絲邀请乐迷去到她在纽约、纳什维尔、洛杉矶和罗德岛的家参加秘密专辑试听会“《1989》秘密会议”<ref>{{cite web|author1=Stephanie Anderson|title=Taylor Swift Invited Fans To Her House For A Secret Listening Session|url=http://www.buzzfeed.com/stephanieanderson/taylor-swift-secret-sessions-la#.ef48ywW3J|website=BuzzFeed|publisher=BuzzFeed, Inc|accessdate=2015-01-15|date=2014-09-22|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141129082037/http://www.buzzfeed.com/stephanieanderson/taylor-swift-secret-sessions-la#.ef48ywW3J|archivedate=2014-11-29}}</ref>。她“熟练的”借助各大社交媒体平台邀请行业分析师发表评论<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.vulture.com/2014/10/taylor-swift-queen-of-celebrity-social-media.html |title=Taylor Swift, Queen of Celebrity Social-Media -- Vulture |author=Lindsey Weber |date=2014-10-29 |work=Vulture |accessdate=2014-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141125163328/http://www.vulture.com/2014/10/taylor-swift-queen-of-celebrity-social-media.html |archivedate=2014-11-25 }}</ref>。她还在众多谈话节目中亮相，在美国和英国的颁奖典礼上表演，并担任《[[美国之声|美国之声]]》的选手顾问<ref>{{cite web |last1=Kreps |first1=Daniel |title=Taylor Swift Joins 'The Voice' as Guest Mentor |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-joins-the-voice-as-guest-mentor-20140830 |website=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2014-08-31 |date=2014-08-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150621120754/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-joins-the-voice-as-guest-mentor-20140830 |archivedate=2015-06-21 }}</ref>。
[[File:Taylor_Swift_057_(18117902988).jpg|左]]上表演]]
专辑的主打单曲《[[通通甩掉|通通甩掉]]》于2014年8月发行，在公告牌百强单曲榜中位列榜首，泰勒絲在受訪时谦虚道：＂在公告牌百强单曲榜中位列榜首，只是一件小事，相较玛丽亚．嘉儿和玛丹娜，我真是小巫见大巫＂。《[[空格_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|空格]]》和混音版的《[[壞到底_(歌曲)|敌对]]》分列单曲榜第二位和第四位，均在美国榜上位列榜首。第三支单曲《風格》在美国榜上跻身前十，位列第六。专辑发行首周在美国卖出1287000张，比过去12年来所有专辑的首周销量要多。这让泰勒成为唯一一位有三张专辑在发行首周卖出超过100万张的艺人<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/6304536/official-taylor-swifts-1989-debuts-with-1287-million-sold-in |title=Taylor Swift's "1989" debuts with 1.287 million copies sold |author=Keith Caulfield |publisher="Billboard" |date=2014-11-04 |accessdate=2014-11-04 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141105082854/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/6304536/official-taylor-swifts-1989-debuts-with-1287-million-sold-in |archivedate=2014-11-05 }}</ref>，后来成为了2014年销量最高的专辑，共卖出366万张<ref>{{cite web|last1=Caulfield|first1=Keith|title=Taylor Swift's '1989' Beats 'Frozen' As Top Selling Album of 2014|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/6422411/taylor-swift-1989-beats-frozen-top-selling-album-2014|work=Billboard|accessdate=2015-01-11|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141231215656/https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/6422411/taylor-swift-1989-beats-frozen-top-selling-album-2014|archivedate=2014-12-31}}</ref>。截至2015年2月，专辑在全球卖出超过860万张<ref name="best selling artist 2014 IFPI">{{cite web|url = http://www.ifpi.org/news/Taylor-Swift-named-IFPI-global-recording-artists-of-2014|title = Taylor Swift named IFPI Global Recording Artist of 2014|date = 2015-02-23|accessdate = 2015-02-24|website = |publisher = IFPI|deadurl = no|archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20150618045141/http://www.ifpi.org/news/Taylor-Swift-named-IFPI-global-recording-artists-of-2014|archivedate = 2015-06-18}}</ref>。专辑发售前夕，泰勒絲为《[[华尔街日报|华尔街日报]]》撰写专栏文章，强调专辑目前的重要性<ref name="Mann">{{cite web|author1=Jordan Weissmann|title=Taylor Swift Has Written an Op-Ed in the Wall Street Journal|url=http://www.slate.com/blogs/moneybox/2014/07/07/taylor_swift_in_the_wall_street_journal_the_music_business_can_be_saved.html|website=Slate|publisher=The Slate Group LLC|accessdate=2015-01-23|date=2014-07-07|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150123074145/http://www.slate.com/blogs/moneybox/2014/07/07/taylor_swift_in_the_wall_street_journal_the_music_business_can_be_saved.html|archivedate=2015-01-23}}</ref>。2014年11月，她从[[Spotify|Spotify]]移除她的整个作品目录，认为流媒体公司靠广告支撑的免费服务损害了能给词曲作者提供更高版税的优质服务。然而，她的备份目录仍然可以在其他流媒体服务平台上找到<ref>{{cite web |last=Knopper |first=Steve |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-scott-borchetta-spotify-20141108 |title=Taylor Swift’s Label Head Explains Spotify Removal |work=Rolling Stone |date=2014-11-08 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150421045432/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-scott-borchetta-spotify-20141108 |archivedate=2015-04-21 }}</ref>。2015年6月21日，泰勒絲批评[[苹果公司|苹果公司]]音乐[[流媒体|流媒体]]服务[[Apple_Music|Apple Music]]在流媒体服务三个月试用期期间不给艺术家提供稿费。在一封公开信中，她称该安排“不公平”，表示“Apple Music不会在那个三个月里头付钱给作曲家、制作人或艺术家……请不要让我们（发片艺人）无偿为你们提供我们的音乐”，并表示会将《1989》从目录中撤下<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6605541/taylor-swift-pens-open-letter-explaining-why-1989-wont-be-on-apple-music|title=Taylor Swift Pens Open Letter Explaining Why '1989' Won't Be on Apple Music|last=Peters|first=Mitchell|publisher=Billboard|date=2015-06-21|accessdate=2015-06-22|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150622135521/https://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6605541/taylor-swift-pens-open-letter-explaining-why-1989-wont-be-on-apple-music|archivedate=2015-06-22}}</ref>。翌日，{{le|埃迪·库伊|Eddy Cue}}在[[Twitter|Twitter]]上宣布苹果公司正在改变政策，将在免费试用期期间付钱给艺人<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6605568/apple-changes-course-after-taylor-swift-open-letter-will-pay-labels-during|title=Apple Changes Course After Taylor Swift Open Letter: Will Pay Labels During Free Trial|last=Halperin|first=Shirley|work=Billboard|date=2015-06-21|accessdate=2015-06-22|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150622065723/https://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6605568/apple-changes-course-after-taylor-swift-open-letter-will-pay-labels-during|archivedate=2015-06-22}}</ref>。泰勒絲同样透过Twitter写道，“本周的事件过后，我决定把《1989》放进Apple Music……（我）太开心了”。她总结道她没跟苹果签订独家合同，这是她“在直觉中第一次感觉到流发行我的专辑是正确的<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.ew.com/article/2015/06/25/taylor-swift-1989-apple-music|title=Taylor Swift is putting 1989 on Apple Music|last=Rosen|first=Christopher|work=Entertainment Weekly|date=2015-06-26|accessdate=2015-06-25|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150626164203/http://www.ew.com/article/2015/06/25/taylor-swift-1989-apple-music|archivedate=2015-06-26}}</ref>。”
[[File:Taylor_Swift_NOW_Super_Saturday_Night_IMG_1028_(33291821435).jpg|替代=]]預熱演唱會上表演]]
[[1989世界巡迴演唱會|1989世界巡迴演唱会]]将于2015年5月到12月举行，泰勒絲将在日本、美国、加拿大、英国、爱尔兰、德国、荷兰和澳大利亚...等地方表演<ref>{{cite news|title=Taylor Swift announces details of 1989 world tour|url=http://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/nov/03/taylor-swift-1989-world-tour|accessdate=2015-02-16|work=The Guardian|date=2014-11-03|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150103061139/http://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/nov/03/taylor-swift-1989-world-tour|archivedate=2015-01-03}}</ref>。{{le|海姆|HAIM}}、{{le|万斯·乔伊|Vance Joy}}、[[肖恩·曼德斯|肖恩·曼德斯]]、[[詹姆斯湾|詹姆斯·贝伊]]将在巡演的不同场次担任暖場嘉賓<ref>{{cite web|author1=Mitchell Peters|title=Taylor Swift Announces Haim as '1989' Tour Opener|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6458185/taylor-swift-announces-haim-as-1989-tour-opener?facebook_20150201|work=Billboard|accessdate=2015-02-02|date=2015-02-01|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150318035300/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6458185/taylor-swift-announces-haim-as-1989-tour-opener?facebook_20150201|archivedate=2015-03-18}}</ref>。在《1989》时期，泰勒絲与其他音乐家进行了合作。她与[[保罗·麦卡特尼|保罗·麦卡特尼]]在“{{le|周六夜现场40周年特别节目|Saturday Night Live 40th Anniversary Special}}”的幕后派对上演唱《[[我看见她站在那儿|我看见她站在那儿]]》和《通通甩掉》<ref>{{cite web |last=Bacle |first=Ariana |url=http://www.ew.com/article/2015/02/16/paul-mccartney-jammed-out-taylor-swift-snl-afterparty |title=Paul McCartney jams with Taylor Swift at 'SNL' afterparty |publisher=EW.com |date=2015-02-16 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150328140632/http://www.ew.com/article/2015/02/16/paul-mccartney-jammed-out-taylor-swift-snl-afterparty |archivedate=2015-03-28 }}</ref>，与肯尼·薛士尼在他的{{le|大复兴巡演|Big Revival Tour}}于纳什维尔的首战演出中演唱《{{le|巨星 (肯尼·薛士尼歌曲)|Big Star|巨星}}》<ref>{{cite web |first=Cindy |last=Watts |url=http://www.tennessean.com/story/entertainment/music/2015/03/27/kenny-chesney-tops-taylor-swift-joe-walsh/70530696/ |title=Kenny Chesney tops 12 a.m. with Taylor Swift, Joe Walsh }}</ref>。在{{le|iHeartRadio音乐奖|iHeartRadio Music Awards}}上，她用吉他与[[麦当娜|瑪丹娜]]不插电演唱《[[鬼城_(麦当娜歌曲)|鬼城]]》<ref>{{cite web |last=Sepinwall |first=Alan |url=http://www.hitfix.com/news/watch-taylor-swift-backed-up-madonna-at-the-iheartradio-music-awards |title=Watch: Taylor Swift backed up Madonna at the iHeartRadio Music Awards |publisher=Hitfix.com |date=2015-03-29 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no }}</ref>。泰勒絲被提名为《公告牌》2014年年度女性，是唯一一位两度荣膺该奖的艺人<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6281490/taylor-swift-2014-billboard-woman-of-the-year |title=Taylor Swift: 2014 }}</ref>。同年，她在[[2014年全美音乐奖|全美音乐奖]]上获得迪克·克拉克杰出贡献奖<ref>{{cite web |first=Chris |last=Payne 2014, Presented by Diana Ross |publisher=Billboard |date=2014-11-23 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150704061502/http://www.billboard.com/articles/events/amas-2014/6327564/taylor-swift-win-first-dick-clark-award-of-excellence-amas-2014-diana-ross |archivedate=2015-07-04 }}</ref>。在[[第57届格莱美奖|2015年格莱美奖]]上，《通通甩掉》入圍了年度製作和年度歌曲，這是歌也替泰勒絲入圍了最佳流行歌手<ref>{{cite web |first=Elias |last=Leight |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/events/grammys-2015/6465596/taylor-swift-grammys-red-carpet-on-shake-it-off-history |title=Taylor Swift Talks Nominated 'Shake It Off' on the Grammys Red Carpet }}</ref>。同时在[[2015年全英音乐奖|2015年全英音乐奖]]上，泰勒赢得最佳国际女歌手奖<ref>{{cite web |first=Tim |last=Jonze |url=http://www.theguardian.com/music/2015/feb/25/taylor-swift-wins-international-female-solo-artist-at-brit-awards-2015 |title=Taylor Swift wins international female solo artist at Brit awards 2015 }}</ref>。泰勒絲被《[[时代_(杂志)|时代]]》杂志提名为2015年“偶像类”[[时代百大人物|时代百大人物]]<ref>{{cite web |first=Nancy |last=Gibbs |url=http://www.msn.com/en-us/news/world/how-we-pick-the-time-100/ar-AAb5qjA |title=How We Pick |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150711113924/http://www.msn.com/en-us/news/world/how-we-pick-the-time-100/ar-AAb5qjA |archivedate=2015-07-11 }}</ref>。泰勒与其他七位艺术家在2015年乡村音乐学院奖上获得50周年里程碑奖<ref>{{cite web |last=Betts |first=Stephen L. |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-miranda-lambert-among-2015-acm-awards-milestone-winners-20150325 |title=2015 ACM Award Milestone Winners Include Swift, Lambert |publisher=Rolling Stone |date=2015-03-25 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150402150635/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-miranda-lambert-among-2015-acm-awards-milestone-winners-20150325 |archivedate=2015-04-02 }}</ref>。 

2015年6月，《空格》在[[YouTube|YouTube]]的點閱率達到10億，成為第二位音樂錄影帶在YouTube突破10億的女歌手和第四位有10億MV點閱率的歌手。<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0KSOMA3QBU0|title=Katy Perry - Dark Horse (Official) ft. Juicy J|work=YouTube|accessdate=2015-06-23|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150622062006/https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0KSOMA3QBU0|archivedate=2015-06-22}}</ref>8月5日，泰勒絲在推特宣布将发行《1989》的第五首单曲《[[狂野的梦|狂野的梦]]》，该曲已于8月25日发行<ref>{{cite web | url = http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6655729/taylor-swift-announces-next-single | title = Taylro Swift Announces Next Single | first = Keith | last = Caufield | date = 2015-08-05 | publisher = Billboard.com | location = New York City | quote = Taylor Swift’s next single will be…"Wildest Dreams". | deadurl = no | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20150808000055/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6655729/taylor-swift-announces-next-single | archivedate = 2015-08-08 }}</ref>。8月31日，泰勒絲在[[2015年MTV音乐录影带大奖|2015年MTV音乐录影带大奖]]上凭借年度音乐录影带、最佳女歌手录影带、最佳流行录影带、最佳合作四项大奖领跑，并在暖场秀上播放《狂野的梦》的音乐录影带<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.mtv.com/news/2248825/taylor-swift-wildest-dreams-vmas/|title=Taylor Swift’s ‘Wildest Dreams’ Video Will Premiere During The VMA Pre-Show|last=Hosken|first=Patrick|date=2015-08-23|website=MTV.com|accessdate=2015-08-23|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150826222809/http://www.mtv.com/news/2248825/taylor-swift-wildest-dreams-vmas/|archivedate=2015-08-26}}</ref>。在{{le|2015年MTV欧洲音乐大奖|2015 MTV Europe Music Awards}}上，泰勒继续以九项提名领跑<ref>{{cite news|author1=Toyin Owoseje|title=MTV Europe Music Awards 2015: Taylor Swift continues winning streak with nine nominations|url=http://www.ibtimes.co.uk/mtv-europe-music-award-2015-taylor-swift-continues-winning-streak-nine-nominations-1519984|accessdate=2015-10-24|agency=IBTimes|date=2015-09-26|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20151028234510/http://www.ibtimes.co.uk/mtv-europe-music-award-2015-taylor-swift-continues-winning-streak-nine-nominations-1519984|archivedate=2015-10-28}}</ref>。

在第64届{{le|BMI流行音乐奖|BMI Awards}}，泰勒絲荣膺「泰勒絲大奖」（英語：Taylor Swift Award）。这是BMI继1990年[[迈克尔·杰克逊|迈克尔·杰克逊]]后二度以个人名字颁发大奖<ref>{{cite web | url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/7325271/bmi-pop-awards-taylor-swift-award-barry-mann-cynthia-weil | title=Taylor Swift to Receive First-Ever Taylor Swift Award From BMI | work=Billboard | date=2016-04-05 | accessdate=2016-04-05 | author=Polanco, Luis | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160406044221/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/7325271/bmi-pop-awards-taylor-swift-award-barry-mann-cynthia-weil | archivedate=2016-04-06 }}</ref>。泰勒絲还于2016年出演[[苹果公司|苹果公司]]广告，与[[德雷克_(歌手)|德雷克]]和[[未来_(歌手)|未来小子]]共唱两人的作品《{{le|飞人 (歌曲)|Jumpman (song)|飞人}}》<ref>{{cite magazine |last=Morris |first=Jessie |title=Taylor Swift's Apple Commercial Benefited Drake and Future in a Huge Way |date=2016-04-06 |magazine=Complex |url=http://www.complex.com/music/2016/04/taylor-swift-apple-commercial-benefited-drake |access-date=2016-06-26 |archive-url=https://www.webcitation.org/6iY2NZsKb?url=http://www.complex.com/music/2016/04/taylor-swift-apple-commercial-benefited-drake |archive-date=2016-06-26 |dead-url=no }}</ref>。2016年2月15日，《1989》在[[第58届格莱美奖|第58屆葛萊美]]獲得年度專輯及最佳流行專輯，單曲《[[壞到底_(歌曲)|壞到底]]》的音樂錄影帶獲得了最佳音樂錄影帶也與[[肯德里克·拉马尔|肯德里克·拉馬爾]]入圍了最佳流行組合/團體，泰勒絲成為史上第一位女歌手獲得兩次年度專輯，單曲《[[空格_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|空白]]》也入圍了年度製作及年度歌曲，也替泰勒絲入圍最佳流行歌手，在典禮中，泰勒絲表演《[[脱离困境|不再迷惘]]》。分手后，泰勒絲用化名尼尔斯·贝舍里（{{lang|en|Nils Sjöberg}}）与[[凱文·哈里斯|凱文·哈里斯]]共同创作及共同制作歌曲《[[天注定_(歌曲)|天注定]]》<ref>{{cite news | url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-wrote-calvin-harris-smash-hit-this-is-what-you-came-for-20160713 | title=Taylor Swift Co-Wrote Calvin Harris' Smash Hit 'This Is What You Came For' | work=Rolling Stone | date=2016-07-13 | accessdate=2016-07-31 | last=Spanos | first=Brittany | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160730023011/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-wrote-calvin-harris-smash-hit-this-is-what-you-came-for-20160713 | archivedate=2016-07-30 }}</ref>。10月，她创作{{le|小大城|Little Big Town}}第七张专辑{{le|《The Breaker》|The Breaker (Little Big Town album)}}的歌曲《{{le|Better Man|Better Man (Little Big Town song)}}》 <ref>{{cite news|last1=Bailey|first1=Alyssa|title=Which Ex Is This New Taylor Swift Song "Better Man" About?|url=http://www.elle.com/culture/celebrities/news/a40417/taylor-swift-better-man-lyrics-calvin-harris-tom-hiddleston/|accessdate=2016-11-01|work=Elle|date=2016-11-01|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://archive.is/20161110232147/http://www.elle.com/culture/celebrities/news/a40417/taylor-swift-better-man-lyrics-calvin-harris-tom-hiddleston/|archivedate=2016-11-10}}</ref>，两个月后又与[[贊恩·馬利克|贊恩·马利克]]共同演唱2017年电影《[[格雷的五十道陰影：束縛_(電影)|格雷的五十道陰影：束縛]]》主题歌曲《[[無愛不活|無愛不活]]》<ref>{{cite news|author=Hunt, Elle|title=Taylor Swift and Zayn Malik release surprise duet for Fifty Shades Darker soundtrack|url=https://www.theguardian.com/music/2016/dec/09/taylor-swift-and-zayn-malik-release-surprise-duet-for-fifty-shades-darker-soundtrack|newspaper=The Guardian|date=2016-12-09|accessdate=2016-12-09|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20161209194716/https://www.theguardian.com/music/2016/dec/09/taylor-swift-and-zayn-malik-release-surprise-duet-for-fifty-shades-darker-soundtrack|archivedate=2016-12-09}}</ref>。

=== 2017年－2019年：《[[舉世盛名|舉世盛名]]》 ===
[[File:Taylor_Swift_Reputation_Tour1_(cropped).jpg|替代=]]上表演]]
2017年8月，泰勒絲在訴就職于[[丹佛|丹佛]]電臺{{tsl|en|KYGO-FM||KYGO-FM}}的DJ大衛·穆勒性騷擾案中勝訴。4年前在，泰勒絲曾向穆勒的上司舉報穆勒在[[红巡回演唱会|紅色巡迴演唱會]]後台對她襲臀。後來，穆勒被炒，於是控告泰勒絲誣陷自己，使自己丟了工作。不久後，泰勒絲反訴穆勒性騷擾。陪審團駁回了穆勒的提告，並依法支持了泰勒絲的訴求，之後泰勒絲勝訴。<ref>{{Cite web|last1=Gonzalez|first1=Sandra|last2=McLean|first2=Scott|last3=Weisfeldt|first3=Sara|last4=Gauk-Roger|first4=Topher|title=Taylor Swift wins court case|url=http://edition.cnn.com/2017/08/14/entertainment/taylor-swift-verdict/index.html|publisher=CNN|accessdate=2017-08-20|date=2017-08-15|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170819230306/http://edition.cnn.com/2017/08/14/entertainment/taylor-swift-verdict/index.html|archivedate=2017-08-19}}</ref>

2017年7月中旬，泰勒絲突然在毫無預警的情况下清空了她的所有社交網絡帳號以及删除了所有的好友和自己的头像，并同时关闭了自己的个人网站<ref>{{Cite news|url=http://www.news.com.au/entertainment/music/music-videos/taylor-swift-appears-to-have-deleted-all-of-her-social-media-accounts/news-story/7e19aa3db991a58a6a5d73241608ffe0|title=Speculation rife over Swift's social media disappearance|date=2017-08-19|publisher=News.com.au|access-date=2017-08-19|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170819062321/http://www.news.com.au/entertainment/music/music-videos/taylor-swift-appears-to-have-deleted-all-of-her-social-media-accounts/news-story/7e19aa3db991a58a6a5d73241608ffe0|archivedate=2017-08-19}}</ref>。
2017年8月，泰勒絲恢复了其个人网站，并發佈了她的第6張錄音室專輯《[[舉世盛名|舉世盛名]]》的首支單曲《[[看是你逼我的|看是你逼我的]]》。<ref>{{Cite journal|last1=Aswad|first1=Jem|title=Taylor Swift's New Single, 'Look What You Made Me Do,' Arrives (Listen)|magazine=Variety|date=2017-08-24|url=https://variety.com/2017/music/news/taylor-swifts-new-single-look-what-you-made-me-do-arrives-listen-1202538781/|accessdate=2017-08-29|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170828211858/http://variety.com/2017/music/news/taylor-swifts-new-single-look-what-you-made-me-do-arrives-listen-1202538781/|archivedate=2017-08-28}}</ref>歌曲在澳大利亞、愛爾蘭、紐西蘭、英國和美國奪冠。<ref>最高排位：<br />
{{Cite web|url=http://www.ariacharts.com.au/news/2017/taylor-swift-scores-fifth-1-single|publisher=Australian Recording Industry Association|date=2017-09-02|accessdate=2017-09-02|title=Taylor Swift Scores Fifth No. 1 Single|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170902191138/http://www.ariacharts.com.au/news/2017/taylor-swift-scores-fifth-1-single|archivedate=2017-09-02}}<br web|title=Taylor Swift holds No. 1 for second week|url=http://www.ariacharts.com.au/news/2017/taylor-swift-holds-1-for-second-week|publisher=Australian Recording Industry Association|date=2017-09-09|accessdate=2017-10-07|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170917034506/http://www.ariacharts.com.au/news/2017/taylor-swift-holds-1-for-second-week|archivedate=2017-09-17}}</ref><ref name="lwymmd" />

在《舉世盛名》專輯中，泰勒絲還是與[[马克斯·马丁|馬克斯‧馬丁]]、[[歇爾貝克_(唱片製作人)|歇爾貝克]]及[[杰克·安东诺夫|傑克‧安東諾夫]]合作，泰勒絲在這張專輯中還是跟以往一樣擔任主要聲樂、和聲、執行製作人、製作人、詞曲作家及專輯包裝設計，本專輯延續了上一張專輯《[[1989_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|1989]]》的流行舞曲、電子流行及合成器流行，但這張專輯有些歌曲的歌詞中，可以看到近幾年泰勒絲在媒體和輿論壓力下的難過以及她被朋友出賣而很失望，雖然這張專輯較黑暗，但是還是可以看到以前的創作元素，例如：敘述愛情、為粉絲寫歌...等。
[[File:Taylor_Swift_performing_Fearless.jpg|缩略图]]上表演]]
《舉世盛名》共發行了《[[完美情人_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|完美情人]]》和《[[随你怎么说_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|随你怎么说]]》兩首宣傳單曲，其中前者於歐洲成為專輯的第5張單曲發行。<ref>{{Cite magazine|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/8006719/taylor-swift-gorgeous-single-release|title=Taylor Swift's 'Gorgeous' New Single Has Arrived: Listen|last=Brandle|first=Lars|date=2017-10-20|magazine=Billboard|access-date=2017-12-07|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171020094302/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/8006719/taylor-swift-gorgeous-single-release|archivedate=2017-10-20}}<br>{{Cite magazine|last1=Iasimone|first1=Ashley|last2=Brandle|first2=Lars|title=Taylor Swift Debuts 'Call It What You Want': Watch Lyric Video|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8022883/taylor-swift-call-it-what-you-want-song-listen|accessdate=2017-12-07|magazine=Billboard|date=2017-11-03|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171205182259/https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8022883/taylor-swift-call-it-what-you-want-song-listen|archivedate=2017-12-05}}<br>{{Cite web |url=http://www.bbc.co.uk/radio1/playlist |title=BBC – Radio 1 – Playlist |publisher=[[BBC廣播一台|BBC Radio 1]] |accessdate=2018-01-12 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180112164557/http://www.bbc.co.uk/radio1/playlist |archivedate=2018-01-12}}</ref>專輯於11月10日正式發行，以121.6萬純銷量成為美國2017年銷量最高的專輯。這讓泰勒絲成為唯一一位有四張專輯在釋出首周賣出超過100萬張的藝人。而其全球首週銷量則超過了200萬份。<ref>{{Cite magazine|title=Taylor Swift Schools the Music Industry Once Again, While Streaming Services Wring Their Hands|first=Robert|last=Levine|magazine=Billboard|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/business/8046278/taylor-swift-streaming-services-reputation-music-industry-analysis|date=2017-11-22|accessdate=2017-12-02|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171130163201/https://www.billboard.com/articles/business/8046278/taylor-swift-streaming-services-reputation-music-industry-analysis|archivedate=2017-11-30}}</ref>專輯在美國、英國、加拿大和澳大利亞等多國奪冠。<ref>{{Cite magazine|last1=Brandle|first1=Lars|title=Taylor Swift's 'Reputation' Rules Australia's Albums Chart|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/8039595/taylor-swift-reputation-rules-australia-albums-chart|accessdate=2017-12-02|magazine=Billboard|date=2017-11-20|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171120194555/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/8039595/taylor-swift-reputation-rules-australia-albums-chart|archivedate=2017-11-20}}</ref><ref>{{Cite magazine|title=Taylor Swift Chart History|url=https://www.billboard.com/music/Taylor-Swift/chart-history/canadian-albums|accessdate=2017-12-02|magazine=Billboard|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171207180058/https://www.billboard.com/music/Taylor-Swift/chart-history/canadian-albums|archivedate=2017-12-07}}</ref>專輯發行之後，泰勒絲在《[[週六夜現場|週六夜現場]]》現場表演了《準備好了嗎》和《随你怎么说》。<ref>{{Cite news|last1=Aswad|first1=Jem|title=Taylor Swift Strips Things Down for 'Saturday Night Live' Performances (Watch)|url=https://variety.com/2017/music/news/taylor-swift-strips-things-down-for-saturday-night-live-performances-watch-video-1202612891/|accessdate=2017-11-18|work=Variety|date=2017-11-12|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171115230246/http://variety.com/2017/music/news/taylor-swift-strips-things-down-for-saturday-night-live-performances-watch-video-1202612891/|archivedate=2017-11-15}}</ref>專輯的第3張單曲《[[游戏终结|游戏终结]]》與[[紅髮艾德|紅髮艾德]]和[[未来小子_(歌手)|未来小子]]合作，於該年11月發行，在美國最高排第18位。<ref>{{Cite magazine|title=Taylor Swift Chart History|magazine=Billboard|url=https://www.billboard.com/music/Taylor-Swift/chart-history/hot-100|accessdate=2018-04-07|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180308171829/https://www.billboard.com/music/Taylor-Swift/chart-history/hot-100|archivedate=2018-03-08}}</ref>專輯的其它單曲包括《[[新年日_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|新年日]]》、《[[不堪一击_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|不堪一击]]》和《[[逃脱之车|亡命飛車]]》，其中第一者僅在鄉村電台發行。<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/country/8039304/taylor-swift-new-years-day-reputation-country-radio|title=Taylor Swift's 'New Year's Day' Goes to Country Radio: Is Country Ready for It?|last1=Trust|first1=Gary|website=Billboard|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171205104854/https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/country/8039304/taylor-swift-new-years-day-reputation-country-radio|archivedate=2017-12-05|deadurl=no|accessdate=2018-04-13}}<br>{{Cite web|last1=Braca|first1=Nina|title=Taylor Swift to Release 'Delicate' Music Video at iHeart Radio Music Awards|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8231873/taylor-swift-delicate-music-video-iheart-radio-music-awards|website=Billboard|accessdate=2018-04-13|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180414113842/https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8231873/taylor-swift-delicate-music-video-iheart-radio-music-awards|archivedate=2018-04-14}}</ref>

為宣傳《舉世盛名》，泰勒絲於2018年開啟了[[舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會|舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會]]，[[查莉·XCX|查莉·XCX]]及[[卡蜜拉·卡貝優|卡蜜拉·卡貝羅]]擔任北美場及歐洲場暖場嘉賓，查莉及布魯茲樂團（英語： Broods）擔任大洋洲場暖場嘉賓，亞洲場暖場嘉賓僅有查莉。<ref>{{Cite magazine|last1=Stubblebine|first1=Allison|title=Taylor Swift Announces First Round of Reputation Stadium Tour Dates|magazine=Billboard|date=2017-11-13|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8031415/taylor-swift-reputation-tour-dates|accessdate=2017-11-18|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171114063459/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8031415/taylor-swift-reputation-tour-dates|archivedate=2017-11-14}}</ref>2018年4月，泰勒絲獻聲{{tsl|en|Sugarland|甜園合唱團|甜園合唱團}}歌曲《[[Babe_(甜園合唱團歌曲)|寶貝]]》，該曲為泰勒絲與[[追隨者合唱團|追隨者合唱團]]成員[[派屈克·莫納漢|派屈克·莫納漢]]共同創作，原本為泰勒絲2012年專輯《[[红_(泰勒·斯威夫特专辑)|紅色]]》創作的歌曲。<ref name="Bigger">{{Cite web|last1=Hudak|first1=Joseph|title=Sugarland Announce New Album 'Bigger,' Taylor Swift Collaboration|url=https://www.rollingstone.com/country/news/sugarland-announce-new-album-bigger-taylor-swift-collaboration-w519097|website=Rolling Stone|accessdate=2018-04-13|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180414113840/https://www.rollingstone.com/country/news/sugarland-announce-new-album-bigger-taylor-swift-collaboration-w519097|archivedate=2018-04-14}}</ref>

2018年3月11日，泰勒絲在[[2018年iHeartRadio音乐奖颁奖典礼|2018年iHeartRadio音樂獎頒獎典禮]]首播第4張單曲《[[不堪一击_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|不堪一擊]]》的音樂錄影帶，並獲得年度女藝人。2018年5月20日，泰勒絲在[[2018年告示牌音樂獎|2018年告示牌音樂獎]]獲得了最佳女藝人，《舉世盛名》也獲得了最佳銷量專輯，亦維持「最多[[公告牌音乐奖|告示牌音樂獎]]的歌手」。
2018年7月，泰勒絲在音樂劇改编的電影《[[貓_(電影)|貓 (電影)]]》中扮演了{{tsl|en|Bombalurina||邦貝魯琳娜}}<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://variety.com/2018/film/news/jennifer-hudson-taylor-swift-james-corden-cats-movie-andrew-lloyd-webber-1202879375-1202879375/|title=Jennifer Hudson, Taylor Swift, James Corden Cast in Movie Version of 'Cats'|last=Chu|first=Henry|date=2018-07-20|work=Variety |access-date=2018-07-20}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://deadline.com/2018/12/universal-working-titles-feature-adaptation-of-andrew-lloyd-webbers-cats-rolls-cameras-1202518943/|title=Universal-Working Title’s Feature Adaptation Of Andrew Lloyd Webber’s ‘Cats’ Rolls Cameras|last=D'Alessandro|first=Anthony|date=2018-12-12|work=Deadline Holllywodd|access-date=2018-12-13}}</ref>。2018年10月9日，泰勒絲在2018年[[全美音樂獎|全美音樂獎]]表演《[[我的错|我的錯]]》，並獲得了年度藝人及最佳流行/搖滾女藝人，[[舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會|舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會]]獲得了年度巡演，《[[舉世盛名|舉世盛名]]》獲得了最佳流行/搖滾專輯。泰勒絲共獲得23項全美音樂獎，成為擁有最多全美音樂獎的女歌手，正式超越[[惠特妮·休斯顿|惠妮·休士頓]]的22項，也成為擁有第二多的歌手，僅次於[[迈克尔·杰克逊|麥可·傑克森]]的24項。2018年11月11日，[[舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會|舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會]]獲得了[[人民选择奖|全美民選獎]]的最佳巡迴演唱會（英語：Favorite Concert Tour）。

2018年11月20日，泰勒絲宣布将不再与[[大機器唱片|大机器唱片]]续约，并在[[Instagram|Instagram]]及[[Facebook|Facebook]]上发布自己将與[[环球唱片|环球音乐]]重新簽約，並入主環球旗下的唱片公司[[Republic_Records|聯眾唱片]]。<ref>{{Cite web|last1=Bruner|first1=Raisa|title=Taylor Swift Says She's 'Ecstatic' to Be Switching Record Labels|url=http://time.com/5459458/taylor-swift-universal-spotify/|website=Time|accessdate=2018-11-20}}</ref>新合約中，泰勒絲可以擁有自己的音樂版權，同時她也要求環球出售[[Spotify|Spotify]]股份時得到的利益讓環球旗下的歌手抽成，而且當中不得扣除任何費用，並且環球也同意以上的要求，此舉保障了音樂人在串流媒體的權益，引起多數媒體的好評，並稱泰勒絲此舉為開創先河。
[[File:Taylor_Swift_Reputation_Tour_Minneapolis_(43490534145).jpg|替代=]]上表演]]
2019年2月10日，《舉世盛名》入圍了[[第61屆格萊美獎|第61屆葛萊美獎]]的「最佳流行演唱專輯」（英語：Best Pop Vocal Album）。2019年3月14日，在iHeartRadio音樂獎（英語：iHeartRadio Music Awards）中，《[[不堪一击_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|不堪一擊]]》的音樂錄影帶獲得了「最佳音樂錄影帶」（英語：Best Music Video），[[舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會|舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會]]也獲得了「年度巡迴演唱會」（英語：Tour of the Year），泰勒絲的粉絲軍團 「Swifties」入圍了「最佳粉絲軍團」（英語：Best Fan Army），泰勒絲擁有10個iHeartRadio音樂獎，成為獲獎最多的歌手，並入圍21次，與[[爱莉安娜·格兰德|亞莉安娜·格蘭德]]並列成為入圍第三多的歌手，僅次於[[德雷克_(歌手)|德雷克]]的27次及[[蕾哈娜|蕾哈娜]]的25次。2019年3月，泰勒絲成為2019年[[ELLE|ELLE]]雜誌美國版及英國版4月份雜誌封面人物；英國版的內容為泰勒絲創作音樂的心得及感想，美國版的內容為泰勒絲一在30歲前學到的30件事情。

=== 2019年－至今：《TS7》 ===
2019年4月13日凌晨，泰勒絲封鎖了其个人网站除购物按钮外的全部連結，并将自己所有的社交网络帐号头像更换成了一片粉色烟雾，同时在Instagram的限時動態和其个人网站上发布了一条倒數。根据泰勒絲之前宣传《舉世盛名》时的动作，4月26日，也就是倒數开始13天后，泰勒絲的《TS7》的首单将发布，并且泰勒絲也将正式公开《TS7》名称。随后，泰勒絲开始在全球各地的广告牌上进行大規模的宣传，并为自己的个人网站提供了一个名为aprilTwentySix.com的转接链接，提供粉絲留下電子信箱及國家，讓粉絲第一時間知道新專輯及主打歌的消息。

2019年4月19日，泰勒絲登上《[[時代雜誌|時代]]》雜誌封面，並入選[[时代百大人物|時代百大人物]]，這是泰勒絲第三次登上時代雜誌封面人物（2014年、2017年、2019年），是首位女性三次登上時代雜誌封面，她也是第三次入選時代百大人物（2010年、2015年、2019年）。

2019年5月1日，在2019年[[公告牌音乐奖|告示牌音樂獎]]中，泰勒絲入圍了「最佳女藝人」及「最佳巡演藝人」兩項。

== 艺术技巧 ==

=== 所受影响 ===
泰勒絲最早的音乐记忆，是听她的外祖母马乔里·芬利（{{lang|en|Marjorie Finlay}}，娘家姓Moehlenkamp）在教堂唱歌<ref name="readingeagle1" /><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1600309/cmt-insider-interview-taylor-swift-part-1-of-2.jhtml |title=News : CMT Insider Interview: Taylor Swift (Part 1 of 2) |publisher=CMT |date=2008-11-26 |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130509053507/http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1600309/cmt-insider-interview-taylor-swift-part-1-of-2.jhtml |archivedate=2013-05-09 }}</ref>。芬利年轻是波多黎各一档电视节目的主持人，还在[[泰国|泰国]]和[[新加坡|新加坡]]出演歌剧<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" /><ref>{{cite web |url=http://raretaylorswift.webs.com/apps/photos/photo?photoid=175760002 |title=Taylor's grandma's obituary – Rare Taylor Swift |publisher=Raretaylorswift.webs.com |date=2013-03-07 |accessdate=2013-11-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131221001555/http://raretaylorswift.webs.com/apps/photos/photo?photoid=175760002 |archivedate=2013-12-21 }}</ref>。泰勒絲年纪小小就会欣赏迪士尼电影原声带：“我的父母发现一旦我忘掉了歌词，就会自己编<ref name="CMT 2008-11-26" /><ref name="theaustralian1">{{cite news |url=http://www.theaustralian.com.au/arts/swift-rise-of-the-anti-diva/story-e6frg8n6-1111119032411 |title=Swift rise of the anti-diva |first=Dan |last=Cairns |newspaper=The Australian |date=2009-03-05 |accessdate=2012-07-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141224030802/http://www.theaustralian.com.au/arts/swift-rise-of-the-anti-diva/story-e6frg8n6-1111119032411 |archivedate=2014-12-24 }}</ref>。”后来，她的父母让她接触[[詹姆斯·泰勒|詹姆斯·泰勒]]、[[西蒙和加芬克尔|西蒙和加芬克尔]]和戴夫·莱帕德等艺术家<ref>{{cite web |author=October 26, 2010; Written by Alison Bonaguro |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/cmt-blog/1650869/taylor-swift-says-to-love-what-you-loved-when-you-were-6.jhtml |title=News : Taylor Swift Says to Love What You Loved When You Were 6 |publisher=CMT |date=2010-10-26 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113174634/http://www.cmt.com/news/cmt-blog/1650869/taylor-swift-says-to-love-what-you-loved-when-you-were-6.jhtml |archivedate=2012年11月13日 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Lane |first=Mary M. |url=http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304050304577375872042368612.html |title=James Taylor Talks About Songwriting, Addiction and His New Friend Taylor Swift – ''The Wall Street Journal'' |work=The Wall Street Journal |date=2012-05-02 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120630090037/http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304050304577375872042368612.html |archivedate=2012-06-30 }}</ref>。泰勒絲表示，她自信归功于帮助还是孩子的她准备课堂展示的母亲<ref>{{cite web |author=Peter Kramer, Associated Press – Ap |url=http://www.startribune.com/lifestyle/12149446.html?elr=KArks:DCiU1PciUiD3aPc:_Yyc:aUoaEYY_1Pc_bDaEP7U |title=Music: OMG! Taylor's senior year |work=Star Tribune |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130612143436/http://www.startribune.com/lifestyle/12149446.html?elr=KArks:DCiU1PciUiD3aPc:_Yyc:aUoaEYY_1Pc_bDaEP7U |archivedate=2013-06-12 }}</ref>。她还认为“迷恋于给母亲写故事和讲故事”<ref>{{cite web|url=http://music.aol.com/sessions/taylor-swift-change-sessions/ |title=Taylor Swift, 'Change' (Sessions) |publisher=AOL Music |accessdate=2012-08-17 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111207024144/http://music.aol.com/sessions/taylor-swift-change-sessions/ |archivedate=2011-12-07 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。

泰勒絲被“仙妮娅、菲思、南方小鸡等90年代的杰出女性乡村音乐家们带入乡村音乐界<ref name="CMT 2007-11-12" /><ref name="USAWEEKEND1">{{cite news |first=Dennis |last=McCafferty |title=Taylor's Swift rise |url=http://159.54.226.237/08_issues/080413/080413taylor-swift.html |date=2008-04-13 |work=USA Weekend |accessdate=2012-04-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121114113840/http://159.54.226.237/08_issues/080413/080413taylor-swift.html |archivedate=2012-11-14 }}</ref>。”她被乡村音乐的故事和音色吸引住了<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.countrystandardtime.com/news/newsitem.asp?xid=4649 |title=Swift starts world tour in Asia, pushes "Speak Now' in NY |publisher=Countrystandardtime.com |date=2007-102-3 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113072555/http://www.countrystandardtime.com/news/newsitem.asp?xid=4649 |archivedate=2012-11-13 }}</ref>。作曲家兼表演者唐恩给她在音乐上的影响最大<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,1893502-1,00.html |title=Interview with Taylor Swift |work=Time |date=2009-04-23 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121115053552/http://www.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,1893502-1,00.html |archivedate=2012-11-15 }}</ref>。希尔是泰勒絲的童年榜样：“但凡她的言行和衣着，我都尝试去模仿<ref>{{cite news|title=Taylor Swift Style: Singer Won't Take Her Clothes Off, Wants People To Focus On Music|url=http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2012/10/23/taylor-swift-style-wont-take-her-clothes-off_n_2006776.html|accessdate=2015-01-04|work=The Huffington Post|date=2012-10-23|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150104081258/http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2012/10/23/taylor-swift-style-wont-take-her-clothes-off_n_2006776.html|archivedate=2015-01-04}}</ref><ref name="billboard2">{{cite web |author=Taylor Swift: Billboard's Woman of the Year |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |title=Billboard – News – |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130203232452/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/464865/taylor-swift-billboards-woman-of-the-year |archivedate=2013-02-03 }}</ref>。”泰勒絲钦佩南方的反叛态度和他们表演自创乐器的能力<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" /><ref name=autogenerated2>{{cite web |url=http://www.instyle.co.uk/news/instyle-meets-country-singing-sensation-taylor-swift-26-10-10 |title=InStyle meets country singing sensation Taylor Swift |publisher=Instyle.co.uk |date=2010-10-26 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120207213523/http://www.instyle.co.uk/news/instyle-meets-country-singing-sensation-taylor-swift-26-10-10 |archivedate=2012-02-07 }}</ref>，该乐队的歌曲《{{le|带我走牛仔|Cowboy Take Me Away}}》是泰勒絲第一支学会用吉他弹奏歌曲<ref>{{cite web |author=July 25, 2011; Written by Alison Bonaguro |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/cmt-offstage/1667840/offstage-taylor-swift-plays-dixie-chicks-for-a-dixie-chick.jhtml |title=News : OFFSTAGE: Taylor Swift Plays Dixie Chicks for a Dixie Chick |publisher=CMT |date=2011-07-25 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113174617/http://www.cmt.com/news/cmt-offstage/1667840/offstage-taylor-swift-plays-dixie-chicks-for-a-dixie-chick.jhtml |archivedate=2012年11月13日 }}</ref>。

泰勒絲开始探索乡村巨星前辈的音乐，包括克莱因、{{le|罗莉·塔琳|Loretta Lynn}}<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" />、[[桃莉·巴顿|桃莉·巴顿]]和{{le|泰咪·怀尼特|Tammy Wynette}}<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" /><ref>Blender, April 2008, page 52</ref>。她认为桃莉是“一位是所有女性词曲作家的杰出榜样<ref name="billboard2" />。”其他影响到她的主流乡村音乐人包括{{le|米兰达·兰伯特|Miranda Lambert}}<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.lasvegassun.com/news/2009/may/24/taylor-swift-miranda-lambert-contrast-country-styl/ |title=Taylor Swift, Miranda Lambert a contrast in country styles – Las Vegas Sun News 其他音樂類型的艺术家也影响到泰勒絲。青少年时期的她喜欢汉森和[[小甜甜布蘭妮|小甜甜布蘭妮]]等{{le|泡泡糖流行乐|bubblegum pop}}艺人，她对斯皮尔斯仍然有“毫不动摇的热爱”<ref>{{cite web |first=Jocelyn |last=Vena
