name="amazon.com" />和[[艾薇儿·拉维尼|艾薇儿·拉维尼]]等当代女性创作型歌手歌迷<ref name="usatoday.com" />。

泰勒絲十分关心电视剧《[[橘郡风云|橘郡风云]]》和《[[实习医生格蕾|实习医生格蕾]]》的音乐总监，剧中的每一首歌她都会去下载<ref name="itunes.apple.com" />。她也是[[嘻哈音乐|嘻哈乐迷]]，表示“（生活方式中的）傲慢是乡村乐和嘻哈共同的元素<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" />。”泰勒絲还从老艺人目录中的作品汲取灵感。她称尼克斯是一位“英雄”，“在很多方面激励着我”<ref name="deadline.com" /><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.shineon-media.com/2010/05/05/taylor-swift-time-100-gala/ |title=Taylor Swift: TIME 100 Gala |publisher=Shine on Media |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131111014303/http://www.shineon-media.com/2010/05/05/taylor-swift-time-100-gala/ |archivedate=2013-11-11 }}</ref>。她认为佩蒂“是我的基座”<ref name=instyle>InStyle June 2011</ref>。她对{{le|雪莉儿合唱团|The Shirelles}}、{{le|多丽丝·特洛伊|Doris Troy}}和[[沙滩男孩|沙滩男孩]]等60年代的艺人也很“痴迷”<ref name="Rolling Stone 2011-08-18" /><ref name="autogenerated1">{{cite web |work=Delta Sky |accessdate=2015-08-29 |url=http://deltaskymag.delta.com/taylorswift.aspx |title=The Sweet Charmed Life of Taylor Swift |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20151029024944/http://deltaskymag.delta.com/taylorswift.aspx |archivedate=2015-10-29 }}</ref>。影响也来自于其他女性[[流行摇滚|流行摇滚]]前辈歌手，包括[[帕特·贝纳塔尔|帕特·贝纳塔尔]]<ref name="usatoday.com" /><ref name="rolling stone rock">{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift Talks Feminism, Misogyny in Maxim|url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-talks-feminism-misogyny-in-maxim-20150519|website=Rolling Stone|accessdate=2015-07-13|date=2015-05-19|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150725065237/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-talks-feminism-misogyny-in-maxim-20150519|archivedate=2015-07-25}}</ref>、[[梅丽莎·埃瑟里奇|梅丽莎·埃瑟里奇]]<ref name="rolling stone rock" />、[[莎拉·克劳克兰|莎拉·克劳克兰]]<ref name="chicagotribune1" />、{{le|肖恩·科尔|Shawn Colvin}}<ref name="Up for Discussion">{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/953737/taylor-swift-the-billboard-cover-story |title=Taylor Swift: The Billboard Cover Story |work=Billboard |date=2009-09-14 |accessdate=2012-07-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20101018200303/http://www.billboard.com/features/taylor-swift-the-billboard-cover-story-1004121338.story |archivedate=2010-10-18 }}</ref>和[[琳达·朗丝黛|琳达·朗丝黛]]<ref name="rollingstone.com">{{cite web |author=Austin Scaggs |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/q-a-with-taylor-swift-20100204 |title=Taylor Swift Opens Up About Her Biggest Year Yet | Music News |work=Rolling Stone |date=2010-02-04 |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130305224331/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/q-a-with-taylor-swift-20100204 |archivedate=2013-03-05 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0,,20434320_2,00.html |title=Taylor Swift Goes Record Shopping with EW |work=Entertainment Weekly |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130502202650/http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0%2C%2C20434320_2%2C00.html |archivedate=2013-05-02 }}</ref>。

泰勒絲把保罗·麦卡特尼、布鲁斯·斯普林斯汀、[[愛美蘿·哈里斯|愛美蘿·哈里斯]]、克里斯·克里斯托佛森和卡莉·西蒙列为她的职业模范：“尽管他们拥有机遇，但他们在整个职业生涯一直没有改变流派<ref name="Up for Discussion" /><ref name="newyorker2">{{cite web |last=Widdicombe |first=Lizzie |url=http://www.newyorker.com/reporting/2011/10/10/111010fa_fact_widdicombe?currentPage=all |title=Taylor Swift Makes Primness Lucrative |work=The New Yorker |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120718214111/http://www.newyorker.com/reporting/2011/10/10/111010fa_fact_widdicombe?currentPage=all |archivedate=2012-07-18 }}</ref><ref name="usatoday1">{{cite news |last=Mansfield |first=Brian |url=http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2010-10-22-taylorswift22_CV_N.htm |title=Taylor Swift learns to 'Speak Now,' reveal her maturity |work=USA Today |date=2010-10-23 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120110125218/http://www.usatoday.com/life/music/news/2010-10-22-taylorswift22_CV_N.htm |archivedate=2012-01-10 }}</ref>。”[[披头士|披头士]]乐队成员，现独唱艺术家麦卡特尼让泰勒絲感觉“好像我进入到他的心脏和他的大脑裡去了”：“所有音乐人仅能奢望这样的遗产<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.people.com/people/archive/article/0,,20567076,00.html |title=Rolling in the Trophies? – Adele |work=People |date=2012-02-06 |accessdate=2012-07-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120601020156/http://www.people.com/people/archive/article/0%2C%2C20567076%2C00.html |archivedate=2012-06-01 }}</ref>。”她欣赏斯普林斯汀，因为他“经过了这么长一段时间仍在乐坛保持影响力”<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0,,20434320_2,00.html |title=Taylor Swift Goes Record Shopping with EW |work=Entertainment Weekly |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130502202650/http://www.ew.com/ew/article/0%2C%2C20434320_2%2C00.html |archivedate=2013-05-02 }}</ref>。她还立志在未来成为像哈里斯那样的人：“她不在乎名利，只在乎音乐<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.channelguidemagblog.com/index.php/2008/11/02/our-interview-with-taylor-swift/ |title=Our Interview with Taylor Swift | Channel Guide Magazine |publisher=Channelguidemagblog.com |date=2008-11-02 |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130201183546/http://www.channelguidemagblog.com/index.php/2008/11/02/our-interview-with-taylor-swift/ |archivedate=2013-02-01 }}</ref>。”泰勒絲认为克里斯托佛森“在写歌方面很有才华……他是行业的老将之一，但你不能够说还没有琢磨透，就把它吐出来了<ref>{{cite web |last=Van |first=Jonathan |url=http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#1 |title=Taylor Swift: The Single Life – Magazine |work=Vogue |accessdate=2012-07-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120615054523/http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#1 |archivedate=2012-06-15 }}</ref>。”她钦佩西蒙“词曲创作和诚实”：“她很情绪化，但也很坚强<ref>{{cite news |last=Adams |first=Cameron |url=http://www.news.com.au/entertainment/music/taylor-swift-is-happy-to-be-your-break-up-musician/story-e6frfn09-1226644234716 |title=Taylor Swift is happy to be your break-up musician |publisher=News.com.au |date=2013-05-16 |accessdate=2013-06-10 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130519111037/http://www.news.com.au/entertainment/music/taylor-swift-is-happy-to-be-your-break-up-musician/story-e6frfn09-1226644234716 |archivedate=2013-05-19 }}</ref>。”

=== 歌曲主题和风格 ===
主题上，《卫报》指出泰勒絲在她的前两张专辑中“难以置信地擅长将青少年生活看作是一种令人向往、棕褐色的怀念<ref name="guardian1" />。”《纽约杂志》指出，很少有创作型歌手能缔造“明确地描绘他们的青少年生活的唱片……离她（泰勒絲）最近的前辈可能是六十年代的[[布赖恩·威尔逊|布赖恩·威尔逊]]，在她（泰勒絲）到来之前，布莱恩是一个真正的青春期性格导演<ref>{{cite web |url=http://nymag.com/arts/popmusic/features/68796/index1.html |title=Taylor Swift on Her Third Album, 'Speak Now' – ''New York'' |work=New York |date=2010-10-08 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131221020459/http://nymag.com/arts/popmusic/features/68796/index1.html |archivedate=2013-12-21 }}</ref>。”[[珍妮斯·艾恩|珍妮斯·艾恩]]也被用作对比<ref name="newyorker2" />。

泰勒絲的第二张专辑《無懼的愛》出现了童话般的想象。她探讨了“童话故事和爱情的现实之间”的脱节<ref>{{cite web |last=Kelly |first=James |url=http://www.accessatlanta.com/atlanta-music/taylor-swift-writing-her-124301.html |title=Taylor Swift: Writing her own songs – and rules |publisher=accessAtlanta |date=2009-08-26 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120626043844/http://www.accessatlanta.com/atlanta-music/taylor-swift-writing-her-124301.html |archivedate=2012-06-26 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |author=Lindsey Roznovsky |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1599049/taylor-swifts-fascination-with-fairy-tales-comes-through-on-new-album.jhtml |title=News : Taylor Swift's Fascination With Fairy Tales Comes Through on New Album |publisher=CMT |date=2011-11-10 |accessdate=2012-07-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121020233804/http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1599049/taylor-swifts-fascination-with-fairy-tales-comes-through-on-new-album.jhtml |archivedate=2012-10-20 }}</ref>。她在后来的专辑探讨更为成年人的关系<ref name="usatoday1" />。除了浪漫和爱情，泰勒絲的歌曲还探讨父母子女的关系（如《完美的一天》（{{lang|en|The Best Day}}）、《长不大》（{{lang|en|Never Grow Up}}）、《[[Ronan_(歌曲)|罗南]]》（{{lang|en|Ronan}}））、友情（如《[[十五岁|十五岁]]》、《呼吸》（{{lang|en|Breathe}}）、《[[22_(歌曲)|二十二岁]]》、《[[壞到底_(歌曲)|敌对]]》、《[[我的错|我的錯]]》）<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.lasvegasweekly.com/news/2009/dec/30/microwaving-tragedy-marriage-romance-and-romantici/ |title=Microwaving a tragedy: The marriage of romance and romanticism in '00s pop |work=Las Vegas Weekly |accessdate=2012-08-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111229182014/http://www.lasvegasweekly.com/news/2009/dec/30/microwaving-tragedy-marriage-romance-and-romantici/ |archivedate=2011-12-29 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |last=Rotman |first=Natalie |url=http://readingeagle.com/article.aspx?id=154886 |title=Colbie Caillat has 'Breakthrough' with sophomore CD |publisher=Readingeagle.com |date=2009-01-09 |accessdate=2012-08-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131221001640/http://www2.readingeagle.com/article.aspx?id=154886 |archivedate=2013-12-21 }}</ref>、逃离（如《外面》（{{lang|en|The Outside}}）、《一席之地》（{{lang|en|A Place in This World}}）、《用微笑做自己》（{{lang|en|Tied Together with a Smile}}）、《[[太刻薄|太刻薄]]》、《[[通通甩掉|通通甩掉]]》、《[[看是你逼我的|看是你逼我的]]》）、成名（如《幸运儿》（{{lang|en|The Lucky One}}）、《藏身之地》（{{lang|en|I Know Places}}）、《[[游戏终结|最後關頭]]》）和寫給粉絲的歌（如《改变》（{{lang|en|Change}}）、《[[直到永遠_(泰勒絲歌曲)|直到永远]]》（{{lang|en|Long Live}}）、《[[新年日_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|新年願望]]》）<ref name="sessionsinterview">{{cite web|url=http://music.aol.com/sessions/taylor-swift-change-sessions/ |title=Taylor Swift Sessions Interview |first=Melinda |last=Newman |date=2008-12-19 |work=AOL |accessdate=2011-03-25 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110220123333/http://music.aol.com/sessions/taylor-swift-change-sessions/ |archivedate=2011-02-20 |deadurl=yes }}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.creme.co.nz/features/94/ |title=Swifty's secret song stories ... – Features – Creme Magazine |publisher=Creme.co.nz |accessdate=2012-08-17 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130208020403/http://www.creme.co.nz/features/94/ |archivedate=2013-02-08 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。

据称泰勒絲所定义的品質是詞曲作家要“有表达和紧抓稍纵即逝的情感和印象的判断力，用怀旧的礼物先发制人（有时甚至是未来的），她知道总有一天自己也会成为过去<ref>{{cite web |last=Fox |first=Jesse |url=http://www.metropulse.com/news/2011/jun/29/you-must-remember-this-taylor-swift-built-mega-sel/ |title=You Must Remember This: Taylor Swift Has Built a Mega-Selling Career Out of Carefully Observed Moments |publisher=Metro Pulse |date=2011-06-29 |accessdate=2012-07-12 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140712165207/http://www.metropulse.com/news/2011/jun/29/you-must-remember-this-taylor-swift-built-mega-sel/ |archivedate=2014-07-12 }}</ref>。”泰勒絲经常利用“一气呵成的语句暗示大量和糟糕不适合用于歌曲的事物及增强或颠覆表面性叙事的事物”<ref name="villagevoice2" />。《纽约人》杂志曾表示，她的歌“尽管不是颠覆性的，但有一定的复杂性……青涩的歌曲夹杂着前程破灭的暗示<ref>{{cite web |last=Widdicombe |first=Lizzie |url=http://www.newyorker.com/reporting/2011/10/10/111010fa_fact_widdicombe |title=Taylor Swift Makes Primness Lucrative |work=The New Yorker |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120514122757/http://www.newyorker.com/reporting/2011/10/10/111010fa_fact_widdicombe |archivedate=2012-05-14 }}</ref>。”

在结构上，《Slate》杂志指出泰勒絲“毫无费力、异于常人地掌握流行乐坛的公约：很少有词曲作者比她建立的结构还要好<ref>{{cite web |last=Keefe |first=Jonathan |url=http://www.slantmagazine.com/house/2012/08/single-review-taylor-swift-we-are-never-ever-getting-back-together/ |title=Single Review: Taylor Swift, "We Are Never Ever Getting Back Together" |publisher=SlantMagazine.com |accessdate=2012-08-16 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120818042138/http://www.slantmagazine.com/house/2012/08/single-review-taylor-swift-we-are-never-ever-getting-back-together/ |archivedate=2012-08-18 }}</ref>。”《滚石》称她为“词曲作者的学者，对主歌-副歌-连结结构有着直觉上的天赋<ref name="rollingstone2">{{cite web |author=Jody Rosen |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/fearless-20081113 |title=Fearless |work=Rolling Stone |date=2008-11-13 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120815082027/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/fearless-20081113 |archivedate=2012-08-15 }}</ref>。”《乡村之声》指出泰勒絲频繁采用了三段主歌[[视觉暂留|视觉暂留]]逆转<ref name="villagevoice2">{{cite web |author=Theon Weber |url=http://www.villagevoice.com/2010-11-03/music/the-iceberg-songs-of-taylor-swift/ |title=The Iceberg Songs of Taylor Swift |location=New York |work=The Village Voice |date=2010-11-03 |accessdate=2012-07-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120707060458/http://www.villagevoice.com/2010-11-03/music/the-iceberg-songs-of-taylor-swift/ |archivedate=2012-07-07 }}</ref>。在画面感方面，重复是泰勒絲歌曲创作的显著特点。《卫报》表示，“她花了太多时间去亲吻雨露，似乎她还没有患上{{le|战壕脚|Trench foot}}是种奇迹<ref name="guardian1" />。”作者补充道，“泰勒絲的功劳是她在（第四张）专辑中探索出一种全新的抒情主题<ref name="slantmagazine.com" />。”《{{le|美国词曲作家|American Songwriter}}》杂志指出泰勒絲是“一位伟大的词曲作家，所写的歌无与伦比、敏锐度几乎不自然……甚至连她最早的素材有着全面的特点——也许是一丝不苟——遣词和蓄意的旋律结构，不带一丝慵懒的韵味或是漫无目的的曲调<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/6/ |title=Taylor Swift: The Garden In The Machine |publisher=American Songwriter |date=2011-05-02 |accessdate=2012-08-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111220052403/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/6/ |archivedate=2011-12-20 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/3/ |title=Taylor Swift: The Garden In The Machine |publisher=American Songwriter |date=2011-05-02 |accessdate=2012-08-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130807054922/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2011/05/taylor-swift-the-garden-in-the-machine/3/ |archivedate=2013-08-07 }}</ref>。”尽管对泰勒絲作品的评价“几乎全是正面的”，但《纽约人》称她一般被形容为“不算[[鲍勃·迪伦|鲍勃·迪伦]]那样有远见的音乐人，而更像个熟练的技术工人”<ref name="newyorker2" />。

{{Quote|「对于一名描写自己的感情的女性来说，被描述成有点黏人、疯狂、不顾一切地想要让你跟她结婚生子的女友，这让我认为可能是值得庆祝的事情——女性描写自身感情的忏悔方式——就是赶走它、翻转它、把它缠绕到一些坦率地说有点性别歧视的事物里。」— ''泰勒絲回应对她的歌词创作的批评''<ref name="Zach Johnson">{{cite web |last=Johnson |first=Zach |title=Taylor Swift: I'm Not a "Clingy, Insane, Desperate Girlfriend" |url=http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/news/taylor-swift-im-not-a-clingy-insane-desperate-girlfriend-201353 |work=Us Weekly |accessdate=2013-06-19 |date=2013-03-05 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130615133346/http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/news/taylor-swift-im-not-a-clingy-insane-desperate-girlfriend-201353 |archivedate=2013-06-15 }}</ref>}}

泰勒絲在她的作品中采用了自传细节<ref>{{cite news |last=Farley |first=Christopher John |title=Taylor Swift's Solo Act |url=http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304510704575562401576663866.html |accessdate=2012-05-24 |newspaper=The Wall Street Journal |date=2010-10-22 |location=Nashville, Tenn |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120430065718/http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052702304510704575562401576663866.html |archivedate=2012-04-30 }}</ref>。小时候听音乐时，让他感到困惑的是，“当我知道某人的私生活要发生些什么，他们却没有在他们的音乐中处理这个问题<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2008/11/09/arts/music/09cara.html?pagewanted=all |title=My Music, MySpace, My Life |newspaper=The New York Times |date=2008-11-07 |accessdate=2012-05-28 |last=Caramanica |first=Jon |location=Chattanooga, Tennessee |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130522025522/http://www.nytimes.com/2008/11/09/arts/music/09cara.html?pagewanted=all |archivedate=2013-05-22 }}</ref>。”

《纽约时报》认为，“伸张正义是泰勒絲女士们存在的理由<ref name="nytimes1">{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2010/10/24/arts/music/24swift.html?pagewanted=all |title=Taylor Swift Is Angry, Darn It |newspaper=The New York Times |date=2010-10-20 |accessdate=2012-07-02 |first=Jon |last=Caramanica |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120911131428/http://www.nytimes.com/2010/10/24/arts/music/24swift.html?pagewanted=all |archivedate=2012-09-11 }}</ref>。”在她的歌曲中，泰勒絲经常处理高中三年和近年来同行名人的难以言表的压榨<ref name="nytimes1" />。梅尔将“亲爱的约翰”的主角假定为自己，认为这首歌羞辱了他：“我认为是一种廉价的词曲创作。我知道她是世界上最炙手可熱的明星之一，我不是那种會落井下石的人，但我认为你寫完歌摩拳擦掌的想著，'等著看他接這一招！'是在濫用你的才華<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/john-mayer-taylor-swifts-dear-john-song-humiliated-me-20120606 |title=John Mayer: Taylor Swift's 'Dear John' Song 'Humiliated Me' |work=Rolling Stone |date=2012-06-06 |accessdate=2012-06-24 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120623203359/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/john-mayer-taylor-swifts-dear-john-song-humiliated-me-20120606 |archivedate=2012-06-23 }}</ref>。”《乡村之声》已经淡化了泰勒絲作曲的这一方面：“教人们读懂歌词就像是一位爱出风头的教授所做。这已危及到对泰勒絲的天赋的由衷赞美。这不是忏悔，但却是戏剧性的<ref>{{cite web |author=Theon Weber |url=http://www.villagevoice.com/2010-11-03/music/the-iceberg-songs-of-taylor-swift/ |title=The Iceberg Songs of Taylor Swift – Page 1 – Music – New York |work=The Village Voice |date=2010-11-03 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120707060458/http://www.villagevoice.com/2010-11-03/music/the-iceberg-songs-of-taylor-swift/ |archivedate=2012-07-07 }}</ref>。”《纽约杂志》认为媒体监督她使用自传细节是“性别上的歧视，由于这不用问她的男同行们”：“了解泰勒絲这位拒绝向曾经问过她的记者认错不那么漂亮的女孩能够让人释然<ref>{{cite web |url=http://nymag.com/thecut/2012/11/stop-asking-taylor-swift-to-apologize.html |title=Stop Asking Taylor Swift to Apologize for Writing Songs About Ex-Boyfriends – The Cut |work=New York |date=2012-11-26 |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121127200757/http://nymag.com/thecut/2012/11/stop-asking-taylor-swift-to-apologize.html |archivedate=2012-11-27 }}</ref>。”

这位歌手她自己也表示，她所有的歌曲都是不真实的<ref>{{cite news |url=http://voices.washingtonpost.com/postrock/2008/02/her_song_talking_taylor_swift_1.html |title=Her Song: Talking Taylor Swift – Post Rock |work=The Washington Post |accessdate=2012-07-30}}</ref>，经常要靠观察<ref name="amazon1">{{cite web |url=http://www.amazon.com/Taylor-Swift/dp/product-description/B000VUFJ4Q |title=Taylor Swift: Taylor Swift: Music |publisher=Amazon.com |accessdate=2012-08-17 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140908124655/http://www.amazon.com/Taylor-Swift/dp/product-description/B000VUFJ4Q |archivedate=2014-09-08 }}</ref>。除了她的自带的线索标签，泰勒絲尽量不去具体谈论歌手“因为这些人都是真实的。你尝试去审视自己算哪根葱敢当作曲家，就不会完全被其他人从公交车上挤下来<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2012/11/18/magazine/the-many-insecurities-of-taylor-swift.html |work=The New York Times |first=Susan |last=Dominus |title=The Many Insecurities of Taylor Swift |date=2012-11-16 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121122131116/http://www.nytimes.com/2012/11/18/magazine/the-many-insecurities-of-taylor-swift.html |archivedate=2012-11-22 }}</ref>。”

=== 音乐和演唱风格 ===
泰勒絲的音乐類型有流行樂、流行舞曲、電子流行、合成器流行、鄉村樂及鄉村流行<ref name="rollingstone1">{{cite web |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/artists/taylor-swift/biography |title=Taylor Swift | Bio, Pictures, Videos |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120709093054/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/artists/taylor-swift/biography |archivedate=2012-07-09 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |author=Ann Powers |url=http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/music_blog/2010/10/album-review-taylor-swifts-speak-now.html |title=Album review: Taylor Swift's 'Speak Now' – ''Los Angeles Times'' |work=Los Angeles Times |date=2010-10-25 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20101028003032/http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/music_blog/2010/10/album-review-taylor-swifts-speak-now.html |archivedate=2010-10-28 }}</ref>，拥有从C3到D6三个八度的抒情[[女高音|女高音]]音域<ref>{{cite web|title=Vocal Profile: Taylor Swift|url=http://thevocalpoint.tumblr.com/post/160287526280/vocal-profile-taylor-swift|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170730171401/http://thevocalpoint.tumblr.com/post/160287526280/vocal-profile-taylor-swift|archivedate=2017-07-30}}</ref>。之前她自称乡村歌手，直至2014年《1989》发行，这被她称为“在音乐层面上有凝聚力的流行专辑<ref name="independent2">{{cite news |last=Mclean |first=Craig |url=http://www.independent.co.uk/arts-entertainment/music/features/taylor-swift-maybe-i-should-just-lighten-up-2112052.html |title=Taylor Swift: 'Maybe I should just lighten up' – Features – Music |work=The Independent |date=2010-10-24 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |location=London |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150722060250/http://www.independent.co.uk/arts-entertainment/music/features/taylor-swift-maybe-i-should-just-lighten-up-2112052.html |archivedate=2015-07-22 }}</ref><ref name="tennessean.com">{{cite web |first=Peter |last=Cooper |url=http://www.tennessean.com/story/entertainment/music/peter-cooper/2014/10/26/taylor-swift-reaches-turning-point/17871775/ |title=Taylor Swift reaches a turning point with '1989' |publisher=The Tennessean |date=2014-10-26 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/6klhMwBEm?url=http://www.tennessean.com/story/entertainment/music/peter-cooper/2014/10/26/taylor-swift-reaches-turning-point/17871775/ |archivedate=2016-09-24 }}</ref>。”尽管《1989》及《舉世盛名》走流行乐路线<ref name="Slam">{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift Slams Hackers' Nude Photo Claims|url=http://www.accesshollywood.com/taylor-swift-slams-hackers-nude-photo-claims_article_103356|website=Access Hollywood|publisher=NBCUniversal, Inc|accessdate=2015-01-30|date=2015-01-28|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150130011616/http://www.accesshollywood.com/taylor-swift-slams-hackers-nude-photo-claims_article_103356|archivedate=2015-01-30}}</ref>，但泰勒絲仍打算在未来继续录制乡村音乐专辑<ref name="tennessean.com"/>。

《滚石》断言，“她可能会在乡村电台上表演，但她迄今为止为数不多的真正的摇滚明星<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/lists/women-who-rock-the-50-greatest-albums-of-all-time-20120622/taylor-swift-speak-now-19691231 |title=Women Who Rock: The 50 Greatest Albums of All Time: Taylor Swift, 'Speak Now' |work=Rolling Stone |accessdate=2012-07-30 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120625070205/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/lists/women-who-rock-the-50-greatest-albums-of-all-time-20120622/taylor-swift-speak-now-19691231 |archivedate=2012-06-25 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。”《纽约时报》指出，“泰勒絲的音乐中没有很多对乡村乐的暗示——几个班卓琴扫弦，在舞台上穿着一双牛仔靴，抱着一个痴痴的吉他——但她迷人、脆弱地表达出独一无二的纳什维尔<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/22/arts/music/pop-and-rock-listings-july-22-28.html |title=Pop and Rock Listings July 22 – 28 |newspaper=The New York Times |date=2011-07-21 |accessdate=2012-07-12 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120128232427/http://www.nytimes.com/2011/07/22/arts/music/pop-and-rock-listings-july-22-28.html |archivedate=2012-01-28 }}</ref>。”《纽约客》认为她“被认为是纳什维尔乡村流行乐传统的一部分，不仅在于她写的叙事曲有着旋律上的识别度和戏剧般的形态——这是纳什维尔人的惯用手法<ref>{{cite web|last=Frere |first=Sasha |url=http://www.newyorker.com/arts/critics/musical/2008/11/10/081110crmu_music_frerejones?currentPage=all |title=Prodigy |work=The New Yorker |accessdate=2012-07-30 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20081218095021/https://www.newyorker.com/arts/critics/musical/2008/11/10/081110crmu_music_frerejones?currentPage=all |archivedate=2008-12-18 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。”《卫报》指出泰勒絲“斯堪的纳维亚人流行乐工厂做无用功的效率制作潦草地制作旋律<ref name="guardian1">{{cite news |author=Alexis Petridis |url=http://www.guardian.co.uk/music/2009/mar/06/taylor-swift-fearless-album-review |title=Pop review: Taylor Swift: Fearless |work=The Guardian |accessdate=2012-06-24 |location=London |date=2009-03-06 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120424210930/http://www.guardian.co.uk/music/2009/mar/06/taylor-swift-fearless-album-review |archivedate=2012-04-24 }}</ref>”。

泰勒絲的声线被认为是“甜蜜但柔弱”<ref name="schillaci1">{{cite news |url=http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/review/taylor-swift-at-staples-center-227968 |work=The Hollywood Reporter |first=Sophie A. |last=Schillaci |title=Taylor Swift at Staples Center: Concert Review |date=2011-08-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160304025206/http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/review/taylor-swift-at-staples-center-227968 |archivedate=2016-03-04 }}</ref>。在录音棚里录音，《洛杉矶时报》称泰勒絲所“定义”的发音姿势像是“滑落的线条，就像一声知足的叹息或像是挑眉毛，给她那受到只顾享乐的年轻女性欢迎的热单带来轻松亲密的空气<ref name="LAT" />。”《滚石》在《爱的告白》的乐评中表示：“泰勒絲的声线不受影响得足以掩饰她作为一名歌手是多么的会算计，为了应付害羞的女孩试图表白的经典模式歌词，她降低了她的声音<ref>{{cite web |author=Rob Sheffield |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/speak-now-20101026 |title=Speak Now |work=Rolling Stone |date=2010-10-26 |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://www.webcitation.org/5vpXbTcTi?url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/albumreviews/speak-now-20101026 |archivedate=2011-01-18 }}</ref>。”在《爱的告白》的另一篇乐评中，《乡村之声》指出她措辞是以前的那种“平淡混乱的，但现在改了。她仍然发出紧张和柔软的声音，而且经常迷失在音调中，把某些人搞疯，但她学会了如何让歌词听起来像是它们的本来意思<ref name="Voice" />。”

在演唱会布置方面，《[[好莱坞报道者|好莱坞报道者]]》称泰勒絲“尽其所能，但肯定不会出现像[[克里斯蒂娜·阿奎莱拉|克里斯蒂娜·阿奎莱拉]]或[[凯莉·安德伍德|凯莉·安德伍德]]的那种旗鼓相当的场面<ref name="schillaci1" />。”她的演唱会唱功在2009年被描述成“平淡”、“细微，有时像个小马驹那样的摇摇晃晃<ref>{{cite news|url=http://blogs.reuters.com/fanfare/2009/11/17/taylor-swift-fearless-or-tone-less/ |agency=Reuters |date=2009-11-17 |title=Taylor Swift – "Fearless" or tone-less? |accessdate=2012-07-02 |first=Jill |last=Serjeant |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20091121141029/http://blogs.reuters.com/fanfare/2009/11/17/taylor-swift-fearless-or-tone-less |archivedate=2009-11-21 |deadurl=yes }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://watching-tv.ew.com/2009/11/12/cma-awards-best-worst/ |work=Entertainment Weekly |date=2009-11-12 |title=CMA Awards best and worst, starring Taylor Swift, the ghost of Kanye West, and Carrie Underwood's purple sequined hot-pants |first=Ken |last=Tucker |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141205123403/http://watching-tv.ew.com/2009/11/12/cma-awards-best-worst/ |archivedate=2014-12-05 }}</ref>。“然而，泰勒絲拒绝用{{le|自动调音修正|Auto-Tune}}软件修音的态度获得赞赏<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.boston.com/ae/music/articles/2010/10/24/taylor_swift_comes_into_her_own_with_speak_now/ |work=Boston Globe |first=James |last=Reed |title=Swift's ascent continues with arrival of new album |date=2010-10-24 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150626004234/http://www.boston.com/ae/music/articles/2010/10/24/taylor_swift_comes_into_her_own_with_speak_now/ |archivedate=2015-06-26 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://in.reuters.com/article/2009/11/20/idINIndia-44133520091120 |agency=Reuters |title=Taylor Swift's dream year brings out naysayers |date=2009-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150712063429/http://in.reuters.com/article/2009/11/20/idINIndia-44133520091120 |archivedate=2015-07-12 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.savingcountrymusic.com/keys-to-taylor-swifts-success-every-artist-can-learn-from |title=Keys to Taylor Swift's Success Every Artist Can Learn From " Saving Country Music |publisher=Savingcountrymusic.com |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120606194329/http://www.savingcountrymusic.com/keys-to-taylor-swifts-success-every-artist-can-learn-from |archivedate=2012-06-06 }}</ref>。

在接受《纽约人》采访时，泰勒絲称她的主要特点是当詞曲作家：“我写的歌、我的声音只是亲近那些歌词的一种方式<ref name="widdicombe1" /><ref>{{cite web |last=DeLuca |first=Dan |title=Focused on 'great songs' Taylor Swift isn't thinking about "the next level" or Joe Jonas gossip |url=http://articles.philly.com/2008-11-11/news/25256467_1_big-machine-records-joe-jonas-country-music-association-awards/3 |page=3 |work=Philadelphia Daily News |accessdate=2012-04-17 |date=2008-11-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121118234627/http://articles.philly.com/2008-11-11/news/25256467_1_big-machine-records-joe-jonas-country-music-association-awards/3 |archivedate=2012-11-18 }}</ref>。“波尔切塔在2010年承认泰勒絲“并不是最好的技术型歌手”，但形容她是“我们所以知道的最好的沟通者<ref>{{cite web |url=http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2010/02/01/taylor-swift-has-mixed-reviews-from-grammy-night/ |title=Taylor Swift gets mixed reviews at Grammys |work=The Tennessean |date=2010-02-10 |accessdate=2012-06-24 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150713203631/http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2010/02/01/taylor-swift-has-mixed-reviews-from-grammy-night/ |archivedate=2015-07-13 }}</ref>。”泰勒絲的声乐表现让人们感到担心，她已经“投入大量的精力”去改进它<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/953737/taylor-swift-the-billboard-cover-story |title=Taylor Swift: The Billboard Cover Story |work=Billboard (magazine) |date=2010-10-15 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |first=Tom |last=Roland |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20101018200303/http://www.billboard.com/features/taylor-swift-the-billboard-cover-story-1004121338.story |archivedate=2010-10-18 }}</ref>。另据2010年的报道，她还在继续上声乐课<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2010/10/24/arts/music/24swift.html?_r=1&pagewanted=all |title=Taylor Swift Is Angry, Darn It |newspaper=The New York Times |date=2010-10-20 |accessdate=2012-06-24 |first=Jon |last=Caramanica |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130522033519/http://www.nytimes.com/2010/10/24/arts/music/24swift.html?_r=1&pagewanted=all |archivedate=2013-05-22 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |last=Kelly |first=James |url=http://www.accessatlanta.com/atlanta-music/taylor-swift-writing-her-124301.html |title=Taylor Swift: Writing her own songs – and rules |publisher=accessAtlanta |date=2009-08-26 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120626043844/http://www.accessatlanta.com/atlanta-music/taylor-swift-writing-her-124301.html |archivedate=2012-06-26 }}</ref>。她表示自己唯一对表演感到紧张是在“我不清楚观众如何看待我，就像是在颁奖典礼上”时<ref>'Country Strong', Teen Vogue, August 2011</ref>。但到至今，泰勒絲的唱功在這幾年有相當明顯的進步，甚至唱功變得特別好，一年一年不斷的突破。

=== 政治立场 ===
2008年[[美国总统选举|美国总统选举]]期间，泰勒絲推广“每位女性都算数”（Every Woman Counts），积极推动参与政治生活，她因此成为了参与PSA为你的国家（PSA for the Vote （For Your）Country）投票活动的乡村明星之一<ref>{{Cite AV media|date=May 30, 2008|title=Every Woman Counts: Funny Taylor Swift Interview Before 2008 ACM Awards|url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MaJLtyYFiBQ|publisher=[[Lifetime_(TV_network)|Lifetime]]|accessdate=August 2, 2016|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20101105043915/http://www.youtube.com//watch?v=MaJLtyYFiBQ|archivedate=November 5, 2010}}</ref>。她表示：“我认为尝试着带动人们投票不是我的分内事”<ref name="Rolling Stone 2008-12-08" />。[[贝拉克·奥巴马|贝拉克·奥巴马]]就职演说过后，她向《滚石》杂志表明支持总统的立场：“我一生从未看到过这个国家对这个政治决定如此高兴。我很庆幸，这是我首次参与选举<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/the-very-pink-very-perfect-life-of-taylor-swift-20090305|title=The Very Pink, Very Perfect Life of Taylor Swift|last=Grigoriadis|first=Vanessa|date=March 5, 2009|work=Rolling Stone|accessdate=August 2, 2016|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160724194744/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/the-very-pink-very-perfect-life-of-taylor-swift-20090305|archivedate=July 24, 2016}}</ref>。”

2012年接受采访时，泰勒絲表示她尽管让自己“尽可能受教育和了解”，但还是不会讨论政治，担心这会影响到其他人<ref>{{Cite news|last=Macsai|first=Dan|date=October 19, 2012|url=http://entertainment.time.com/2012/10/19/taylor-swift-on-going-pop-ignoring-the-gossip-and-the-best-worst-nickname-shes-ever-had/?iid=ent-main-lede|title=Taylor Swift on Going Pop, Ignoring the Gossip and the Best (Worst) Nickname She's Ever Had|work=Time|accessdate=August 2, 2016|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160527063803/http://entertainment.time.com/2012/10/19/taylor-swift-on-going-pop-ignoring-the-gossip-and-the-best-worst-nickname-shes-ever-had/?iid=ent-main-lede|archivedate=May 27, 2016}}</ref>。写到媒体给公开站政治立场的泰勒絲所带来的压力时，《[[外交政策|外交政策]]》认为泰勒絲“刻意回避政治议题”<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.politico.com/magazine/story/2017/12/06/the-weird-campaign-to-get-taylor-swift-to-denounce-donald-trump-215994|title=The Weird Campaign to Get Taylor Swift to Denounce Donald Trump|last=Glatsky|first=Genevieve|work=[[Politico|Politico]]|date=December 6, 2017|accessdate=December 8, 2017|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171206211450/https://www.politico.com/magazine/story/2017/12/06/the-weird-campaign-to-get-taylor-swift-to-denounce-donald-trump-215994|archivedate=December 6, 2017}}</ref>。实际上，泰勒絲和[[肯尼迪家族|肯尼迪家族]]有过密切交往<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.eonline.com/news/334846/taylor-swift-kennedys-should-be-so-lucky-to-have-her-in-the-family-says-boyfriend-conor-s-grandmother|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20151102061702/http://www.eonline.com/news/334846/taylor-swift-kennedys-should-be-so-lucky-to-have-her-in-the-family-says-boyfriend-conor-s-grandmother|archivedate=November 2, 2015|title=Taylor Swift: Kennedys Should Be So Lucky to Have Her in the Family, Says Boyfriend Conor's Grandmother|last=Malkin|first=Marc|publisher=E!|accessdate=November 10, 2015}}</ref>，曾一度表示钦佩{{le|埃塞尔·肯尼迪|Ethel Kennedy}}<ref name="single life">{{Cite news|last=Van Meter|first=Jonathan|url=http://www.vogue.com/865383/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#1|title=Taylor Swift: The Single Life|work=Vogue|accessdate=July 3, 2012|date=January 17, 2012|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140908124308/http://www.vogue.com/865383/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#1|archivedate=September 8, 2014}}</ref>。泰勒絲是一位[[女权主义|女权主义]]者，也曾公开反对歧视[[LGBT|LGBT]]<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/aug/23/taylor-swift-shake-it-off|title=Taylor Swift: 'Sexy? Not on my radar'|last=Hoby|first=Hermione|date=August 23, 2014|work=[[The_Guardian|The Guardian]]|accessdate=May 29, 2015|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150610104506/http://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/aug/23/taylor-swift-shake-it-off|archivedate=June 10, 2015}}</ref>。2008年{{le|拉里·金谋杀案|Murder of Larry King}}发生后，她参与{{le|GLSEN|GLSEN}}电视台打击[[仇恨犯罪|仇恨犯罪]]公众节目录制<ref name="eonline1">{{Cite web|url=http://uk.eonline.com/news/59855/portia-joins-ellen-to-stop-the-hate|title=Portia Joins Ellen To Stop The Hate|last=Malkin|first=Marc|date=March 10, 2010|publisher=E!|accessdate=July 12, 2012|deadurl=no|archiveurl=http://archive.wikiwix.com/cache/20120712123129/http://uk.eonline.com/news/59855/portia-joins-ellen-to-stop-the-hate|archivedate=July 12, 2012}}</ref>。拉里·金去世周年祭，泰勒絲告诉《[[17_(杂志)|十七岁]]》杂志，父母告诉她，“永远不要按照伴侣、肤色或宗教来评判其他人<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.seventeen.com/college/advice/mission-taylor-swift|title=Taylor Swift's Mission: Take a Stand Against Hate!|date=March 28, 2009|last=Koday|first=Dan|work=Seventeen|accessdate=August 30, 2012|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140129013422/http://www.seventeen.com/college/advice/mission-taylor-swift|archivedate=January 29, 2014}}</ref>。”泰勒絲反霸凌歌曲《[[太刻薄|太刻薄]]》的音乐录影带部分提到了高中校园的[[同性恋恐惧|同性恋恐惧]]。录影带获提名2011年MTV音乐录影带大奖社交活动奖<ref name="Hawgood 2010-11-05" /><ref>{{Cite news|url=http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/08/04/idINIndia-58624620110804|title=MTV adds social activism category to VMAs|date=August 4, 2011|agency=Reuters|last1=Mayberry|first1=Carly|last2=Tourtellotte|first2=Bob|accessdate=August 30, 2012|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121012205523/http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/08/04/idINIndia-58624620110804|archivedate=October 12, 2012}}</ref>。《纽约时报》认为，她参与到“为同性恋歌迷提供原声带的青年女性（大多数很直率）的浪潮中，使他们在文化信息汹涌和困顿的年代逐渐认同自己的身份”<ref name="Hawgood 2010-11-05" />。

[[2018年美国中期选举|2018年美国中期选举]]前夕，泰勒絲首次公开拥护两位[[民主党_(美国)|民主党]]的公职候选者<ref>{{cite news|author=Zimmerman, Amy|url=https://www.thedailybeast.com/taylor-swift-finally-got-political-why-now|title=Taylor Swift Finally Got Political. Why Now?|work=The Daily Beast|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20181009012452/https://www.thedailybeast.com/taylor-swift-finally-got-political-why-now|archivedate=October 9, 2018|date=October 8, 2018|accessdate=October 9, 2018}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|author=Parkinson, Hannah Jane|title=Taylor Swift finally makes a political intervention – will it sway voters?|url=https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2018/oct/08/taylor-swift-political-intervention-sway-voters-singer-vote-democrat-midterm-elections-millennials|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20181008172804/https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2018/oct/08/taylor-swift-political-intervention-sway-voters-singer-vote-democrat-midterm-elections-millennials|archivedate=October 8, 2018|work=The Guardian|date=October 8, 2018|accessdate=October 9, 2018}}</ref>：竞争连任的国会[[美国众议院|众议员]][[吉姆·库珀|吉姆·库珀]]和前竞选[[美国参议院|参议员]]的前{{le|田纳西州州长|Governor of Tennessee}}[[菲尔·布雷德森|菲尔·布雷德森]]。然而，她公开反对布雷德森的对手、[[共和党_(美国)|共和党]]国会议员{{le|玛莎·布雷克本|Marsha Blackburn}}，表示她的投票记录让她“胆寒”、“震惊”，而美国总统[[唐纳德·特朗普|唐纳德·特朗普]]则发推特表示自己对泰勒的歌曲的喜爱程度已经减少了18%。她渴望LGBTQ权利及性别种族平等，谴责系统性种族主义<ref>{{cite news|author=Buitrago, Juan|title=What about her reputation? Taylor Swift's political stance draws praise, backlash |url=https://www.usatoday.com/story/life/people/2018/10/08/taylor-swift-political-phil-bredesen-endorsement-marsha-blackburn/1563958002/ |date=October 8, 2018 |accessdate=October 8, 2018 |newspaper=USA Today}}</ref>。Vote.org提到泰勒絲发帖24小时后，有65000人注册登记为选民，随着最后限期的临近，登记数量出现前所未有的增长<ref name="France18">{{cite news |last1=France |first1=Lisa Respers |title=Voter registration reportedly spikes after Taylor Swift post |url=https://www.cnn.com/2018/10/09/entertainment/taylor-swift-voter-registration/index.html|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20181009194930/https://edition.cnn.com/2018/10/09/entertainment/taylor-swift-voter-registration/index.html|archivedate=October 9, 2018|accessdate=October 9, 2018 |publisher=CNN |date=October 9, 2018}}</ref><ref name="Haag18">{{cite news |last1=Haag |first1=Matthew |title=Voter Registrations Spike as Deadlines Loom. Taylor Swift Had Something to Do With It. |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2018/10/09/us/politics/taylor-swift-voter-registration.html|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20181009210812/https://www.nytimes.com/2018/10/09/us/politics/taylor-swift-voter-registration.html |archivedate=October 9, 2018|accessdate=October 10, 2018 |work=The New York Times |date=October 9, 2018 |language=en}}</ref>。斯威夫特在{{le|2018年全美音乐奖|American Music Awards of 2018}}年度艺人的获奖感言中，继续鼓励歌迷参加中期选举投票<ref name="AMA Record">{{cite magazine|author=Havens, Lyndsey|title=Taylor Swift Breaks an All-Time AMA Record -- And Urges People to Vote In Midterm Elections|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/events/amas/8479150/taylor-swift-breaks-record-most-AMA-wins-woman-urges-voting-midterms|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20181010082243/https://www.billboard.com/articles/events/amas/8479150/taylor-swift-breaks-record-most-AMA-wins-woman-urges-voting-midterms|magazine=Billboard|accessdate=October 10, 2018|archivedate=October 10, 2018|date=October 9, 2018}}</ref>。

=== 公众形象 ===
[[File:5.3.10TaylorSwiftByDavidShankbone.jpg|thumb]]晚宴]]
泰勒絲有着很高的{{le|Q Score|Q Score}}和{{le|戴维-布朗指数|Davie-Brown Index}}，这反映出她在美国有着高水平的公众辨识度（90%）和流行性（80%）<ref>{{cite web |url=http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2012/10/30/taylor-swifts-appeal-soars-with-her-album-sales/ |title=Taylor Swift's appeal soars with her album sales | Tune in Music City |work=The Tennessean |date=2012-10-30 |accessdate=2012-11-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121105161849/http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2012/10/30/taylor-swifts-appeal-soars-with-her-album-sales/ |archivedate=2012-11-05 }}</ref>。这位歌手认为她有着意识到给年轻歌迷带来影响的“责任感”对年轻歌迷的影响是有知觉<ref>{{cite news |url=http://articles.latimes.com/2011/nov/18/news/la-heb-taylor-swift-role-model-20111118 |title=Taylor Swift weighs in on being a role model |work=Los Angeles Times |date=2011-11-18 |accessdate=2012-04-18 |first1=Jeannine |last1=Stein |first2=/ |last2=For |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120715024559/http://articles.latimes.com/2011/nov/18/news/la-heb-taylor-swift-role-model-20111118 |archivedate=2012-07-15 }}</ref>。一名《滚石》记者在2009年在礼仪方面描述泰勒絲：“如果泰勒絲有着（选美）比赛的面孔，那它一定是纹上去的，因为它永远不会掉<ref name="Rolling Stone 2009-03" /><ref>{{cite web |author=Daniel Kreps |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-the-story-behind-rolling-stones-cover-story-20090217 |title=Taylor Swift: The Story Behind Rolling Stone's Cover Story |work=Rolling Stone |date=2009-02-17 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120902225426/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-the-story-behind-rolling-stones-cover-story-20090217 |archivedate=2012-09-02 }}</ref>。”

2012年，《滚石》称泰勒絲“习惯了阿谀奉承”<ref>Taylor in Wonderland by Brian Hiatt, Rolling Stone, page 34, October 2012</ref>，而《好莱坞报道者》称她是“自[[比尔·克林顿|比尔·克林顿]]以来最棒的人（{{lang|en|Best People Person}}）<ref>{{cite news |author=Willman, Chris |url=http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/news/taylor-swift-tapes-vh1-storytellers-379446 |title=Taylor Swift Tapes VH1 'Storytellers' |work=The Hollywood Reporter |date=2012-10-17 |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121123033439/http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/news/taylor-swift-tapes-vh1-storytellers-379446 |archivedate=2012-11-23 }}</ref>。”据称她是那种“发奋图强、野心勃勃的人，愿意让她的事业茁壮成长<ref>{{cite web |last=Tucker |first=Jeremiah |url=http://www.joplinglobe.com/lifestyles/x691728681/Jeremiah-Tucker-Adulthood-takes-toll-on-Swift-s-songwriting |title=Jeremiah Tucker: Adulthood takes toll on Swift's songwriting » Lifestyles » The Joplin Globe, Joplin, MO |publisher=Joplinglobe.com |date=2012-11-02 |accessdate=2013-02-25}}</ref>。”2012年《[[时尚_(杂志)|时尚]]》杂志的封面故事将泰勒絲描述为“聪明、风趣、偶尔有点彻头彻尾的淫秽”<ref name="voguep1">{{cite web |last=Van Meter |first=Jonathan |url=http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#1 |title=Taylor Swift: The Single Life – Magazine |page=1 |work=Vogue |date=2012-01-17 |accessdate=2012-04-18 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120405214259/http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#1 |archivedate=2012-04-05 }}</ref>。Grantland将泰勒絲描述为“书呆子”，“某种意义上有公开的神经质，这种神经质是你在菲斯·希尔或凯莉·安德伍德等金发乡村公主身上从未看到过的。她更像“《[[安妮·霍尔|安妮·霍尔]]》中的[[黛安·基顿|黛安·基顿]]——过分亲切又总想讨好他人，但充满了马不停蹄、紧张和飘飘乎的能量<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.grantland.com/blog/hollywood-prospectus/post/_/id/42556/lana-taylor-and-michelle |title=Lana, Taylor, and Michelle – Hollywood Prospectus Blog |publisher=Grantland |date=2012-02-01 |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120413142941/http://www.grantland.com/blog/hollywood-prospectus/post/_/id/42556/lana-taylor-and-michelle |archivedate=2012-04-13 }}</ref>。”

在推广《1989》期间，泰勒絲开始运用社交媒体直接回应乐迷，并邀请100名乐迷参演《通通甩掉》的音乐录影带<ref>{{cite web|author1=Giana Ciapponi|title=Behind the Scenes of Taylor Swift's New Music Video, "Shake It Off"|url=http://www.ravishly.com/2014/08/20/behind-scenes-taylor-swifts-new-music-video-shake-it|website=ravishly.com|publisher=ravishly.com|accessdate=2015-01-31|date=2014-08-18|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150131052215/http://www.ravishly.com/2014/08/20/behind-scenes-taylor-swifts-new-music-video-shake-it|archivedate=2015-01-31}}</ref>。泰勒絲还给乐迷们私人邮寄节日礼物<ref>{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift's Gift Giving of 2014|url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=j3yyF31jbKo|website=Taylor Swift on YouTube|publisher=Google Inc|accessdate=2015-01-31|format=Video upload|date=2014-12-31|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150129150157/https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=j3yyF31jbKo|archivedate=2015-01-29}}</ref>，并邀请乐迷到家中做客<ref>{{cite web|title=All Shall Love Taylor Swift's Fancy Fourth Of July Party And Despair |url=http://www.pedestrian.tv/news/music/all-shall-love-taylor-swifts-fancy-fourth-of-july-/d309bd24-4f8b-4110-9f10-06dbcb0ead3a.htm |website=pedestrian.tv |accessdate=2015-07-14 |date=2015-05-07 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150705232109/http://www.pedestrian.tv/news/music/all-shall-love-taylor-swifts-fancy-fourth-of-july-/d309bd24-4f8b-4110-9f10-06dbcb0ead3a.htm |archivedate=2015-07-05 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。她表示，乐迷是“我所拥有的最持久且最亲密的关系”<ref>{{cite web|title=Billboard Music Awards: Taylor Swift thanks her fans for being her ‘longest and best relationship’|url=http://metro.co.uk/2013/05/20/billboard-music-awards-taylor-swift-thanks-her-fans-for-being-her-longest-and-best-relationship-3801610/|publisher=Metro|accessdate=2015-04-04|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150410124115/http://metro.co.uk/2013/05/20/billboard-music-awards-taylor-swift-thanks-her-fans-for-being-her-longest-and-best-relationship-3801610/|archivedate=2015-04-10}}</ref>，并定期在颁奖典礼上感谢他们<ref>{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift Tracked Down a Fan at the GRAMMYs and Brought Her Backstage|url=http://www.etonline.com/awards/grammys/159519_taylor_swift_tracked_down_a_fan_at_the_grammys_and_brought_her_backstage/|publisher=ET|accessdate=2015-04-04|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150408111821/http://www.etonline.com/awards/grammys/159519_taylor_swift_tracked_down_a_fan_at_the_grammys_and_brought_her_backstage/|archivedate=2015-04-08}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|title=The Amazing Thing Taylor Swift Did for Two Fans at the iHeartRadio Awards is Just Taylor Being Taylor|url=http://www.seventeen.com/celebrity/news/a29711/the-amazing-thing-taylor-swift-did-for-a-fan-after-the-iheartradio-awards-is-just-taylor-being-taylor/|publisher=Seventeen|accessdate=2015-04-04|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150409120514/http://www.seventeen.com/celebrity/news/a29711/the-amazing-thing-taylor-swift-did-for-a-fan-after-the-iheartradio-awards-is-just-taylor-being-taylor/|archivedate=2015-04-09}}</ref>。她还喜欢追寻并找出在场歌迷。泰勒絲在社交媒体上有非常多的粉丝，包括[[Instagram|Instagram]]和最近的[[Tumblr|Tumblr]]<ref name="Erin">{{cite web|author1=Erin Strecker|title=Read Taylor Swift's Sweet Message to Bullied Fan|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6451041/taylor-swift-sweet-message-bullied-fan-tumblr|work=Billboard|accessdate=2015-01-30|date=2015-01-27|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150130032719/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6451041/taylor-swift-sweet-message-bullied-fan-tumblr|archivedate=2015-01-30}}</ref>——即使是出席颁奖典礼时<ref>{{cite journal|title=LURKING-AT-IHEART-WHAT-NOW|journal=Taylor’s Tumblr|date=2015-03-29|issue=N/A|url=http://taylorswift.tumblr.com/tagged/LURKING-AT-IHEART-WHAT-NOW|accessdate=2015-04-04|deadurl=yes|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150401111258/http://taylorswift.tumblr.com/tagged/LURKING-AT-IHEART-WHAT-NOW|archivedate=2015-04-01}}</ref>。

在她早年的职业生涯中，泰勒絲的{{le|标志性造型|signature look}}是吊带裙加牛仔靴<ref name="newyorker1">{{cite web |last=Widdicombe |first=Lizzie |url=http://www.newyorker.com/reporting/2011/10/10/111010fa_fact_widdicombe?currentPage=all |title=Taylor Swift Makes Primness Lucrative |work=The New Yorker |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120718214111/http://www.newyorker.com/reporting/2011/10/10/111010fa_fact_widdicombe?currentPage=all |archivedate=2012-07-18 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |author=Vernell Hackett |url=http://www.theboot.com/2009/07/29/taylor-swift-talks-daydreams-come-to-life/ |title=Taylor Swift Talks Daydreams Come to Life |work=The Boot |date=2009-07-29 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120707210104/http://www.theboot.com/2009/07/29/taylor-swift-talks-daydreams-come-to-life/ |archivedate=2012-07-07 }}</ref>。这种时尚风格仍然被众多歌迷在出席她的演唱会时模仿<ref name="newyorker1" /><ref name="vogue1">{{cite web |last=Van |first=Jonathan |url=http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#2 |title=Taylor Swift: The Single Life – Magazine |work=Vogue |date=2012-01-17 |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120615054523/http://www.vogue.com/magazine/article/taylor-swift-the-single-life/#2 |archivedate=2012-06-15 }}</ref>。在正式活动中，泰勒絲因“闪闪发光的串珠礼服”而闻名<ref name="newyorker1" />。她的自来卷发型被乐迷们复制，泰勒絲表示：“我记得我把头发拉直过，我想像其他人那样，那现在的事实是还会有人模仿我这样做么？说笑而已<ref name="vogue1" />。”2011年末，《时尚》杂志让她剪刘海来拍封面照片，现在她经常拉直头发<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.vogue.com/videos/behind-the-scenes-taylor-swift-cover-shoot/?mbid=nl_VO_VOG_Edit_SUB_Taylor_011712 |title=Behind the Scenes: Taylor Swift Cover Shoot – Video |work=Vogue |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120225183538/http://www.vogue.com/videos/behind-the-scenes-taylor-swift-cover-shoot/?mbid=nl_VO_VOG_Edit_SUB_Taylor_011712 |archivedate=2012-02-25 }}</ref>。2011年，泰勒絲被《时尚》杂志提名为“美国风格标志性人物”（{{lang|en|Icon of Amercian Style}}）<ref>{{cite web |last=Holt |first=Emily |url=http://www.vogue.com/vogue-daily/article/american-idols-icons-of-stateside-style/ |title=American Idols: Icons of Stateside Style – Vogue Daily |work=Vogue |date=2011-07-01 |accessdate=2012-06-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121016122700/http://www.vogue.com/vogue-daily/article/american-idols-icons-of-stateside-style/ |archivedate=2012-10-16 }}</ref>。

== 影响力和认可 ==
[[File:YouTube_Presents_Taylor_Swift.jpg|thumb]]专访，摄于2011年]]
泰勒絲的作品获得前辈艺人的好评。{{le|比尔·威瑟斯|Bill Withers}}表示：“她是一个聪明詞曲作家，我能体会到她的智慧，她的成功实至名归<ref>{{cite web |last=Greene |first=Andy |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/features/10-things-we-learned-spending-two-days-with-bill-withers-20150327?page=2 |title=Page 2 of 10 Things We Learned Spending Two Days With Bill Withers |publisher=Rolling Stone |date=2015-03-27 |accessdate=2015-04-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150404011426/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/features/10-things-we-learned-spending-two-days-with-bill-withers-20150327?page=2 |archivedate=2015-04-04 }}</ref>。”[[尼尔·杨|尼尔·杨]]把她形容为“一位伟大的詞曲作家”：“我喜欢泰勒絲，我喜欢听她（的歌）。我喜欢看她回应所有的攻击。我喜欢她给自己下的定义。所以我关注它<ref>{{cite web |last=Gold |first=Adam |url=http://www.nashvillescene.com/nashvillecream/archives/2011/06/16/neil-young-talks-about-a-treasure-the-international-harvesters-taylor-swift-and-more-the-cream-interview |title=Neil Young Talks About A Treasure, The International Harvesters, Taylor Swift and More |publisher=Nashvillescene.com |date=2011-06-16 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archivedate=2011-11-03 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |first=Cory |last=Stromblad |url=http://www.theboot.com/2011/06/24/neil-young-taylor-swift/ |title=Neil Young Gives Props to Taylor Swift |publisher=The Boot |date=2011-06-24 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110808064956/http://www.theboot.com/2011/06/24/neil-young-taylor-swift |archivedate=2011-08-08 }}</ref>。”{{le|斯蒂芬·斯蒂尔斯|Stephen Stills}}则为泰勒絲的忏悔式创作风格辩护：“这就是詞曲作家该做的……袒露自己的感情，然后把它写下来。去他妈的。如果我还年轻，我肯定会完全被她俘获，成为她的粉丝<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2013/01/crosby-stills-and-nash-there-and-back-again/2/ |title=Crosby, Stills and Nash: There And Back Again | Page 2 of 2 |publisher=American Songwriter |date=2013-01-02 |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130118045123/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2013/01/crosby-stills-and-nash-there-and-back-again/2/ |archivedate=2013-01-18 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.uncut.co.uk/stephen-stills-im-a-little-like-taylor-swift-news |title=Stephen Stills: "I'm a little like Taylor Swift" |work=Uncut |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131221043713/http://www.uncut.co.uk/stephen-stills-im-a-little-like-taylor-swift-news |archivedate=2013-12-21 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://social.entertainment.msn.com/music/blogs/reverb-blogpost.aspx?post=c4c0329d-a0db-46e5-b2e1-b551c2185a0f |title=Stephen Stills carries on |publisher=MSN |accessdate=2013-03-29 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130331032348/http://social.entertainment.msn.com/music/blogs/reverb-blogpost.aspx?post=c4c0329d-a0db-46e5-b2e1-b551c2185a0f |archivedate=2013-03-31 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。”

曾两次与泰勒絲合作的詹姆斯·泰勒表示：“我们一拍即合。我喜欢她的歌，她在舞台上的亮相太棒了<ref name="autogenerated3" /><ref name="post-gazette1" />。”[[埃尔维斯·科斯特洛|埃尔维斯·科斯特洛]]表示：“我觉得她挺有意思的……你可以从她身上看到一定程度的淡定，我对此很好奇<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.elviscostellofans.com/phpBB3/viewtopic.php?f=2&t=8000&p=130254#p130512 |title=Elvis Costello Fan Forum • View topic – SPECTACLE APOLLO 2 debut! |publisher=Elviscostellofans.com |accessdate=2013-12-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131231001537/http://www.elviscostellofans.com/phpBB3/viewtopic.php?f=2&t=8000&p=130254#p130512 |archivedate=2013-12-31 }}</ref>。”[[朱迪·科林斯|朱迪·科林斯]]指出泰勒絲继承了思想独立的艺术家的血统，是当今明星的模范<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.vindy.com/news/2012/dec/13/judy-collins-is-still-looking-to-the-fut/?newswatch |title=Youngstown News, Judy Collins is still looking to the futureSFlb |publisher=Vindy.com |date=2012-12-13 |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130521210500/http://www.vindy.com/news/2012/dec/13/judy-collins-is-still-looking-to-the-fut/?newswatch |archivedate=2013-05-21 }}</ref>。{{le|史蒂夫·厄尔|Steve Earle}}称赞《1989》：“是一张非常棒的專輯！她是一位真正的词曲作家<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.chicagoreader.com/chicago/steve-earle-winery-terraplane-quinn-tsan-interview/Content?oid=16275924 |title=Steve Earle on hanging out with Levon Helm, learning to love Taylor Swift, and more |work=Chicago Reader |date=2015-01-26 |accessdate=2015-07-11 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150712044154/http://www.chicagoreader.com/chicago/steve-earle-winery-terraplane-quinn-tsan-interview/Content?oid=16275924 |archivedate=2015-07-12 }}</ref>。”

至于泰勒絲，克里斯托佛森表示“她把我给征服了。让我惊讶的是，这人那么年轻竟然能写出如此伟大的歌曲。摆在她前面的是一个伟大的职业生涯<ref>{{cite news |last=Lewis |first=Randy |url=http://www.latimes.com/entertainment/news/la-ca-taylor-swift-20101024,0,5164888,full.story |title=Taylor Swift: the next chapter |newspaper=Los Angeles Times |date=2010-10-24 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121015154637/http://www.latimes.com/entertainment/news/la-ca-taylor-swift-20101024,0,5164888,full.story |archivedate=2012-10-15 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.lasvegassun.com/blogs/kats-report/2012/may/20/billboards-begin-justin-bieber----stunnigly----win/ |title=Live from Billboard Music Awards: Stevie Wonder closes with 'Superstition'; Adele wins 12 awards |newspaper=Las Vegas Sun |first=John |last=Katsilometes |date=2012-05-20 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120526091830/http://www.lasvegassun.com/blogs/kats-report/2012/may/20/billboards-begin-justin-bieber----stunnigly----win/ |archivedate=2012-05-26 }}</ref>。”珍妮斯·伊恩写道，“泰勒絲改变了音乐、歌曲创作和女孩弹吉他的面貌……他们是的确存在的<ref>{{cite web |author=Janis Ian: Echoes of Endurance and Evolution Feb 7 |url=http://musicconnection.com/janis-ian-echoes-endurance-evolution/ |title=Janis Ian: Echoes of Endurance and Evolution |publisher=Musicconnection.com |date=2013-02-07 |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130216070917/http://musicconnection.com/janis-ian-echoes-endurance-evolution/ |archivedate=2013-02-16 }}</ref>。”尼克斯认为泰勒絲写的歌“就像尼尔·戴蒙德和埃尔顿·约翰那样，让整个世界为之歌唱<ref name="nicks1" />。”她评论道，这位年轻的歌手的歌《今天是个童话》“永远地住进了我的心房，在很多方面都让我想到自己<ref>{{cite news |title=Stevie Nicks on Fleetwood Mac's Reunion Tour, Rihanna, Kanye West & Her Early Years in Music |date=2012-12-03 |work=The Huffington Post |url=http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2012/12/03/stevie-nicks-fleetwood-mac-reunion-rihanna-kanye_n_2220029.html?utm_hp_ref=entertainment?ncid=dynaldusaolp00000250 |first=Kia |last=Makarechi |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160304035557/http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2012/12/03/stevie-nicks-fleetwood-mac-reunion-rihanna-kanye_n_2220029.html?utm_hp_ref=entertainment%3Fncid%3Ddynaldusaolp00000250 |archivedate=2016-03-04 }}</ref>。”{{le|林赛·白金汉|Lindsey Buckingham}}将泰勒絲称为目前有着[[佛利伍麦克|佛利·伍麦克]]的耐力艺术家：“其他我很喜欢泰勒絲。我很佩服她所做的事<ref>{{cite web|title=Fleetwood Mac's Lindsey Buckingham Speaks at USC, Confesses 'I Like Taylor Swift'|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6553526/fleetwood-macs-lindsey-buckingham-speaks-at-usc-confesses-i-like-taylor-swift|website=Billboard|accessdate=2015-07-11|date=2015-05-01|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150705074331/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6553526/fleetwood-macs-lindsey-buckingham-speaks-at-usc-confesses-i-like-taylor-swift|archivedate=2015-07-05}}</ref>。”

[[琼·邦·乔飞|琼·邦·乔飞]]称她“在各个方面、外貌和形态上是实打实的。她是一个詞曲作家，她是一个歌手，她还是一个漂亮的女孩……就像，她什么都有<ref>{{cite news |url=http://transcripts.cnn.com/TRANSCRIPTS/1012/09/lkl.01.html |title=CNN.com – Transcripts |publisher=CNN }}</ref>。”帕顿“对她的印象非常深刻，尤其是她写的歌……真正让我印象深刻的是她的深度，她所拥有的这些特质将持续很长一段时间<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1607426/cmt-insider-interview-dolly-parton.jhtml |title=News : CMT Insider |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121113174622/http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1607426/cmt-insider-interview-dolly-parton.jhtml |archivedate=2012-11-13 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |accessdate=2012-05-29 |publisher=Contactmusic.com |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121015123612/http://www.contactmusic.com/news/parton-admires-smart-beautiful-incredible-swift_1186116 |archivedate=2012-10-15 }}</ref>。”瑟里奇评论道，“我爱她的灵魂，她的精神。我认为她能给人们带来惊喜，她的影响会持续一段时间<ref>{{cite web |url=http://melissaetheridgeradioshow.com/tag/taylor-swift/ |title=taylor swift |publisher=The Melissa Etheridge Radio Show |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131221001402/http://melissaetheridgeradioshow.com/tag/taylor-swift/ |archivedate=2013-12-21 }}</ref><ref>{{cite Window' on my album" |publisher=AfterEllen.com |date=2012-11-01 |accessdate=2013-03-29 }}</ref>。”

泰勒絲还受到同时代词曲作家的称赞。梅尔是泰勒絲职业生涯早年的支持者——两人曾录制过二重唱歌曲，曾两次在演唱会上合唱：“不管你把她放进哪一个时期的时间机器，她都会有热门的唱片<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/957722/taylor-swift-among-diverse-honorees-at-songwriters-hall |title=Taylor Swift Among Diverse Honorees at Songwriters Hall |work=Billboard |date=2010-06-18 |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130508152716/http://www.billboard.com/articles/news/957722/taylor-swift-among-diverse-honorees-at-songwriters-hall |archivedate=2013-05-08 }}</ref>。”瑞恩·亚当斯称她是“我所见过的最他妈惊人的詞曲作家之一。我曾跟她坐在房间里，听到她即兴创作歌曲，这真的让人难以置信。这是纯粹的炼金术<ref>{{cite web|author1=Rob LeDonne|title=Ryan Adams: Pure Alchemy|url=http://www.americansongwriter.com/2014/12/ryan-adams-pure-alchemy/3/|website=American Songwriter|publisher=ForASong Media, LLC|accessdate=2015-01-04|date=2014-12-04|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141226215425/http://www.americansongwriter.com/2014/12/ryan-adams-pure-alchemy/3/|archivedate=2014-12-26}}</ref>。”{{le|凯瑟琳·汉纳|Kathleen Hanna}}表示，“总的来看泰勒絲，我认为她的歌词非常的聪明，我喜欢她自己写的音乐<ref>{{cite web |last=Sykes |first=Tom |url=http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2013/03/13/punk-rock-feminist-pioneer-kathleen-hanna-on-her-sxsw-doc-more.html |title=Punk Rock-Feminist Pioneer Kathleen Hanna on Her SXSW Doc & More |work=The Daily Beast |date=2013-03-13 |accessdate=2013-03-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130328205937/http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2013/03/13/punk-rock-feminist-pioneer-kathleen-hanna-on-her-sxsw-doc-more.html |archivedate=2013-03-28 }}</ref>。”{{le|雪莉·曼森|Shirley Manson}}表示，泰勒絲“写歌非常有才华……她自己创造了成功的大门，并朝它而去。我们应该为她与体制逆流而行的勇气鼓掌。这就是艺术家应该做的<ref>{{cite web|author1=Shirley Manson |title=Shirley Manson defends Taylor Swift |archivedate=2015-01-04 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。”[[HBO|HBO]]电视连续剧《[[衰姐们|衰姐们]]》原创人兼演员[[莉娜·丹恩|莉娜·丹恩]]形容泰勒絲跟她“在艺术上志趣相投<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.kcrw.com/music/programs/gd/gd101222lena_dunham/ == 其他事业 ==

=== 代言产品 ===
