SQUARE SQ6」的拍立得相機，相機印上了與《舉世盛名》專輯封面相似的圖案及泰勒絲的親筆簽名圖案；在這期間中，也為美國電信業者[[AT&T|AT&T]]拍攝不同的3支廣告。

=== 演艺生涯 ===
[[File:TaylorSwiftApr09.jpg|thumb]]
泰勒絲的首次表演是于2009年在[[CBS_(電視網)|CBS]]电视连续剧《[[CSI犯罪现场|CSI犯罪现场]]》中扮演一位叛逆的少年<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.eonline.com/uberblog/b103119_wild_card_american_idol_holds_off.html |title=Wild Card American Idol Holds Off Taylor Swift CSI |publisher=E! |date=2009-03-06 |author=Joal Ryan |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110629154626/http://www.eonline.com/uberblog/b103119_wild_card_american_idol_holds_off.html |archivedate=2011-06-29 }}</ref>。《纽约时报》指出，该角色让泰勒絲“有点调皮，但也让人信服”<ref>{{cite news |last=Caramanica |first=Jon |url=http://artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com/2009/03/06/omg-taylor-swift-does-csi/ |title=OMG! Taylor Swift Does 'CSI'! - ''The New York Times'' |publisher=Artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com |date=2009-03-06 |accessdate=2012-05-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20110814164338/http://artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com/2009/03/06/omg-taylor-swift-does-csi/ |archivedate=2011-08-14 }}</ref>。《滚石》认为她“本色出演”，“当演员不错”，並稱她为永远的配角<ref>{{cite web |author=Daniel Kreps |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-hits-the-small-screen-as-murdered-teen-on-csi-20090306 |title=Taylor Swift Hits the Small Screen as Murdered Teen on CSI |work=Rolling Stone |date=2009-03-06 |accessdate=2012-05-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120222131405/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/news/taylor-swift-hits-the-small-screen-as-murdered-teen-on-csi-20090306 |archivedate=2012-02-22 }}</ref> 。而《[[芝加哥论坛报|芝加哥论坛报]]》认为，她“表现得很好”<ref>{{cite news |url=http://featuresblogs.chicagotribune.com/entertainment_tv/2009/03/csi-taylor-swift.html |title=Taylor Swift appears in an engrossing 'CSI' investigation – The Watcher |work=Chicago Tribune |date=2009-03-04 |accessdate=2012-05-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120331183337/http://featuresblogs.chicagotribune.com/entertainment_tv/2009/03/csi-taylor-swift.html |archivedate=2012-03-31 }}</ref>。当年晚些时候，泰勒絲主持并担任《[[周六夜现场|周六夜现场]]》的音乐嘉宾<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.nbc.com/saturday-night-live/video/clips/taylor-swift-monologue/1173589/ |title=Clips from the November 7, 2009 episode of ''Saturday Night Live'' at |publisher=Nbc.com |date=2010-12-18 |accessdate=2011-01-15 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20091110225626/http://www.nbc.com/saturday-night-live/video/clips/taylor-swift-monologue/1173589 |archivedate=2009-11-10 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。《[[娱乐周刊|娱乐周刊]]》称她为“《周六夜现场》本季迄今为止最棒的主持人”，并指出她“总是准备好迎接挑战，似乎从其中找到乐趣，还帮助其他剧组成员炮制笑料。“她证明自己”在众多小品角色拥有令人叹服的适应能力，启发更多女性，展现出自蒂娜·菲-艾米·波勒时期以来的最棒的少女感性<ref>{{cite web |last=Barrett |first=Annie |url=http://watching-tv.ew.com/2009/11/08/taylor-swift-saturday-night-live/ |title=Taylor Swift hosted the best 'Saturday Night Live' of the season so far ... really!?! |work=Entertainment Weekly |date=2009-11-08 |accessdate=2012-05-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120922232851/http://watching-tv.ew.com/2009/11/08/taylor-swift-saturday-night-live/ |archivedate=2012-09-22 }}</ref>。

泰勒絲于2010年出演了她的电影处女作《[[情人节快乐|情人节快乐]]》，饰演高中校队运动员的无厘头女友<ref>{{cite web |title=Winners of 'Teen Choice 2010' Awards Announced; Teens Cast More Than 85 Million Votes |url=http://tvbythenumbers.com/2010/08/08/winners-of-teen-choice-2010-awards-announced-teens-cast-more-than-85-million-votes/59453?utm_campaign=WP-TWITTER&utm_medium=twitter&utm_source=twitter}}</ref>。《洛杉矶时报》感受到她的表演蕴藏着“认真的喜剧功力”<ref>{{cite news |author=Betsy Sharkey |url=http://articles.latimes.com/2010/feb/12/entertainment/la-et-valentines-day12-2010feb12/2 |title=Review: 'Valentine's Day' – Page 2 – Los Angeles Times |work=Los Angeles Times |date=2010-02-12 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121011052229/http://articles.latimes.com/2010/feb/12/entertainment/la-et-valentines-day12-2010feb12/2 |archivedate=2012-10-11 }}</ref>，而《[[旧金山纪事报|旧金山纪事报]]》则认为她“非常可笑”<ref>{{cite news |author=Mick LaSalle, Chronicle Movie Critic |url=http://www.sfgate.com/movies/article/Review-Happy-Valentine-s-Day-3273334.php |title=Review: Happy 'Valentine's Day' |work=San Francisco Chronicle |date=2010-02-12 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130515111503/http://www.sfgate.com/movies/article/Review-Happy-Valentine-s-Day-3273334.php |archivedate=2013-05-15 }}</ref>。《时代》杂志表示，泰勒絲饰演的角色“相当迷人”<ref>{{cite news |last=Pols |first=Mary |url=http://www.time.com/time/arts/article/0,8599,1963839,00.html |title=Valentine's Day Review: A Soggy Love Note |work=Time |date=2010-02-12 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120708061008/http://www.time.com/time/arts/article/0,8599,1963839,00.html |archivedate=2012-07-08 }}</ref>。然而，《[[综艺_(杂志)|综艺]]》杂志认为“完全失去方向……她需要找一位在行的导演夯实她的基础，引导她那明显充沛的精力”<ref>{{cite news |last=McCarthy |first=Todd |url=http://www.variety.com/review/VE1117942089/ |title=Valentine's Day – Film Reviews |work=Variety |date=2010-02-07 |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121225112802/http://www.variety.com/review/VE1117942089/ |archivedate=2012-12-25 }}</ref>。《[[每日新闻|每日新闻]]》称她的表演“笨拙得令人难堪”，而《Slant》杂志则认为她“不具观赏性”<ref>{{cite news |author=Elizabeth Weitzman |url=http://events.nydailynews.com/reviews/show/141665-review-valentines-day |title=Review of Valentine's Day |work=Daily News |location=New York |accessdate=2012-07-30 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121025143826/http://events.nydailynews.com/reviews/show/141665-review-valentines-day |archivedate=2012-10-25 }}</ref><ref name="Slant">{{cite web |url=http://www.slantmagazine.com/house/2012/08/single-review-taylor-swift-we-are-never-ever-getting-back-together/ |title=Single Review: Taylor Swift, "We Are Never Ever Getting Back Together" |date=2012-08-15 |author=Jonathan Keefe |work=Slant Magazine |accessdate=2012-08-15 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120818042138/http://www.slantmagazine.com/house/2012/08/single-review-taylor-swift-we-are-never-ever-getting-back-together/ |archivedate=2012-08-18 }}</ref>。2012年，泰勒絲在动画电影《[[老雷斯的故事|老雷斯的故事]]》中为一棵树的爱人奥黛丽（{{lang|en|Audrey}}）配音。2013年，她在情景喜剧《[[房客小妹|房客小妹]]》中有短暂的客串演出。2014年，她在[[授者|改编电影]]《[[授者_(电影)|授者]]》中担任配角罗斯玛丽<ref>{{cite web |url=http://insidemovies.ew.com/2013/09/27/taylor-swift-the-giver-movie/ |title=Taylor Swift will co-star in long-awaited adaptation of 'The Giver' |work=Entertainment Weekly |date=2013-09-27 |author=Busis, Hillary |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140214192348/http://insidemovies.ew.com/2013/09/27/taylor-swift-the-giver-movie/ |archivedate=2014-02-14 }}</ref> 。2019年，泰勒絲演出《[[貓_(電影)|貓（電影）]]》。

=== 慈善事业 ===
泰勒絲也是一名[[慈善家|慈善家]]，她的慈善事业受到{{le|做点什么奖|Do Something Awards}}<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1669376/taylor-swifts-rehearsal-concert-wins-award.jhtml |title=Taylor Swift's Rehearsal Concert Wins Award |publisher=Country Music Television |date=2011-08-19 |accessdate=2011-11-05 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121024053612/http://www.cmt.com/news/news-in-brief/1669376/taylor-swifts-rehearsal-concert-wins-award.jhtml |archivedate=2012-10-24 }}</ref>、回馈基金（{{lang|en|The Giving Back Fund}}）<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.looktothestars.org/news/7569-giving-back-fund-announces-top-30-celebrity-charity-donations-for-2011 |title=Giving Back Fund Announces Top 30 Celebrity Charity Donations For 2011 |publisher=Looktothestars.org |accessdate=2012-08-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120818044914/http://www.looktothestars.org/news/7569-giving-back-fund-announces-top-30-celebrity-charity-donations-for-2011 |archivedate=2012-08-18 }}</ref>和田纳西州灾害服务部（{{lang|en|Tennessee Disaster Services}}）的认可<ref>{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift Receives Star of Compassion Award|url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-star-of-compassion-award/|website=Taste of Country|accessdate=2015-07-13|date=2012-06-13|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150713131701/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-star-of-compassion-award/|archivedate=2015-07-13}}</ref>。

[[File:Taylor_Swift_2012.jpg|thumbnail]][[悉尼|悉尼]]站上表演，摄于2012年]]

2012年，[[米歇爾·奧巴馬|米歇尔·奥巴马]]授予泰勒絲重大帮助奖（{{lang|en|The Big Help Award}}），以表彰她“献身于帮助他人的事业，通过行动激励其他人<ref>{{cite web |url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-kids-choice-awards-michelle-obama/ |title=Taylor Swift to Receive 'Big' Honor From Michelle Obama at Kids' Choice Awards |publisher=Tasteofcountry.com |date=2012-03-27 |accessdate=2012-08-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120330024204/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-kids-choice-awards-michelle-obama/ |archivedate=2012-03-30 }}</ref>。”当年，{{le|罗伯特·肯尼迪司法和人权中心|Robert F. Kennedy Center for Justice and Human Rights}}的[[凯莉·肯尼迪|凯莉·肯尼迪]]希望涟漪奖（{{lang|en|Ripple of Hope Award}}），以表彰她“年纪轻轻全心全意为了宣传……泰勒絲就是那种我们希望我们的女儿去学习的女人<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jGCj_NpC3__yibr26VeeBtxhAOZw?docId=CNG.79e55df3401a2cb91a3a2f8222d0f6f1.141 |title=AFP: Kennedys honor Taylor Swift with 'social change' award |publisher=Google |date=2012-07-13 |accessdate=2012-08-07 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120826211322/http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jGCj_NpC3__yibr26VeeBtxhAOZw?docId=CNG.79e55df3401a2cb91a3a2f8222d0f6f1.141 |archivedate=2012-08-26 |deadurl=yes }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/taylor-swift-honored-with-rfk-centers-ripple-of-hope-award-182081831.html |title=Taylor Swift Honored With RFK Center's Ripple of Hope Award – NASHVILLE, Tenn., Dec. 4, 2012 /PRNewswire/ |agency=PR Newswire |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130507092910/http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/taylor-swift-honored-with-rfk-centers-ripple-of-hope-award-182081831.html |archivedate=2013-05-07 }}</ref>。”

泰勒絲是艺术教育的支持者。2010年，她向母校亨德森威尔高中捐出7.5万美元，帮助学校整修礼堂的音响和灯光系统<ref>{{cite news |url=http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2010/09/23/taylor-swift-becomes-namesake-of-hendersonville-high-school-auditorium/ |title=Taylor Swift becomes namesake of Hendersonville High School auditorium |work=The Tennessean |date=2010-09-23 |agency=Associated Press |accessdate=2011-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://archive.is/20150712025238/http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2010/09/23/taylor-swift-becomes-namesake-of-hendersonville-high-school-auditorium/ |archivedate=2015-07-12 }}</ref>。2012年，她认捐400万美元，用于兴建纳什维尔的乡村音乐名人堂博物馆的全新教育中心<ref>{{cite news |last=Mckinley |first=James C. |url=http://artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com/2012/05/17/taylor-swift-donating-4-million-to-country-music-hall-of-fame-and-museum/ |title=Taylor Swift to Donate $4 Million to the Country Hall of Fame – ''The New York Times''. |location=Nashville (Tenn) |publisher=Artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com |date=2012-05-17 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120605201908/http://artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com/2012/05/17/taylor-swift-donating-4-million-to-country-music-hall-of-fame-and-museum/ |archivedate=2012-06-05 }}</ref>。这座7500平方英尺的建筑于2014年开张，方便青少年和老年人开展新项目，也用作工作室<ref>{{cite web|url=http://countrymusichalloffame.org/recent-press-releases/view/1910 |title=Superstar Taylor Swift pledges $4 million to fund new education center at the country music hall of fame and museum |date=2012-05-12 |accessdate=2012-05-12 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120523101314/http://countrymusichalloffame.org/recent-press-releases/view/1910 |archivedate=2012-05-23 |deadurl=yes }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://abclocal.go.com/kabc/story?section=news/entertainment&id=8666209 |title=Taylor Swift donates $4M for country music education |publisher=abclocal.go.com |date=2012-05-17 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120519093107/http://abclocal.go.com/kabc/story?section=news%2Fentertainment&id=8666209 |archivedate=2012-05-19 }}</ref>。中心包括三间教室和一件陈列室，还有一间屋子设有音乐可爱动物园和一间“潮湿”的教室，用来制作演唱会海报及其他艺术品<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/the-615/488365/taylor-swift-donates-4-million-to-country-hall-of-fame |title=Taylor Swift Donates $4 Million to Country Hall of Fame |last=Talbott |first=Chris |work=Billboard |date=2012-05-17 |accessdate=2012-08-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130508162904/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/the-615/488365/taylor-swift-donates-4-million-to-country-hall-of-fame |archivedate=2013-05-08 }}</ref>。博物馆工作人员将它命名为「泰勒絲教育中心」（{{lang|en|The Taylor Swift Education Center}}），歌手可作为顾问参与其中<ref>{{cite web |url=http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2012/05/17/taylor-swift-pledges-4-million-to-country-music-hall-of-fame-and-museum/ |title=Taylor Swift pledges $4 million to Country Music Hall of Fame and Museum |work=The Tennessean |date=2012-05-17 |accessdate=2012-07-01 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120521105511/http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2012/05/17/taylor-swift-pledges-4-million-to-country-music-hall-of-fame-and-museum/ |archivedate=2012-05-21 }}</ref>。同年，泰勒絲与教材租赁公司{{le|Chegg|Chegg}}共同向美国六所学校的音乐系捐出6万美元<ref>{{cite web |last=Golden |first=Zara |url=http://www.vh1.com/music/tuner/2012-10-01/taylor-swift-vh1-storytellers-harvey-mudd-college/ |title=And The Taylor Swift VH1 Storytellers Contest Winner Is ... Harvey Mudd College! – | VH1 Tuner |publisher=VH1 |date=2012-10-01 |accessdate=2014-04-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150712144643/http://www.vh1.com/music/tuner/2012-10-01/taylor-swift-vh1-storytellers-harvey-mudd-college/ |archivedate=2015-07-12 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.boston.com/names/2012/10/01/horace-mann-school-for-the-deaf-allston-gets-personal-gift-from-taylor-swift/GDs3zPxWK5XO2msI1JxirJ/story.html |title=Horace Mann School for the Deaf in Allston gets a personal gift from Taylor Swift |work=Boston Globe |accessdate=2012-10-23 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121030163951/http://www.boston.com/names/2012/10/01/horace-mann-school-for-the-deaf-allston-gets-personal-gift-from-taylor-swift/GDs3zPxWK5XO2msI1JxirJ/story.html |archivedate=2012-10-30 }}</ref>。2013年，泰勒絲捐10万美元给{{lang|en|纳什维尔交响乐团|Nashville Symphony}}<ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2013/12/16/taylor-swift-birthday-donation_n_4453904.html |title=Taylor Swift Celebrated Her Birthday By Donating $100,000 to the Nashville Symphony |work=The Huffington Post |date=2013-12-16 |accessdate=2014-04-03 |first=Hilary |last=Miller |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140220202320/http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2013/12/16/taylor-swift-birthday-donation_n_4453904.html |archivedate=2014-02-20 }}</ref>。

泰勒絲还推广儿童识字教育。2009年，她捐25万美元给全美各所她曾上过学或有过合作的学校。该款项用于购买图书、资助教育项目并帮助支付教师工资<ref>{{cite web |last=Sanz |first=Cynthia |url=http://www.people.com/people/article/0,,20326948,00.html |title=Taylor Swift Gives Big as She Turns 20 – Good Deeds, Taylor Swift |work=People |date=2009-12-14 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120617035852/http://www.people.com/people/article/0%2C%2C20326948%2C00.html |archivedate=2012-06-17 }}</ref>。2010年，她参与在全美学校转播的网上直播节目《与泰勒絲一起读书》（{{lang|en|''Read Now! with Taylor Swift''}}），响应{{le|学乐|Scholastic}}的每日阅读活动（{{lang|en|Read Every Day}}）<ref>{{cite web|url=http://oomscholasticblog.com/2010/10/read-and-rock-out-with-taylor-swift.html |title=Read (and rock out!) with Taylor Swift! |publisher=Oomscholasticblog.com |date=2010-10-27 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111014115733/http://oomscholasticblog.com/2010/10/read-and-rock-out-with-taylor-swift.html |archivedate=2011-10-14 |deadurl=yes }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/scholastic-unveils-global-literacy-campaign-read-every-day-lead-a-better-life-105169059.html |title=Scholastic Unveils Global Literacy Campaign |location=New York |agency=PR Newswire |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121025045859/http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/scholastic-unveils-global-literacy-campaign-read-every-day-lead-a-better-life-105169059.html |archivedate=2012-10-25 }}</ref>。2011年，泰勒絲向宾夕法尼亚雷丁市公共图书馆捐献6000册学乐书籍<ref>{{cite web |url=http://readingeagle.com/article.aspx?id=339089 |title=Taylor Swift donates 6,000 books to Reading Library |publisher=Readingeagle.com |date=2011-10-14 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120512192515/http://readingeagle.com/article.aspx?id=339089 |archivedate=2012-05-12 }}</ref>。2012年，她向田纳西州纳什维尔公共图书馆捐献14000册书<ref name="tasteofcountry1">{{cite web |url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swifts-donates-14000-books-nashville-public-library/ |title=Taylor Swift Donates 14,000 Books to Nashville Public Library |publisher=Tasteofcountry.com |date=2012-02-02 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120617153215/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swifts-donates-14000-books-nashville-public-library/ |archivedate=2012-06-17 }}</ref>，其中大部分书籍被流动放置，其余的送给低收入家庭儿童、幼儿园和托儿所<ref name="tasteofcountry1" />。2012年，她共同支持了{{le|美国全国教育协会|National Education Association}}的全美阅读活动（{{lang|en|Read Across America}}），并录制{{le|公共服务公告|Public service announcement}}，鼓励孩子们多读书<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.nea.org/home/50724.htm |title=Millions will join NEA's Read Across America Day celebration on March 2 |publisher=NEA |date=2012-02-08 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120530181921/http://www.nea.org/home/50724.htm |archivedate=2012-05-30 }}</ref>。同年，泰勒絲在第二个学乐网络直播节目中宣传阅读的力量，全美教室观看直播<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.scholastic.com/readeveryday/taylor-swift-live-webcast.htm |title=Taylor Swift Live Webcast | Read Every Day, Lead a Better Life |publisher=Scholastic.com |accessdate=2012-09-14 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120916002214/http://www.scholastic.com/readeveryday/taylor-swift-live-webcast.htm |archivedate=2012-09-16 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。2013年，透过{{le|儿童阅读推广计划|Reach Out and Read}}发起的倡议，她向{{le|雷丁医院|Reading Hospital|雷丁医院儿童保健中心}}的早期识字计划捐赠2000册学乐书籍<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.wfmz.com/news/news-regional-berks/Taylor-Swift-Scholastic-donate-books-to-Reading-Hospital/-/121418/18185568/-/6m2plgz/-/index.html |title=Taylor Swift, Scholastic donate books to Reading Hospital | Regional: Berks – Home |publisher=Wfmz.com |date=2013-01-18 |accessdate=2013-02-25 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130228050245/http://www.wfmz.com/news/news-regional-berks/Taylor-Swift-Scholastic-donate-books-to-Reading-Hospital/-/121418/18185568/-/6m2plgz/-/index.html |archivedate=2013-02-28 }}</ref>。2014年，她亮相[[美国图书馆协会|READ]]活动<ref>{{cite web |last=Billups |first=Andrea |url=http://www.people.com/article/taylor-swift-read-campaign-first-look-poster |title=Taylor Swift READ Campaign: Poster from American Library Association |work=People |accessdate=2014-07-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140717142609/http://www.people.com/article/taylor-swift-read-campaign-first-look-poster |archivedate=2014-07-17 }}</ref>，参与另一个学乐网络直播节目，节目在美国教室直播<ref>{{cite web |url=http://abcnews.go.com/Entertainment/wireStory/taylor-swift-talks-books-music-kids-26551165 |title=Entertainment |publisher=ABC News |accessdate=2014-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141111132554/http://abcnews.go.com/Entertainment/wireStory/taylor-swift-talks-books-music-kids-26551165 |archivedate=2014-11-11 }}</ref>；同年，她将歌曲《[[欢迎来纽约|欢迎来纽约]]》的所有收益捐给纽约市公立学校（{{lang|en|New York City Public Schools}}）<ref>{{cite web |url=http://abcnews.go.com/Entertainment/taylor-swift-donate-york-proceeds-nyc-public-schools/story?id=26545696 |title=Taylor Swift to Donate 'Welcome to New York' Proceeds to NYC Public Schools |publisher=ABC News |accessdate=2014-11-20 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141119091236/http://abcnews.go.com/Entertainment/taylor-swift-donate-york-proceeds-nyc-public-schools/story?id=26545696 |archivedate=2014-11-19 }}</ref>，也在2015年捐贈25000本書籍給紐約市的學校。2016年，她去澳洲探望兒童醫院；並在同年捐助V基金會10萬美元。2017年，她慷慨捐款「Joyful Heart基金會」。2018年，她邀請了2000個寄養/收養家庭免費現場觀看[[舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會|舉世盛名體育場巡迴演唱會]]的彩排演出，並把簽名及合照讓他們做紀念。2019年4月，她捐贈「田納西州平等計畫」11.3萬美元，成為該組織最高金額的捐贈。

纵观她的职业生涯，泰勒絲曾捐献资金帮助自然灾害的受害者。2008年，她将在乡村音乐节上销售的产品的收益捐给红十字会赈灾基金<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.looktothestars.org/news/863-taylor-swift-gives-her-vote-to-charity |title=Taylor Swift Gives Her Vote To Charity |date=2009-06-04 |publisher=Look to the Stars |accessdate=2009-03-27 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090207101536/http://www.looktothestars.org/news/863-taylor-swift-gives-her-vote-to-charity |archivedate=2009-02-07 }}</ref>。当年晚些时候，她向红十字会捐出10万美元，帮助{{le|2008年爱荷华州洪灾|Iowa flood of 2008}}的灾民<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.people.com/people/article/0,,20218079,00.html |title=Taylor Swift donates $100,000 to victims of Iowa Flood |date=2009-08-09 |work=People |accessdate=2009-09-09 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090607053519/http://www.people.com/people/article/0%2C%2C20218079%2C00.html |archivedate=2009-06-07 }}</ref>。2009年，泰勒絲参加悉尼的{{le|声音救济|Sound Relief}}演唱会，帮助[[2009年维多利亚森林大火|维多利亚森林大火]]的救灾行动<ref>{{cite news |last=Writer |first=Entertainment |url=http://www.dailytelegraph.com.au/kylie-leads-mega-star-mercy-mission/story-fna7dq6e-1111119064914 |title=Kylie to play at Sound Relief with Coldplay, Midnight Oil |work=The Daily Telegraph (Australia) |date=2009-03-08 |accessdate=2009-12-30}}</ref>，据报道她给澳大利亚[[红十字会|红十字会]]作出的贡献比任何艺术家都要多<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.tunebinder.com.au/2009/03/14/new-taylor-swift-love-story-live-at-sound-relief-sydney/ |title=New Taylor Swift |date=2009-03-14 |publisher=Tune Binder |accessdate=2009-03-15 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090606150614/http://www.tunebinder.com.au/2009/03/14/new-taylor-swift-love-story-live-at-sound-relief-sydney/ |archivedate=2009-06-06 |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。2010年，她参加{{le|海地的希望|Hope for Haiti}}募捐活动，在活动中表演并回复那些希望捐款的观众的电话<ref>{{cite web |author=Gayle Thompson |url=http://www.theboot.com/2010/01/21/taylor-swift-haiti-benefit/ |title=Taylor Swift 'Passionate' About Helping People of Haiti – The Boot |publisher=Theboot.com |date=2010-01-21 |accessdate=2012-08-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20100831145930/http://www.theboot.com/2010/01/21/taylor-swift-haiti-benefit |archivedate=2010-08-31 }}</ref>。她还为《{{le|海地的希望|Hope for Haiti Now (album)}}》专辑录制歌曲<ref>{{cite web |last=Vena |first=Jocelyn |url=http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1630485/better-than-ezra-honored-by-taylor-swifts-breathless-performance.jhtml |title=Better Than Ezra }}</ref>。为响应{{le|2010年田纳西州洪灾|2010 Tennessee floods|2010年5月美国田纳西州洪灾}}的救灾行动，泰勒絲向{{le|WSMV|WSMV}}电视台举办的募捐活动捐赠50万美元<ref name="Talbottflood">{{cite news |url=http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/news/taylor-swift-donates-500k-to-nashville-flood-victoms-201075 |title=Taylor Swift Donates $500K to Nashville Flood Victims |date=2010-05-07 |work=Us Weekly |accessdate=2010-05-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120410202422/http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/news/taylor-swift-donates-500k-to-nashville-flood-victoms-201075 |archivedate=2012-04-10 }}</ref>。当年晚些时候，她捐出10万美元协助重建田纳西州亨德森威尔因洪水损坏的游乐场<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.theboot.com/2010/08/27/taylor-swift-hendersonville-playground-donation/ |title=Taylor Swift Gives $100,000 to Help }}</ref>。2011年，泰勒絲将[[愛的告白世界巡迴演唱會|爱的告白世界巡回演唱会]]北美站的最终彩排，改为用于帮助{{le|2010年4月美国龙卷风袭击|April 25–28, 2011 tornado outbreak|美国近期龙卷风}}受害者的慈善音乐会，筹集了超过75万美元<ref>{{cite news |last=Lewis |first=Randy |title=Taylor |url=http://www.al.com/sports/index.ssf/2011/07/taylor_swift_alabama_tornado_donation.html |newspaper=Alabama Local News |date=2011-07-21 |accessdate=2012-05-24 |first1=Izzy |last1=Gould |first2=Tuscaloosa |last2=Bureau |location=Alabama |title=Taylor Swift donates $250,000 to Nick's Kids for Alabama tornado relief |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120617214440/http://www.al.com/sports/index.ssf/2011/07/taylor_swift_alabama_tornado_donation.html |archivedate=2012-06-17 }}</ref>。2012年，泰勒絲支持{{le|人道建筑|Architecture for Humanity}}的重建海岸（{{lang|en|Restore the Shore}}）MTV募捐活动，为[[飓风桑迪|飓风桑迪]]善后<ref>{{cite web |url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-hurricane-sandy-restore-the-shore/ |title=Taylor Swift Sends 'Love and Support' to Hurricane Sandy Victims, Asks Fans to Help 'Restore the Shore' |publisher=Tasteofcountry.com |date=2012-11-13 |accessdate=2014-04-21 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140711183241/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-hurricane-sandy-restore-the-shore/ |archivedate=2014-07-11 }}</ref>。2016年，她捐助5萬美元給美國[[伊利诺伊州|伊利諾州]]的天主教學校Ascension School，資助他們水災校園重建。2017年，她捐助修[[休斯敦|休士頓]]食物銀行，以此幫助休士頓受哈維颶風影響的災害重建工作。

泰勒絲反对歧视[[LGBT|LGBT]]。2008年{{le|拉里·金谋杀案|Murder of Larry King}}过后，她录制了一段{{le|男女同性恋和异性恋教育网络|Gay, Lesbian and Straight Education Network}}公共服务公告，与仇恨犯罪搏斗<ref name="eonline1">{{cite web |url=http://uk.eonline.com/news/59855/portia-joins-ellen-to-stop-the-hate |title=Portia Joins Ellen To Stop The Hate|publisher=E! |date=2010-03-10 |accessdate=2012-07-12}}</ref>。在金逝世周年纪念日，泰勒絲告诉《[[17_(杂志)|十七岁]]》杂志，她的父母教她“永远不要用他们所爱的人、他们的肤色或他们的信仰来判断别人<ref>{{cite web |last=Koday |first=Dan |url=http://www.seventeen.com/college/advice/mission-taylor-swift |title=Taylor Swift's Mission: Take a Stand Against Hate! – Seventeen |publisher=Seventeen.com |accessdate=2012-08-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140129013422/http://www.seventeen.com/college/advice/mission-taylor-swift |archivedate=2014-01-29 }}</ref>。”2011年，泰勒絲的反霸凌歌曲《[[太刻薄|太刻薄]]》的音乐录影带出现了高中的歧视同性恋问题。该录影带后来被提名为MTV音乐录影带大奖社会活动奖<ref name="Hawgood 2010-11-05">{{cite news |url=http://www.nytimes.com/2010/11/07/fashion/07ANTHEM.html |title=For Gays, New Songs of Survival |last=Hawgood |first=Alex |work=The New York Times |date=2010-11-05 |accessdate=2012-08-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120609020459/http://www.nytimes.com/2010/11/07/fashion/07ANTHEM.html |archivedate=2012-06-09 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.queerty.com/is-taylor-swifts-new-anti-bullying-video-simply-gay-washing-for-pink-dollars-20110519/ |title=Is Taylor Swift's New Anti-Bullying Video Simply "Gay-washing" For Pink Dollars? / Queerty |publisher=Queerty.com |accessdate=2012-08-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20111210195035/http://www.queerty.com/is-taylor-swifts-new-anti-bullying-video-simply-gay-washing-for-pink-dollars-20110519/ |archivedate=2011-12-10 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/08/04/idINIndia-58624620110804 |title=MTV adds social activism category to VMAs |agency=Reuters |date=2011-08-04 |accessdate=2012-08-30 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20121012205523/http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/08/04/idINIndia-58624620110804 |archivedate=2012-10-12 }}</ref>。《纽约时报》认为她涌入“年轻女性（多数为异性恋）为一代同性恋乐迷提供配乐的浪潮，让他们在当前动荡和混乱的文化信息中找回自己<ref name="Hawgood 2010-11-05" />。”2018年3月12日，泰勒絲的單曲《[[不堪一击_(泰勒·斯威夫特歌曲)|不堪一擊]]》音樂錄影帶中更請來了[[㚻片|㚻片]]公司Randy Blue的前知名[[㚻片演員|㚻片演員]]Kevin Falk出演一名帥氣的黑衣保鑣，引起媒體爭相報導。據報導稱，這並不是泰勒絲第一次邀請同志色情行業的演員出演自己的音樂錄影帶。早在2012年，men.com公司旗下的㚻片演員Mike de Marko就在《[[我们再也回不去了|我們再也回不去了]]》中出演過一名派對愛好者<ref>[https://www.billboard.com/articles/news/pride/8242779/taylor-swift-delicate-video-actor-kevin-falk Taylor Swift Features Gay Porn Performer Kevin Falk in New 'Delicate' Video] billboard 2018年03月17日</ref>。

泰勒絲还参与了一些慈善机构为患儿提供服务的活动。2008年，她向维多利亚路口冈营（{{lang|en|Victory Junction Gang Camp}}）捐献一辆粉红色的雪佛兰皮卡<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.looktothestars.org/news/500-musicians-start-the-year-with-generosity |title=Musicians Start The Year With Generosity |publisher=Looktothestars.org |date=2008-01-10 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |first=Tim |last=Saunders |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120620161332/http://www.looktothestars.org/news/500-musicians-start-the-year-with-generosity |archivedate=2012-06-20 }}</ref>。2011年，身为乡村音乐学院年度艺人，泰勒絲向田纳西州{{le|圣席德儿童研究医院|St. Jude Children's Research Hospital}}捐献25000万美元。这一数字跟学院配对过<ref>{{cite web |url=http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2011/06/13/taylor-swift-and-acm-lifting-lives-present-50000-to-st-jude/ |title=Taylor Swift and ACM Lifting Lives present $50,000 donation to St. Jude |work=The Tennessean |date=2011-06-13 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |author=Tennessean Music Team |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://archive.is/20150712053711/http://blogs.tennessean.com/tunein/2011/06/13/taylor-swift-and-acm-lifting-lives-present-50000-to-st-jude/ |archivedate=2015-07-12 }}</ref>。2012年，泰勒絲参与[[对抗癌症|对抗癌症]]募捐活动，表演歌曲《[[罗南|罗南]]》。这首歌是她用来纪念一位死于神经母细胞瘤的四岁男孩的。这首歌可在数字渠道下载，所获得的全部收益捐赠给与癌症相关的慈善<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.rollingstone.com/music/videos/taylor-swift-debuts-ronan-at-stand-up-to-cancer-benefit-20120908 |title=New and Hot Video: Taylor Swift Debuts 'Ronan' at Stand Up To Cancer Benefit |work=Rolling Stone |date=2012-09-08 |accessdate=2012-09-14 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20120913054843/http://www.rollingstone.com/music/videos/taylor-swift-debuts-ronan-at-stand-up-to-cancer-benefit-20120908 |archivedate=2012-09-13 }}</ref>。2014年，她向{{le|V癌症研究基金会|V Foundation for Cancer Research}}和[[费城儿童医院|费城儿童医院]]分别捐出10万美元<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.tampabay.com/sports/basketball/college/dick-vitale-holds-annual-fundraiser-for-pediatric-cancer/2180291 |title=Dick Vitale holds annual fundraiser for pediatric cancer |work=Tampa Bay }}</ref>和5万美元<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.bizjournals.com/philadelphia/blog/health-care/2014/06/taylor-swift-donates-50k-to-chop-to-help-teens.html |title=Taylor Swift donates $50K to CHOP to help teens with cancer |work=The Business Journals |accessdate=2014-07-05 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150712164028/http://www.bizjournals.com/philadelphia/blog/health-care/2014/06/taylor-swift-donates-50k-to-chop-to-help-teens.html |archivedate=2015-07-12 }}</ref>。泰勒絲还透过[[愿望成真基金|愿望成真基金]]会见了许多患病的乐迷<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.makeawishna.ca/wishes/alexis-wish |title=Make-A-Wish Northern Alberta – alexis' wish |publisher=Makeawishna.ca 泰勒絲鼓励年轻在{{le|全球青年服务日|Global Youth Service Day}}当日参加当地社区的志愿者活动<ref name="Hardiman 2007-04-07">{{cite web |author=Tim Hardiman |url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1557662/taylor-swift-encourages-teen-volunteers.jhtml |title=Taylor Swift Encourages Teen Volunteers |publisher=CMT |date=2007-04-20 |accessdate=2012-07-01 }}</ref>。2007年，她与田纳西州警察局长协会（{{lang|en|Tennessee Association of Chiefs of Police}}）联合发起一场保护儿童免受网络侵犯的运动<ref name=swift>{{cite |deadurl=yes }}</ref>。当年，她支持{{le|好事达保险|AllState}}）的青少年安全驾驶推广活动<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.allstatenewsroom.com/channels/news-releases-teen-driving/releases/Country-Music-Star-Taylor-Swift-Rewards-Top-Holiday-Carolers-at-Smart-Driving-Competition |title=Country Music Star |archivedate=2012-11-22 }}</ref>。2009年，泰勒絲录制音频公共服务公告，使听众“[[聋|有鉴别能力地]]”意识到听觉的重要性<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.soundmatters.org/taylorswift.php |title=Sound Matters: Celebrity Profile-Taylor Swift Milk?}}”活动<ref>{{cite web |title=Join Taylor Swift As A Got Milk Model |url=http://www.looktothestars.org/news/4685-join-taylor-swift-as-a-got-milk-model |publisher=Looktothestars.org |date=2010-07-02 |accessdate=2012-05-29 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20130430200353/http://www.looktothestars.org/news/4685-join-taylor-swift-as-a-got-milk-model |archivedate=2013-04-30 }}</ref>。泰勒絲还向众多慈善机构捐赠大量拍卖物品，包括{{le|埃尔顿·约翰艾滋病基金会|Elton John AIDS Foundation}}<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.sys-con.com/node/1732440 |title=19th Annual Elton John AIDS Foundation Academy Awards == 奖项和成就 ==
:主条目：{{le|泰勒·斯威夫特获奖及提名奖项列表|List of awards and nominations received by Taylor Swift}}

泰勒絲曾获得过许多奖项和荣誉，包括10项[[葛莱美奖|葛莱美奖]]<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.people.com/people/mobile/article/0,,20336343,00.html|title=Grammy Awards 2010 Winners & Nominees|work=People|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141029184510/http://www.people.com/people/mobile/article/0,,20336343,00.html|archivedate=2014-10-29}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://m.hollywoodreporter.com/news/grammy-awards-2012-winners-whitney-houston-death-adele-289778|title=Grammy Awards 2012: Complete Winners And Nominees List|work=The Hollywood Reporter|accessdate=2015-02-02}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.forbes.com/sites/zackomalleygreenburg/2013/02/11/grammy-winners-2013-the-full-list/|title=Grammy Winners 2013: The Full List|author=Zack O'Malley Greenburg|date=2013-02-11|work=Forbes|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141029191303/http://www.forbes.com/sites/zackomalleygreenburg/2013/02/11/grammy-winners-2013-the-full-list/|archivedate=2014-10-29}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.latimes.com/entertainment/envelope/music/la-et-ms-grammy-nominations-winners-list-story.html#page=1|title=Grammys 2014: The complete list of nominees and winners|date=2014-01-26|work=Los Angeles Times|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150211004747/http://www.latimes.com/entertainment/envelope/music/la-et-ms-grammy-nominations-winners-list-story.html#page=1|archivedate=2015-02-11}}</ref>,
並成為史上第一位獲得兩次葛萊美最高獎項《年度專輯》的女歌手<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.independent.co.uk/arts-entertainment/music/news/grammys-2016-winners-awards-taylor-swift-kenrick-lamar-becomes-first-woman-to-win-album-of-the-year-a6876451.html|title=Grammys 2016: Taylor Swift becomes first woman to win album of the year twice|date=2016-02-16|accessdate=2016-07-22|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160819170901/http://www.independent.co.uk/arts-entertainment/music/news/grammys-2016-winners-awards-taylor-swift-kenrick-lamar-becomes-first-woman-to-win-album-of-the-year-a6876451.html|archivedate=2016-08-19}}</ref>、23项[[全美音樂獎|全美音乐奖]]<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.latimes.com/env-ama-nom9oct09-htmlstory.html |title=2007 American Music Awards Nominees and Winners |work=Los Angeles Times |accessdate=2015-02-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141011071539/http://www.latimes.com/env-ama-nom9oct09-htmlstory.html |archivedate=2014-10-11 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |author=Entertainment |url=http://www.buzzsugar.com/List-Winners-2008-American-Music-Awards-2533136 |title=List of Winners at the 2008 American Music Awards | POPSUGAR Entertainment |publisher=Buzzsugar.com |accessdate=2015-02-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140812214625/http://www.buzzsugar.com/List-Winners-2008-American-Music-Awards-2533136 |archivedate=2014-08-12 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web|last=Esmailian|first=Asi|url=http://www.hollyscoop.com/taylor-swift/2009-american-music-award-winners-list.html|title=2009 American Music Award Winners List|publisher=Hollyscoop|date=2009-11-23|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=yes|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150203041852/http://www.hollyscoop.com/taylor-swift/2009-american-music-award-winners-list.html|archivedate=2015-02-03}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|last=Rovenstine|first=Dalene|url=http://music-mix.ew.com/2010/11/21/american-music-awards-see-list-of-winners-here/|title=American Music Awards|publisher=Music-mix.ew.com|date=2010-11-21|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141226174645/http://music-mix.ew.com/2010/11/21/american-music-awards-see-list-of-winners-here/|archivedate=2014-12-26}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://abc7.com/archive/8439273/ |title=American Music Awards 2011: Full list of winners |publisher=ABC |accessdate=2015-02-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150203035657/http://abc7.com/archive/8439273/ |archivedate=2015-02-03 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.mtv.com/news/1697612/2012-amas-winners-list/ |title=American Music Awards 2012: Complete Winners List |publisher=MTV |date=2012-11-18 |accessdate=2015-02-02 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150103100915/http://www.mtv.com/news/1697612/2012-amas-winners-list/ |archivedate=2015-01-03 }}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://abc.go.com/shows/american-music-awards/winners |title=American Music Awards 2014 Winners – AMAs The Complete List |publisher=ABC |accessdate=2015-02-02 |deadurl=yes |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20091125131215/http://abc.go.com/shows/american-music-awards/winners |archivedate=2009-11-25 }}</ref>、11项[[鄉村音樂協會獎|乡村音乐协会奖]]、8项{{le|乡村音乐学院奖|Academy of Country Music Awards}}<ref>{{cite web|title=Taylor Swift Nashville Tickets|url=http://www.excite.com/events/concert-tickets/Taylor-Swift/Taylor-Swift-Nashville-TN/index.php|work=Excite|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150203042220/http://www.excite.com/events/concert-tickets/Taylor-Swift/Taylor-Swift-Nashville-TN/index.php|archivedate=2015-02-03}}</ref>、23项[[公告牌音乐奖|公告牌音乐奖]]<ref>{{cite news|author1=Stephanie Marcus|title=Billboard Music Awards 2015 Winners List: Taylor Swift Cleans Up|url=http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2015/05/17/billboard-music-awards-2015-winners-list_n_7268128.html|accessdate=2015-07-11|agency=The Huffington Post|date=2015-05-17|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150712220816/http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2015/05/17/billboard-music-awards-2015-winners-list_n_7268128.html|archivedate=2015-07-12}}</ref>、1项[[全英音乐奖|全英音乐奖]]<ref>{{cite news|author1=Tim Jonze|title=Taylor Swift wins best international female solo artist at Brit awards 2015|url=http://www.theguardian.com/music/2015/feb/25/taylor-swift-wins-international-female-solo-artist-at-brit-awards-2015|accessdate=2015-02-28|work=The Guardian|date=2015-02-25|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150402151203/http://www.theguardian.com/music/2015/feb/25/taylor-swift-wins-international-female-solo-artist-at-brit-awards-2015|archivedate=2015-04-02}}</ref>和1项[[艾美奖|艾美奖]]<ref>{{cite news|author1=Tim Jonze|title=Taylor Swift wins best international female solo artist at Brit awards 2015|url=http://www.theguardian.com/music/2015/feb/25/taylor-swift-wins-international-female-solo-artist-at-brit-awards-2015|accessdate=2015-02-28|work=The Guardian|date=2015-02-25|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150402151203/http://www.theguardian.com/music/2015/feb/25/taylor-swift-wins-international-female-solo-artist-at-brit-awards-2015|archivedate=2015-04-02}}</ref>。凭借25项大奖，泰勒絲成为[[青少年选择奖|青少年选择奖]]获奖最多的艺人。身为词曲作家，她还受到纳什维尔词曲作家协会<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.nashvillesongwriters.com/news.php?viewStory=42/ |title=NSAI Songwriter/Artists of the Year Winners List |work=NSAI |accessdate=2015-02-02 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20090213211226/http://www.nashvillesongwriters.com/news.php?viewStory=42%2F |archivedate=2009-02-13 |deadurl=yes }}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0,,GAC_26063_5723533,00.html |title=Taylor Swift Youngest Winner of Songwriter/Artist Award |date=2007-10-16 |work=GAC |accessdate=2015-02-02 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20071018033827/http://www.gactv.com/gac/nw_headlines/article/0%2C%2CGAC_26063_5723533%2C00.html |archivedate=2007-10-18 |deadurl=yes }}</ref><ref>{{cite web|date=2010-10-18|author=Craig Shelburne|url=http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1650268/taylor-swift-named-nsais-songwriter-artist-of-the-year.jhtml|title=Taylor Swift Named NSAI's Songwriter-Artist of the Year|work=CMT|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20140314015434/http://www.cmt.com/news/country-music/1650268/taylor-swift-named-nsais-songwriter-artist-of-the-year.jhtml|archivedate=2014-03-14}}</ref>和词曲作家名人堂<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.songwritershalloffame.org/ceremony/entry/C6029/207943|title=Songwriters Hall of Fame|website=Songwriter s'hall of fame|accessdate=2015-02-02|deadurl=yes|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141129025255/http://www.songwritershalloffame.org/ceremony/entry/C6029/207943|archivedate=2014年11月29日|df=}}</ref>的表彰。

截至2016年年初，泰勒絲已售出超过4000万张专辑，单曲下载1.3亿次，是全球数字销量前五名的音乐家之一<ref name="best selling artist 2014 IFPI"/>。泰勒絲的每一张录音棚专辑都在美国至少卖出400万张，《泰勒絲》卖出500萬张，《无惧的爱》卖出708万张，《爱的告白》卖出450万张，《红》卖出425万张，《1989》卖出600万张<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6612586/taylor-swift-1989-apple-music-streaming-decision |title=Taylor Swift: 'I've Decided To Put '1989' on Apple Music' |last=Lipshutz |first=Jason |work=Billboard (magazine) |date=2015-06-25 |accessdate=2015-06-25 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20150627161419/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6612586/taylor-swift-1989-apple-music-streaming-decision |archivedate=2015-06-27 }}</ref>。
